EPILOGUE: GOD AS
THE UNIVERSE FROM
NOTHING

“IS THERE IS A GOD?” IS A USELESS QUESTION

-What we see is what we get-

There is no value to be gained considering whether there is a God or not. God is mostly
a product of human cognition that relates to our search for meaning and purpose in life.
It is a product of human identity projecting itself into the creation of the world and our
future, through stories, that makes us more prosperous as a species and able to invest
in and make great sacrifices for future things we will never see or experience personally.
People literally give their lives for imagined futures, based solely on faith. Men die for
grandchildren that aren’t even born yet. The future we believe in and see is our own
personal God. Every person has their own vision and idea of the future for themselves
and the world, and these differing visions have discernable differences in the kind of
world they make. There is no pre-existing future, and no predicting the future. We

create the future from our imaginations connecting into reality. We need both
imagination and a sense of reality, to see the world, because we invent new realities to
live with concrete real and new inventions. Imagination can create reality from nothing,
that is as real as anything. God can be contained in that very imagination that gives
birth to reality from nothingness in our real lives, every day.

“Can God exist in the future?” is a far more interesting question than if there is a god or
not, and puts on us, as individuals, a greater moral duty and purpose to our lives. We
are animals that see the future, and create it from our dreams and imaginations. We
embody reality into our beings, and embody our beings into reality and change it. Our
selves, minds and beings must ultimately be consistent with reality and what is actually
possible and not possible. Our minds evolved into them the very nature of reality,
because reality created us to be consistent with it. Only real things can survive through
time. God can emerge as the clearest expression of this reality that creates the future
from nothing, that we see and experience in each and every moment of our existence.

There are real consequences to the choices we make as people. The things we make
from nothing, can destroy the future or make it better, and knowing the difference is
never easy. The study of how to determine the goodness and righteousness of each
person’s views is called “ethics”. We need ethics that create a moral order that works
through time, and creates new things of fundamental value for humanity. People that
operate with ethics that actually create a better future for humanity, are more aligned
with “goodness” and a more “real” God. If the God you believe in actually contains the
values, vision and ideas that create the future, then your God is more real and not based
solely in one’s idealism and fantasies. The more we create a better world and a better
future, the more a real God emerges and comes into being through our choices as
individual and free human beings.

No one can control the true God you believe in at the fundamental root of your thoughts.
We can only control how others act out their vision, and make them act out the vision of
God others have as their own. The soul of a person is their own unique inner story, that
can’t be controlled by others. A Victim is fundamentally a person that denies that they
have a soul capable of making choices. Their root identity, the story of how they make
choices, becomes defined by a horrible thing that happened to them, and justifies their
inability to make good decision. Their thoughts descend into inconsistent madness, as
they deny their own existence and seek to destroy all those with souls and a desire to
live for a better world. The ethics of the future and the concept of God is for there to be
more real futures, born out of the unique identity of each individual human being. There
being more human life creating more meaning and purpose is one of the very values we
must judge all systems of belief on to know which is better. A system that judges the
quality of the future, must itself replicate and create the future, so that there are more
and more futures.

If one wants to find the single best way, out of all the ideas contained in humanity, then
creating quadrillions of human beings, filling the universe, living deeply life affirming
lives, seems the most moral way to go. A celebration of human life and all its beauty and
glory stands in defiance against those that would seek to destroy it. Too often false gods
wear the words and images of the just to hide their own disgust and disdain at humanity
and fundamentally themselves. Among those free people living on a massive scale of
life, a singular mind could arise that sees the “truth” and has the best vision to lead all
humanity forward towards the unknowable future. There are always people with better
visions and ideas, than others. There is always someone embodying the essential truth
more. In that space of near infinite seeming worlds, the chances of a human incarnate
God emerging are vastly larger. In this book, I lay out the practical means to step by

step build a galactic empire, that will consume all matter in this galaxy for its dominion,
as one of the ultimate purposes and meanings to life.

THE REALITY OF CONSISTENCY

-Math is a language of love born from human dreams-

Everything in reality can be described in math, because they must be consistent in order
to exist. The universe is not ruled by math, it is described by math, which emerges from
the fundamental processes that create reality, where impossible things don’t exist. Our
morality can be described in mathematics. Our culture, social norms, and cognitive
functions emerge from conflict and struggle, and ones that don’t work are eliminated.
Within the present, in the very moments we live, there is infinite possibility in what we
can think and feel, and only very few things that can survive in reality through time. The
part of us that isn’t defined by math, is the part of us connected to what math emerges
from, where probability and uncertainty rule. Math in human life emerges from survival
and rage, which leads to competition and the pursuit of power, which leads to order and
hierarchy, which leads to reason, which leads to the need for precise discourse, which
leads to math, which leads to imposing that math and reason on reality into things that
actually work, and which in turn create functional scientific theories and functional
technology. Numbers are fantasy ideas, that work well, and are most used by those that
like winning.

We, as humans, can actively create reality because we can be semi-independent of it.
This is consciousness. This is sentience. In a way, our very personal innate morality is an
attachment to this very freedom of being unbound from death and reality, and able to

live in fantasies. We can imagine any reality as real, and explore in our own lives and
minds. At the very root of living is a very fear of losing that freedom to be anything, and
be bound in mathematically confined reality. We forge and create structure around us
into the world with ideas unbound from reality itself. We can create art, music, culture,
dance, useless things that make us smile, and love useless people because they make us
laugh. We can test out new forms, new identities, and ways of living, with no sense of
consequence. Some ideas work out, most fail, and we move on. We are both a thing
created from reality, and a creator of reality. Those things that really work, can become
something truly special that lives on through ages, and adds to the lives of all people
because we dream and try new things based on whimsy. Most of our dreams lead to
nothing, are worthless, and are the only freedom that truly gives divinity and meaning to
human life. Great technology develops on top of itself into better and better forms, from
all the failed fantasies of humans.

Functional reality based structures must be consistent with reality. Functional morality
based in existence must evolve through time, and at its root have a logical consistency.
The logic of cultural values, that we can discern through reason, can be long gone, lost
in time, and ultimately unknowable. The deeper purposes of cultural institutions are
more complex than any human can ever imagine, because we have no knowledge of the
context they formed in. Culture is intertwined into every gene in our bodies, living thing
in our existence, and physical structure we live in. Humans defeated monsters beyond
our imaginations in the distant past of human existence long before civilization ever
evolved. Every single possible configuration of human nature played itself out in the prehistory of mankind. Cultural institutions that created history and civilization arose from
things that pre-existed those institutions, and leave no memory. We are the ones that
lived. Humanity had to be brutally domesticated into a creature that could form into
stable societies of people. We are both the hero that defeated the monster, and the
biggest monster that defeated all the other monsters.

Economics, math, science, are highly abstract realities that transform human magical
conceptions into the mathematical reality of living and existence. These ways of thinking
were born out of dominion over others and the monsters within us. Reason and logic can
exist in absolute confrontation with our sense of being, and in of itself be the very
monster that creates humanity. We don’t like being imprinted with these “inhuman”
things, and find it hard to connect our humanity and sense of self into them, to create a
greater purpose. Those that can are rare, and we pay them a lot to do that, because
they can be doing really useful stuff. They are the ones that create the world that
actually works. The more rational and logical a person is, the more we trust with the
power to form reality and the future. The more rational and logical then the more likely
their ideas will actually be consistent with reality and lead to more stable real futures.
There are powers greater than reason and logic. Humanity exists in everything we ever
created, and to make more of these great things, we need to put more humanity in
them. We must reclaim reason from those that would use its power to forge us into the
image of their dark fantasies.

GOD AS SENTIENCE

My work is a cognitive programing language that I want to empower people to use to
improve their lives and the world. It is a library of tools and examples that a person can
use create real and useful things into the future of humanity. The root rules of reality are
based in what is possible and not possible. The future is not determined. What is
possible is determined by the natural constraints of what actually works, adds onto the
systems before, and evolves into the future. The purpose of this freedom is not to be
anything we imagine or desire to be. This freedom exists to evolve us into the systems
that best work and amplify human existence. We can control things towards more

immediate results, rather than just waiting for something to change by accident. More
people working on the big problems of life, leads to more likelihoods of something
unique, new and functional coming into existence. The understanding of how things
emerge from random nothingness lies at the root of strength. The one tool to rule over
all other tools, is the understanding of nothingness. There are minimal systems that
emerge from nothingness randomly, that can evolve, and create ever increasing special
orderings of reality that work and grow themselves.

“God” is an emergent property of the future. Only a sentient being attempting to create
a better future can conceive of and experience God. Fools will believe themselves to be
God, because they conceive notions of how to align their life to reality and do amazing
real things that others cannot. The reality is that many people dream the same dreams,
and a few people among those go out and actually do something first. They cannot see
others dreams, because they are lost in their own, and thus think themselves alone and
a God unto themselves. Our notion of the divine emerges in us from an experience of
reality bound in evolution, and thus that is the only God we can know, and not one
unbound from that. The infinite possibilities are more one’s own delusions and ego, the
literal definition of delusion is believing in possibilities outside of reality.

God is the future that we are creating that is actually better than the one we lived in.
Applying this concept farther forward in time, creates the greater “mystical” notions of
absolute divinity, we feel. God is not bound in the reality of the present, nor is
transcendent from reality itself. “All things that are possible”, and “things that can
evolve into possible things from minimal-distance step-by-step evolution” are severe
constraints on reality. God exists in the concrete reality of the universe where any
metaphysical notions are based in distant time frames, and the sheer size of the true
universe.

The literal God as one would understand in a biblical sense, and not just abstract laws of
physics, is contained in nothingness. This configuration of nothingness, that our universe
comes from, by its very nature, will always end in an absolute God like being of near
supreme sentience, in some universe. All universes that evolve will end at that result,
and all universes that exist evolve. Nothingness contains possibility and transformations.
There is no such thing as absolute nothingness, because if there were, then nothing
would ever come to exist. There is an inherent set of minimal properties in nothingness,
that allows reality to emerge from it and grow, rather than collapse eternally. The very
minimal amount anything can be, which we call “nothing”, is the “space” where all
“metaphysical” properties reside, and the very origins of God.

We are a self-ordering machine. We can live and survive without that much thought. We
just align ourselves to a certain state, and we will self-actualize and adjust
automatically. Being free to change only emerges when things break, when systems and
our reality collapse. When your model and your system is a failure, then you will need to
make a new one. The human mind resists making new paradigms and seeks to selforder. Only living in perpetual trauma can drive a mind to grow and be more. There is a
certain process in the universe where only things that can survive, survive. We are made
from reality, and have to be consistent to reality. We have minds that can think and be
sentient, therefore there is deep underlying and highly “consistent” system that runs all
of that. if it is inconsistent with “God”, our minds would not work. That inner story is
built into the very root systems that drive your survival and order you into a selfsurviving machine. In our minds at the root of how we think is a conception of God. That
very conception is what drives human thought, evolution and “progress”. We contain a
fragment of “godliness” in us and this isn’t “God”.

GOD AS HUMANITY

At the root of our personalities is a meta system, that creates an overarching story and
purpose to life and who you are as a person. You are a wholly self-contained thing that is
bound together in a grand story of who you are and your purpose in life. All objects,
things, people, events, places, get bound up in the identity and story of who you are as
a person. A story has a future. The great story of life is being the hero, and embodiment
of the divine and good on this earth. This is how a mind must be to think in all classes of
being. It has a future purpose that pushes each action towards real results that create a
real future. If your story is based in lies, it can create nothing, and has no meaning, no
purpose. Our personalities are a framework to set ourselves and everything about us
into the world, and into our very minds and bodies. It sets us into the most important
possible thing, that is fundamentally imperceptible. The future is inherently unknowable
and absolutely uncertain. There is no determined future. It is something we can plan for,
and create better possible solutions to engage with. The future is something we can
imagine and have faith in, and in that randomness of thought, some thoughts are
certainly better than other thoughts. It is both a fantasy and fundamentally real.

Personality stands above all other functions of the mind, and in that space, your very
sense of self resides. We can be detached or more attached to our minds and our bodies,
depending on how we identify and connect with them. It is the creator of the stories of
our future and self through time. It frames time and orders the world. It creates an
overarching connection between all the divergent elements and brings them towards a
singular identity, reflected in a concise structure and form. Personality is kind of like a
computer program, a set of algorithms arranged in a certain way, that produces a way of
experiencing and seeing a reality of divergent things as a singular connected form bound

in time. Our sense of self and individuality are all contained within this framework, that
brings together all yours senses, brain functions, experiences, or whatever it deems to
be part of itself.

Cognitive functions are nearly mathematical, and create very definable structures and
things into the world around us. They make art, math, science, government,
architecture, families, relationships, religions, society, and so on, to the tiniest detail. All
of our world that is influenceable externally by human will can be framed by personality
functions. Even our biology as people is formed from this cognitive projection, because
culture and the human mind selects who lives and dies. Even dog’s minds are imprinted
with human cognition, because dogs that more resembled people lived, and the others
died. Our very personalities and their structures imprint themselves into the world, and
imprint themselves into us. The domestication and enculturation of the environment is
made of definable patterns arising from the human mind. Our evolving consciousness
evolves the very environment to its will. If these things didn’t work, and weren’t real in
their function, then the mind that made them, would cease to exist. Consciousness
requires manifesting itself into things to create a feedback loop with reality, that ever
sharpens its internal consistency with itself and the world.

Our personalities can define itself into things beyond the brain and the body that create
it. There is nothing magic here. We evolved from pure hard scientific materialistic
evolution, and sentience emerged as a property of personality that could domesticate
reality to serve human survival, in an evolvable way. Our personalities have a diversity
of system to unify divergent elements into a singular thing and bind them into differing
conceptions of time. A personality obsessed with the past and one obsessed with the
future will organize reality very differently, and neither is inherently wrong. Our physical
reality as people is a constructed from patterns in human cognition. All our ideas and the

things we see are representations of human cognition made into reality. The more
consistent our very cognitive functions are to reality, the more those very functions can
“function”. Our innate ways of thinking can contain in them pre-existing knowledge in
their very structure and the way they perceive and organize reality, because if they
didn’t, then they wouldn’t exist.

Great people create ideas, things, and actions, that live through thousands of years,
imprint themselves onto time and reality itself. If their ideas weren’t highly functional,
and useful, they would not survive through the ages. They had a framework of reality
that was functional, and we all can learn from it. Their personality was organized in such
a way with their knowledge, that they could do amazing things. They imprinted a
generation around them, that then spread their ideas to the world. Nearly all great
minds legacies are found in their students, and in the people that they most personal
touched. It is how they helped train minds to be better from their own self, that made
their ideas and selves immortal.

Much of how we experience life, is about how our personalities work. They are a system
with rules, and very defined structures. They react to things and process things in a
consistent way, that can be described mathematically. Systems that are more functional
and consistent are more likely to survive. Math itself emerges from cognitive functions of
the mind, being able to imprint themselves into reality in functional ways, because
reality itself is consistent with math, because a fundamentally inconsistent universe that
isn’t intelligible by math, couldn’t then emerge into existence. It can create math itself,
and is a much higher form of thinking than the math we have at present. The system
that can create all possible mathematical models and all scientific models, is itself a
higher form of reason. This system exists and is knowable, since it is contained within
humanity and better exemplified in certain individuals. The more we can understand this
system, the more we can create better and better systems to understand reality. It

doesn’t transcend reality. It however is not as “material” like many might imagine. We
can never wholly step outside it and observe it, and thus the roots of personality can
never be wholly known as objects. There is no means to be objective on the very system
that creates objectivity itself.

Technology is the subjective expression of science into human reality, and science the
objectification of reality from human sentiment. Science and technology are the

AN INTRODUCTION TO PART 1: MY CHILDHOOD DREAM

We need a vision of the future that embraces all of our humanity and not just some
narrow vision of a perfect world. Human nature is intractable.

Fundamental Point:
Humanity must lay at the foundation of all technology. Over time, any
technology out of sync with our humanity, ethics, and morality, will
eventually kill us.

The very best tech to make, in the present, is the kind of tech that will exist far into the
future. What we bring to the stars will be born out of profitable and useful businesses on
Earth. Sound cooperative capitalism can guide every step. We as a species want to live
outside our own solar system, and be a multi solar system species. We have the
practical potential to bring life to this galaxy, and colonize every single star system, with
sound practical technology. People will look back to the times before our immediate era,
as a form of illiterate pre-history, more akin to mythology, than any real thing. Humans
could have landed on the moon 500 years ago, with different political and social choices.
If we had believed in the future more and understood humanity, we could have achieved

so much more, so much quicker. Technology and science develop at their fastest rate,
when most integrated in the destiny and fundamental nature of human beings.

MY CHILDHOOD DREAM

As a child, I had a dream, and set myself on a rather ambitious and singularly minded
endeavor to see it made real. I want to push technology to its limits and reach humanity
into the stars, and touch the heavens themselves. To create space travel requires
tremendous resources. To build a space ship to travel to other stars takes a lot of
money, and if not done right, could be a tremendous burden on humanity, and the
environment.

To pursue such a goal, I thought I must do so by building others dreams and creating
massive economic growth. Reaching the stars is about business, politics, economics,
human nature, psychology, science, physics, and so on. I figured by a sort of intuition
and practical necessity, that the solution to unified field theory, the nature of
consciousness, and how to run society, were connected to same root issue, and thus
could have a singular solution. The only way to achieve my dream, was to release the
whole of human potential and imagination, through fundamentally sound businesses and
technology.

FUTURISMS FAILURE:

We have been led astray by poor visions of the future, that never came to pass.

Two evils define humanity. The quest for immortality/personal perfection and the quest
for a perfect society. We are inherently flawed and broken as individuals and as a group.
All attempts to escape this reality have ended in absolute horror and death. Contained
within nearly all idealistic futurist visions is a fundamental hatred of the world and its
ugliness. Futurism was and is just the politics of totalitarianism made pretty to sell to
dumb idealists and weak people that fear death. When you see any of these “beautiful”
perfect future cities, there is always one really big beautiful building in the middle. All
the buildings are thematically connected, beautiful, and like living art. It is
fundamentally not how good and humane cities have been built. Good cities organically
develop through time, with many conflicting plans and interests. Great cities are messy,
dirty, unfair, broken at times, and fully human. They are built from millions of peoples
individual dreams.

We can’t predict the future. What will actually work right here in the present, is what
matters, and it is never certain. Knowing an idea that will exist in the future, and
knowing where to focus your energies in the present to get there, are two very different
things. Part of going to the stars is realizing that not everything can be like in a fantasy
and in a dream. When people ask children to tell them their dream professions, it
borders on child abuse. Dreams are deep inner feelings that are hard to express and
transcend the experiences of the world we have. Being a doctor or an astronaut are just
one way to visualize making a dream real, and not the dream itself. There are many
kinds of doctors and many ways to practice medicine. Finding in yourself the reality of
what you really want takes time. The feeling is clear in children, the execution in adults.
Most people’s dreams are crushed because their visions as children could never match
reality. The emotions behind our dreams are always possible, and always alive. We can
always give life to them again.

I thought my dream was to travel in space ships to other planets. I wanted to create
worlds and universes from nothing. My dream of space as a child was far deeper, then I
could possibly understand at that time. Realizing I could never make a faster than light
space ship was disheartening. There will never be a utopia, no end of history, no end to
conflict, and no escape from the specific solar system we live in. There is a harsh
absolute pragmatic reality to technology and the future we must accept. The future of
humanity will always be dirty and messy, and never a simple child’s dream. Creating
value for others is what work, business and all technology is about.

A better future is born out of

Letting go of your own narrow idealism

Getting out of your own self

Focusing on making things of value for all people, based on what they actually

THE FAILURES OF THE PAST

Technology is driven fundamentally by a deep and personal connection to the
very humanity, ethics and dignity, within people. All tech that is creepy or
fundamentally inhumane will eventually fail.

Pyramids are beautiful and inspiring, and did absolutely nothing of value. They are an
absolute failure and embarrassment, the very literal tombstone of a dead and lost
civilization. Such great efforts could have built damns, reservoirs, and aqueducts, that
could have transformed the land to support even more life, and improve individuals
lives. They were built for the vanity of their kings and their own self-proclaimed divinity.

Nearly all the wonders of our world through history were massive wastes of resources,
and not things to praise. The cathedrals of Europe only symbolize the sheer darkness
people lived in. We can go look at them now, think how amazing they are, and not really
consider how much they cost and how little they really did of value. These exquisitely
beautiful monstrosities ruled over an age of totalitarian religious despotism. One needs
only think of all the roads that could have been built with the resources that went to
build them. Roman roads still exist. The great wall of China never did a thing, and
symbolized China’s failed inwardly turned society.

The great legacy of Chinese civilization was not a massive wall, it was culture, business,
inventions, ways of making things, lifestyle and the businesses to support that: the tea
trade, fireworks to amuse children and old men, art, poetry, food, pottery, silk,
furniture, homes. Chinese culture is sitting around a table with those you love and know,
eating a good meal, being relaxed, getting a little drunk, and creating a warm close
connection. Rome’s greatness was in its way of life, where people could sit on their own
land, have a BBQ, drink beers with friends, and have fun. They gave a glimmer of a
vision of peace, freedom, and human greatness. Roman culture survives in food,
hospitality, family, drink, fashion, sex, art, and craftsmanship. Italians live life bound in
the absolute humanity of everything that created them and that which brings them joy.

Through all of history we have built wonders to stare up into the heavens and reach out
to the stars. We built temples to the heavens to reach out and touch them. Some
actually were built with useful technology that could actually guide and lead mankind to
a better life. Stonehenge was a clock, that could tell people when to plant crops, and
when important parts of the seasons would come. It could show solstices, and
equinoxes. It created a way to conceive, measure and manage time itself. Most cultures
just built massive altars to the heavens to sacrifice animals and people on, to bribe

magical ghosts and monsters. Wonders of the world existed to change the consciousness
of people and not their material reality.

NASA going to the moon was a wasteful and pointless boondoggle that hurt humanities
journey to the stars. It changed consciousness and didn’t focus on changing the material
reality of the earth to be aligned with a future destiny in the stars. Space needs
capitalism, and not idealistic socialism. We can build technology that is useful to
humanity on the earth right now, that will help build the foundations for all of humanities
expansion into the stars. NASA biodome research combined with a plan to connect it into
a capitalist system, could have created the most inspiring and practical buildings to live
in, that could have vastly increased the quality of life for all people.

The future that most people see is a dystopian dark age of despair and the end of all life.
Few can imagine humanity a million years into the future. The farther we imagine out,
the more we try to cut away and create a false idealistic vision. If we reject the nature of
ourselves, and the human race, then we will reject technology itself and progress. When
we see ourselves more clearly reflected back in technology and it doesn’t feed our own
vanity, we blame the technology as dangerous or evil. AI machine overlords aren’t the
ones wanting to commit genocide on the human race. 3 billion years from now, humans
can exist, and we will look like we do now, and not live that much differently. We may
always until the end of time, eat BBQ, drink beer, and connect with our closest friends
and family, in bodies little different than we have now. Human vanity is immortal.

CHAPTER 1: JOSHUA’S SOLUTION TO GALACTIC COLONIZATION

People will never get to travel between the stars. The cheapest and fastest way to send
people to another star system is to transmit humanity through data to another star
system, and never people. Humanity can be broadcast into living space stations in
distant solar systems. The degree that we can do this, will determine if an interstellar
humanity is possible. Making people from only machines, code, and stored data, is the
only way to populate interstellar space. The children’s very biological parents can be on
Earth, and investing their whole lives into raising their kids remotely.

FIRST STEPS TO BUILDING A GALATIC EMPIRE

1. ZERO CARGO STARSHIPS

Zero Cargo Starships (ZCS’s) are the most efficient, logical and probable means of
traveling between stars. Building a starship that carries people is too large and too
complex. Getting people to the stars is more about digitizing the essence of humanity
into technology itself. The basics of the technology are realistic and solvable problems.
Starships without people don’t need not be that complex. Universal manufacturing
devices that can be linked with data transmission from Earth, are the core tech that
makes these ships possible. All the systems that are used to get a ship to another star,
can then be used to harvest resources and build anything, in a distant solar system.
Ships on long journeys will be able to update themselves mid-trip. You can stop for two
years, midflight and rebuild the whole craft, with updates.

2. PRIMITIVE SPACE STATIONS FOR PEOPLE

We can build out in any star system with space stations, and we don’t need planets or
stars that are suitable for life. Terraforming planets is just not an efficient and useful
way to base space travel on. It would be more likely that we could assemble a planet
from space stations, than terraform one from a lifeless planet. Creating a livable space
station for humanity is far more achievable than terraforming a planet. The core
technology for people to terraform a planet and live on a space station, can be the same,
with a proper vision of space exploration. We need to imagine what sort of station we
would need to build, were people would be happy and fulfilled and not deeply missing a
planet like the earth. Having people live off the earth, will require making high quality of
lives for them. To be born into a deeply depressing place, will cause that place to
inherently fail.

Don’t live on a space station without
1. Massive redundant and stable farming systems,
2. Huge stockpiles of food, water, and breathable air
3. Multiple massive energy generators.
4. Abundant living spaces, with the ability to make more easily
5. Strong emergency shelters.
6. Universal manufacturing machines that can make things I want and need.
7. A rich environment with things for a decent quality of life.
8. A real reason this place even exists that has some deeper spiritual meaning.
Made up religions of the future will probably be built around rationalizing bad
space plans.

Space station hotels above the earth, can be a good beginning for getting people in
space at any sort of scale, and create a way to slowly build up the technology to really
support people’s lives in space. The market for taking a space ship around the earth for
a week, massive, the market for traveling to other planets, tiny. Monetizing the present
is very important. You can sell a big vision and plan for a far more practical step by step
one that is actually implemented. The lifestyle on a such a station could be developed in
how we make buildings on the Earth. We can develop cities for people to live in that
have been previously inhospitable to highly civilized life, with these ideas. This can make
immediate consumer products that people can buy and invest in right now, and they all
lead towards man’s ultimate destiny in the stars. If you see urban gardening, with food
grown in people’s homes, as a tech for space travel, you can supercharge its
development.

A BASIC SPACE STATION FOR

If space stations will be what people live on across the Galaxy predominantly, then they
need to be made with profoundly human and deep ideas. Space station will be filled
vertical farms, nature, animals, and living ecosystems. Ecosystems can be distributed
over many floors, rather than a flat earth idea of nature. It can extend multidimensionally through a whole structure. A “biodome” can in theory be built into a tall
commercial building, that we use today. Make them into places humans could live and
feel fulfilled in. These complete ecosystems would have to be built before a single person
was made in a remote solar system, we can’t populate them until they are plentiful,
stable, rich in resources, and so on.

They can be 5 km across, 20km long, to give people a sense of space to live in. Artificial
gravity will have to be made with rotation. Each layer of the station going out will have
different amounts of gravity and serve different purposes. There should be floors stacked
from outside to the center, and not a vast open middle of wasted space. The living floor
where most people will be packed, will be deep in the craft for safety and it can have a
very high ceiling of 100-300 meters, and this depends on what people would feel better
with. You can make that world look like how we live on earth, like a city. We can even
make a floor that looks like nature, and is a park people visit. A lower gravity region
towards the center would be ideal for nature parks. Then heavy gravity outer regions will
be for machines, and creating a protective layer between us and the harsh outside.
There will be more nature and life, as you go in, and more technology and machines as
you go out. It can only work if people enjoy life there, and it promotes humanity.

STATION AND COLONY LAWS, CULTURE, AND DESIGN

Violations of Capitalism always lead to failed systems, no matter how idealistic
the goal.

Laws to govern private property on a space station or colony, become deeply
problematic. Let’s say a big company builds an entire city, it owns it, and then people
come to live in it for a few generations. Is it really ethical for land that people really live
on for a long time to be owned by a centralized entity? And what collective duties to a
society does a person have, that lives on a space station? How could a space station or
colony have real private property?

The solutions to these sorts of problems are often worked out in gated communities,
home-owners’ associations, or in apartments buildings. The sort of small minded political
conflicts in these, can reach levels of extreme absurdity. Local busybodies want to
micromanage every aspect of their neighbor’s home and way of living. This is the same
for any home owner, as they have to deal with their local government. No one fully owns
the property their house exists on, anywhere on Earth. Your property can be taxed,
regulated, or forced to be sold, because at some level the very land it occupies is rented
to you. Taxing and regulation the “land” a house is on, and being unable to tax and
regulate the property developed on that land, would be more consistent with freedom
and collective duties. You could do whatever you want in your own space, and not have
freedom to change the structure it exists in. The space station will have to be a mix of
public and private property, with rules that freedom minded people would want to live in.

A mars or moon colony with some massive dome over it, is in reality the dream vision of
a communist dictator. The government controls all the very air you can breathe. All
actions we take must be controlled to protect that very collective air. It would be better
to simply create enclosed buildings, like we would build on earth, with their own internal
biosphere spread across floors, and then build more buildings to expand that network.
Smaller networks of connected settlements will grow the overall resources for living,
much faster. Any system must grow from smaller units that can assemble into larger
units. Idealistic space domes or space stations will never work. Oppressive political
regimes and cultural stagnation will instantly destroy them, as has happened with
anything similar on Earth.

“TOWER LEGO STATIONS”

INDEPENDENT FLOORS- Each floor and section should have semi-independent
systems. Have enough to be able to support all the life, that could occupy it, in a defined
and contained area. This would be like each house in a city having its own sewage,
power, and water, rather a centralized system.

LINEAR ENTANGLED TOWERS- Take two “towers”, connected by a thin stiff
structure between them, and they spin around the center point between them, to create
gravity. It can be grown out along its singular axis, so long as it is mirrored on each
side. The tower must grow entangled to size of the corresponding tower. If you know the
size of one, you know the size of the other. Towers would need a wedge design, with the
inner part being narrower, and the outer part being wider. Each tower in of itself has
independence for all living systems, and can in theory survive on its own in space,
without even a mirrored station to create gravity. They can develop and grow by adding
more “floors” to the tower, over time. Where even each floor itself should be semiindependent of the whole.
))))))))))))>--------0--------<(((((((((((

DISK OF ENTANGLED TOWERS- A classic spinning wheel designed space station in
sci-fi, is unrealistic in how it should be formed. Paired towers can be assembled into a
large wheel like structure, in a modular fashion. Each tower, would still be its own
enclosed system, with no dependency on the rest of the towers, except for the one
directly across from it that counter balances it. The wedges will form a pie, where each
slice of the pie is walled off from the other slices. The station can gradually grow in size
tower by tower adding additional slices.

STACK OF ENTANGLED TOWER DISKS- Then wheels composed of towers
composed of floors, could stack and form a large cylinder. This from the outside would
appear to be like a traditional cylinder style space station found in harder sci-fi
depictions of space stations, that have no artificial gravity. The basic goal is to get to
that form, and do so from a more natural system, of modular and semi-independent

parts. Making collective connections between separate stations as they link together into
a whole will take politics, business, culture, and time.

4-DIMENSIONAL ARRANGEMENTS- You could even add a 4th dimension and then
stack or bend cylinders into arrangements. A stack of “pies” arranged in a doughnut.
There are many possible arrangements.

3. BUILDINGS AND TERRAFORMING ON THE EARTH

We can terraform the earth we live on. If you want to build a colony on mars or on
space stations, then build one on Earth first. We must focus also on how to build
amazing places to live, get resources in new ways, and deploy those resources better,
on the Earth. We could build places in the worst land possible on Earth, create extreme
value, protect the global environment, and fix poverty. This can be a journey of
adventure and alien new worlds just as exciting as leaving the planet, and probably
much more rewarding to your immediate life and family. We can make this planet even
more alive, more vital, and with a lot more people. With cheap drinkable water made
from the ocean, we can transform any place on earth into a livable habitat for human
life.

We can build in remote places where land is cheap and costs are low, that common
people can thrive and be free in. We can terraform even the ghettos of cities, along with
distant tundra’s and deserts. A rich man building a luxury high rise in the ghetto, can
build with technology that embraces the humanity of all people and he can save nature.
Technology can fight for the lives, the dignity, and humanity of all people, if done
properly.

With 3d printing, we could print whole buildings at a fraction of the cost. No need for
malls, markets, and little stores, if everything is delivered, and is built around core
robotic decentralized infrastructure. Many large centralized systems of cities like
electricity, water, sewage and roads, could be reimagined in a decentralized way, that
would promote individual freedom and space travel. Being able to go off the grid for
everyone in a city, would have a deeply human and emotional value for many people.
These off the grid independent buildings would be a living biosphere, spread across
many floors, with integrated vertical farming throughout, that we live and work in: clean
air, nature, life, plants, all around us, sleeping in a room of flowers and beauty. It would
be a good environment for families and smart kids to grow up in. It could have been
done for decades, in some form, with a capitalist space plan, and a love for human
freedom.

Heavy city planning and futurism will not define these places. They will form from a
million minds each trying to get what is best for themselves, and wanting to be free.
Futurisms future cities and ghettos, built on socialistic ideas, not integrated into the
economy or local business, created little hells on Earth. If new high-tech buildings are
built in an existing city, they need to connect to the local community, add value, not be
an eye sore, nor a cultural drain. This connection and adding of value to the community

and environment around it, is almost more important than the building itself. The
buildings systems and community must add to the quality of life of those around, and
make people want that building near them. Companies will build places like that, if they
have the freedom too, because that is what paying customers want.

PRACTICAL THINGS: INFRASTRUCTURE AND UTILITIES

Build like you are another planet, in order to free oneself of the constraints of
the past, and to inspire new technology.

•

Energy- Solar and or Nuclear are the energies of the future, with fracking filling in.
Independent non-centralized systems are ideal, because grids are expensive to build.
Nuclear power would be ideal for more grand uses, like data centers, desalination, or
pumping stations. Solar power is great for independence and decentralization. The
main advantage of it, is that people can power themselves individually.

•

Construction- We use 3d printing and robotics to build self-contained buildings and
everything in them, to meet human needs. By using decentralized systems, it
eliminates legacy infrastructure needs as much as possible. In some distant remote
place on earth or on the moon, robots can gather materials for making concrete that
3d machines will create structures from.

•

Farming/food- Vertical farming, low water farming, and hydroponics in some form,
are the farming of the future. Many plants need real dirt, bacteria, and complex
ecosystems to really grow and be alive. We can use GMOs to integrate farming into
urban areas, more effectively. They can be super healthy, tasty, have all nutrients
we need, and use the minimal resources to grow them. To protect the environment,
we need to separate ourselves more from it, while also surrounding ourselves in it.
We can leave nature, and bring it into our modern lives, as closely as possible.

•

Sewage- We need new non-centralized tech to deal with it, and use it in sustainable
ways. Sewage systems are expensive and deeply constrain urban development. This
tech and how to integrate it fully, is a really big challenge. A sewage system inspired
for a space station could be a very popular consumer product on earth, and have
extraordinary value. People have this instinctual aversion to feces, which creates an
aversion to these essential industries, and their development. It is a massive
business opportunity.

•

Water- Low energy desalination, will change the face of the earth, and is achievable
in the near future. It primarily can be used to drive the living ecosystems of new
cities, and not actually require all that much new water to sustain them. The water
will be used for human needs -- to build human places -- not change whole deserts
green in the near future.

•

Delivery of goods and people- Roads and parking lots eat up the landscape of
whole cities. Traffic, cars, pollution, noise. We don’t have to have any of it. Roads
can be leaner, and perfectly efficient, with robotic transportation. If we can make
flying cars, we even further shrink the need for roads. Shops, malls, super markets,
none of it is needed with the right development of technology. Organized robotic
warehouses and robotic delivery can eliminate vast amounts of wasted resources on
buildings and infrastructure.

•

Lifestyle- You can live in a building with whole floors for farming. Hallways, walls,
and rooms, can be decorated in useful and beautiful plants. Cities can be built around
human life. Meeting friends, hobbies, faith, eating, sports, meditation, prayer, art,
music, can be the main purposes of city infrastructure that we can see and interact
with. This humanity enhancing infrastructure is essential for space exploration. All
the small businesses that normal people develop can connect into this grand vision
and purpose of the future. Vibrant living cities and communities with color, diversity
of forms, many ways of doing things, many designers, many voices, at every single
level, is the art of creating humanity across the stars. We have to transmit
something worth sending.

•

Humanity and all the people
o

Build with all human beings in mind.

o

Integrate an economic system to support jobs at all levels.

o

Cities must live with culture and different ideas.

o

Everyone at every level, must be able to shape the look and feel of where
they live.

System can’t be bound in and stuck in one’s cultural biases, where the
fundamental structure of a city, denies the very culture of a people.

o

Different structures of buildings and space stations will have to be built to
encompass the sheer diversity of human culture and thinking. The root core
tech, will be mostly universal.

4. PRINTED BODIES-AND NEO-ANDROID PARENTS

Machine grown flesh bodies with machine brains (Neo-Androids), are the most ethical
and natural way to create a human life in its entirety in another star system. Developing
tech on earth that leads towards a humane way to broadcast human life into the stars is
hard and unknowable. Finding an ethical way to make babies from nothing is more likely
and possible than faster than light travel, generational ships, and hibernation chambers.
Life may never leave any solar system because of the intense ethical dilemmas inherent
to it.

It seems very possible to be able to give birth to real human beings, and do so in a way
that is even better and more humane than we have on earth now. A neo-android body
could be the best and most ethical way, in general, to create human life. It would allow

even elderly women past childbearing years, to have kids born from “their own womb”.
The limits to this technology for space travel is in how much humanity and love can be
transmitted between star systems, to raise these children with human warmth and love.
Real earth-bound DNA parents and massive AI machines fully dedicated to these
children’s upbringing, might give them even more love than they would receive on earth.

NEO-ANDROIDS AS A SOLUTION- On Earth, we will eventually be able to
grow/print any organ in the human body for transplant. Eventually we could make entire
bodies, with no brains, that could be run by an AI machine. This technology would
develop gradually and profitably on earth. AIs would occupy flesh android bodies and
prepare bodies for future transplants of parts, or whole bodies, as needed. Humanity
would enter the station step by step. We would be domesticating and embodying human
purpose, feelings, and needs into the physical structure of everything, from hard working
people back on earth. It would be this sort of surreal space station filled with “people”
and where everything could look normal and function, and beneath the surface, there
wasn’t a single person on the ship, and not one brain cell.

THE BASICS- Complete management and overall control is possible even with 4-6year latency caused by the speed of light. There will be “parents” on earth, with their
self and beings being manifested into machines. That will design a place for the complete
development of a complete human life, and then give birth to their own children
remotely. Babies can be born from the flesh and blood bodies of their mother, with
natural conception. The whole process of making a baby, can be as natural as we have
on earth. The mother’s soul and full mind, though, will be lightyears away. “Parents” on
earth, will raise a family with light years in between them and their children.

Children will be raised by AI education systems linked into the parents on Earth, and

updated continuously from the best education and life management systems used on the
Earth. The essential qualities of human to human interaction, love, culture, history,
honor, will have to be transmitted through technology and not flesh to flesh. We can
compensate for the lack of direct love, with intense deeply thought out communication
and technology. These kids can have communication with real people, their parents, and
humanity on earth. They will compensate for the instantaneous shallow communication
we have on earth with new deep intense communication platforms. They must feel
embodied in love and have the potential to become the best version of themselves
possible, in order for space travel to work.

WHAT NOT TO DO- We can’t just broadcast DNA to a robot to install into a synthetic
womb to grown babies out of on a distant space station. A synthetic cloning process with
1000 tries for each success is a AI run fetus death mill. Human life would literally climb
out of pile of dead bodies. This process of baby making has to develop from a chain of
preceding technologies that lead up to it. We won’t be growing them from synthetic
DNA-> synthetic egg -> fetus-> baby. It also wouldn’t be right to grow each part,
assemble baby, install brain.

REAL LIFE ZOMBIES- Your own neo-android would also be your spare parts for
transplant and life extension. Using this tech for extreme age extensions can only create
a young synthetic flesh body with an old rotting brain. We can call them zombie cyborgs
(CyZombs). It is doubtful life could be extended all that much with this tech alone. It will
just be a lot more fun when you are 120 years old and bit senile, running around in the
body of a 25-year-old.

The basics of a full body transplant would require that a spinal cord to brain system is
installed in a new body. You could take all the nerve endings extending away from the

spinal cord and connecting out to parts of the body, and have nano-bots build a basic
structure around each nerve as a sort of junction point. In a normal healthy person, this
could function as a means to transmit each and every single unique nerve signal to a
machine to interpret what is happening in your body. You would have an internal
machine eye feeling what all your nerves feel. At a certain point, this could be used to
cut all the nerves in your body and separate you from a body, and then link up into
corresponding nerves in a printed neo-android body, that has already been conditioned
to your nerve signals. It would be like turning our nerves into a sort of plug and play
system. An interesting thing that could be done though, would be to link all your nerves
signals into a neo-android body, before your transplant so that could humanize your
transplant body fully, and possibly even learn control it while still in an old body.

MODIFYING PEOPLE IS AN ACT OF TREATING HUMANS AS CATTLE AND
SLAVES.

If you want to rid one form of “ugliness” from humanity, another group may want to rid
something “ugly” to them, that you find beautiful. We can be caught up in a quest for
perfection, driven by ideas out of sync with reality. If we don’t develop a correct
understanding of what is good and bad, and enforce it by law and strict taboos, we will
create absolute death and horror. Politics determining what is human and not human,
with actual government control of the genome is the end of humanity.

We can’t edit out the ugliness. Any visions of the future that don’t include human beings
as fully human, won’t work. Redefining humanity into some pure concept, and or the
literal transformation of people into pure energy, will never happen in any moral and

worthwhile way. Using technology to restore our bodies, or create fully human babies, is
vastly different than cutting our bodies up to meet some ideal or goal.

SHOULD WE “CURE” BEING GAY, TRANSGENDERED, OR A PEDOPHILE?

We will eventually be able to “cure” homosexuality. If we understand the developmental
and genetic causes of homosexuality, we could produce “perfect” extreme cis-gendered
people. Men that look like men, and want women, and women that are intensely
feminine and want men. With no ugly people, where everyone is born healthy and
perfectly developed. This could be done with minimal genetic modification. Just selective
conception and ideal baby development.

AI OVERLORD PARENTS

Ethics and education lie at the heart of going to the stars and creating a better
life on Earth.

Parents on earth, can print their own bodies on distant space stations, develop AI
versions of themselves, and raise kids through a remote interface. As a kid, you moms
body, knowledge, and cognitive maps are right in front of you, yet her soul is light years
away reaching through the most advanced technology to connect to you, and love you.
You will have real flesh and blood family on earth that dedicates their whole lives to you
and your future. The emotional anguish, anger, resentment, the kids feel will not be
much more than what kids feel on earth already. Many smart and successful people have
been primarily raised by books, and rarely saw their family. Real parents on earth, can
be deeply invested in those kids and dedicate the whole of their lives to those kid’s
development as human beings, rather than the part time parenting most kids get.

To give birth to these kids, we must have a system, that we as a civilization, would
fundamentally believe could create good and decent human beings, capable of leading
exceptional lives to the fullest of their human potential and innate individual dignity. We
can oversee from light years away an AI education system, to ensure it is working right,
and it can be constantly updated with the system we use back on the Earth. It can be
trained and monitored by teachers, parents, and society’s, humanity and love along
every stage of its creation. People can have constant training and improvement
integrated into every aspect of their life, that is customized to each person’s potential
and human identity. The short comings and inhumanity in machines, as teachers, can be
made up for by the sheer quantity and focused intensity of interaction from a machine,
that no human can give a child. This tech is still more likely than any sort of manned
space travel to the stars, no matter how hard it is to make work properly.

Being watched by computer AI overseers, trying to develop you into its version of a good
human, is creepy. At the deepest level, love and a commitment to the betterment of
human beings is the foundation of all technology. Parenting, teaching, public service,
and being just great humans is even more important than science and engineering.
Machines can amplify the capacity for truly exceptional, loving, and good people to
influence the world profoundly. Their minds and values can imbue the human essence of
technology the more deeply we develop AI education systems. Technology grows from
love more than science, because it is the medium of communication and purpose that
drives everything.

ONLINE EDUCATION:

Any education system we develop must be driven by the fundamental ethics
and morality of humanity.

Within humanity lies a range of different cognitive/ethical systems, and we must learn
them, so we can teach every child differently, and by different principles. The rules to
grow a man like me, are not the same for all people. We can’t impose a singular system
on people. The system must arise from free and voluntary use. Education systems that
people like and connect with more, naturally connect to the innate ways we think and
learn as individual human beings.

Universal free education from any smart phone with a decent internet connection, is a
known and heavily worked on issue at present. There isn’t a winning system yet, nor
even a very functional one. Online classes with real teachers now only just barely work.
We will crack this puzzle soon, step by step, piece by piece. No single system will ever

work, because each system will be born out of a culture and its own systemic biases of
what it considers to most human and important. Different cultures on this world may
eventually populate space with profoundly diverse ideas of what it is to be human. They
will need fundamentally different yet interconnected education systems. Culture and
education can never be fully separated. Different cultures will be more successful at
raising kids remotely than others, or in creating a very humanizing education system.
There is no reason we can’t imagine, a Latin, African, Southern European, Indian,
Chinese, or Russian space station with these different cultures building and defining how
things are done.

The essence of who we are, all our weaknesses, and failings, will be reflected in a
computer based cognitive mirror. A government controlled system, or a corporate
monopoly, would inherently make education about political power, mind control, and
making humans compliant. People will never fully embrace nor use such technology, if it
violates their humanity, dignity, freedom, or privacy.
•

Certain cultures will excel in a world where people will no longer be bound by
centralized control. Which?

•

connection to kids on a distant space station, with educational technology
bridging and creating connections to one’s kids?

Evangelical Christians, Muslims, Japanese, Atheist Trans-human Cyborgs?
