Also investigate who he wants to role model himself after. If he loves Steve Jobs, then
also help channel the lessons of Steve Jobs to that kid. Can also suggest role models,
show him people and see who he likes. Get a group of more than one person. We admire
people for very specific qualities. Investigate what they really like.

Take all the aspects he likes and unify them into one game, and at a level his son can
start to do. Can play with art tools and gather up images and styles he likes across many
sources. Father can help get them organized and do things his son can’t do or isn’t even
aware of yet, but the boy can feel he is doing all. He is the “leader” of sorts. The boy
asks “HOW?”, and this will inverse typical parenting roles. And the father can teach and
help based on his kid’s needs, arising from the kid. The “how” questions leads to respect
back to his father, and to different things that the father can teach him. Parents can’t do
it all, and they delegate a lot to mentors and trainers. Find teachers the kid can use,
even if just virtual.

Then clean up and prototype the overall package. Father can talk and guide son. Not
criticize bad habits, but empower new better habits. The boy can learn to keep all the
previous 5 steps clear in his own mind, as a child can understand them, when he finds
himself straying. The father is instilling effective habits, ethics and values into his son
through training him to do the things he asks his father to help him do. The vice of
playing is the danger that will keep him from succeeding. With power comes temptation
to use it not to fulfill a responsibility but to avoid them, and the father can mitigate this

by keeping the son focused on the goals the child set for themselves and adjusting those
goals as the child comes to understand what they really want.

COLLECTIVE HUMANE CYBERNETICS: CIVILIZING AND SAVING ALL
MANKIND

JOSHUA’S LAWS OF CYBERNETICS

Cybernetics is fundamentally a bridge to humanize AI, and thus turn it into
something that we can profoundly accept and embrace. Humanity must
maintain dignity and never objectified.

We have to explore that exact line where cybernetics are ethical, and not ethical--where
want we to embrace them, and where they are just plain creepy, ugly and wrong. People
driven to mutilate themselves in pursuit of an ideal fixation, if allowed to have free reign,
would be bad for techs development. Creepy “hi tech” people, frighten people and limit
technologies future development. Developing technology in the least creepy way, will
allow to grow the fastest, and be embraced by humanity.
•

First Rule of Cybernetics: Cybernetics for body and brain parts, should be
able to be turned off, and that person should be better off than if they
never had those augmentations.

•

Second Rule of Cybernetics: The system should make a person more
human. Their individual freedom and dignity must be expanded.

•

Third Rule of Cybernetics: Follow medical ethics. Do no harm. Don’t
damage healthy functioning body parts.

BUILDING COGNITIVE CYBORGS (CYCOGS)

We can augment people, with even IQs below 85, by turning their reality into a cartoon,
and enhance their ability to succeed in the world and do things of value. The very
interfaces of modern first-person video games are not much different than how we could
literally live in the world, for those that need this help. All of existence can be simplified,
exaggerated, and slowed, for less developed minds to perceive important things more
clearly. Cybernetic interfaces can be built around people’s sensations, so that their very
senses are processed through machines, and their self is expressed out through their
senses. We don’t need to cut or install anything into people. The technology can be as
simple as glasses, headphones, and gloves. We will be turning people into a kind of
cyborg that I call- Cognitive cyborgs (CyCogs).

Humans will still be human, and we still be what we have always been through the ages.
Technology must make us more human and enrich our lives. Cybernetics must be life
affirming. We don’t need robot limbs, nor robot eyes, or chips implanted in our brains.
This technology will also constrain the dangerous elements in society, and possibly be
the very foundation and means by which collective norms are imposed on people, and
where we as a society are protected from harmful and dangerous individuals. It can be
the foundations of collective education, civilizing mankind, and binding us together. Mass
killings, terrorism, murder, robbery and suicide should be far lower with such
technology. How we do this, is far trickier, and can create a new form of
authoritarianism, unless it is an inherently un-hackable decentralized system. It certainly
can help the disabled and less fortunate, live better if done correctly. The very first
people to help with technology, could ideally be autistic children with fully functioning
intelligent minds unable to connect fully to the world.

In the big picture, this is about the disabled kid, in all of us, that has a full functioning
mind that can’t connect to the world fully. Our inner humanity can be amplified by
technology and then shape that very technology to the beauty of the human soul that
lies trapped inside us. This technology will help you to express yourself and find more
deeply in yourself who you are, what you want, and to reach your full potential. It will be
mirror inside yourself, and a means to communicate those things inside you to the
world, where only the smartest and most creative people could express themselves
before. We will be augmenting human intelligence with AI, at a more root and personal
level, where anything AI can do, then all of humanity will be able to do it.

Countless masterpieces of music and art have existed in minds through history, that
never learned how to play musical instruments, write music, or craft any art, and so
these things were never created, and we as a civilization go to experience them. Only
the most talented people could express their deep inner visions and ideas through
history. Technology will lessen the skills and resources people need to bring their inner
visions to life. A single person can be a symphony and not even be able to play one of
the instruments, and still create music more beautiful than any musician trained to play.
AI is humanized through a deep innate cybernetics interface, that allows cybernetics and
AI together to augment us to our fullest. It is just a tool, that extends out from us and
expresses us. We will be able to be augmented with AIs directly through a CyCog
interface, and train AIs in turn through that system.

COLLECTIVE AUTISM

We live at present, in a collective Autistic Society with asocial walls between us
where we can see each other and hear nothing, with little empathy.

AUTISM- Autism is a disability where people have fully functioning brains inside, that
can’t connect to the world easily. They live behind metaphorical sound proof glass walls
that get thicker and harder, as the environment becomes more threatening and
overwhelming. They can see out but not connect. Degrees of autism relate to the
thickness and height of those walls. They can be overcome and breached with will power
and training. At a basic level autism, is having no sensory filter. Autism causes people to
become sensory overloaded, more readily. The brains natural defenses cause a
shutdown, to protect the ego. Inside their own mind, they often develop strong and
unique inner characters, with intense passions directed at things.

“COLLECTIVE AUTISM” is a disease that infects our society. As collective groups, we
behave little different than individual autistic people. When the fundamental cultural
institutions of society are destroyed, eroded away, it releases an autistic walling off in
society, as people can no longer cognitively communicate and connect to groups
different than themselves. Social skills between out group members is dropping. In
general, Autistic people are not attached to any fixed external social system, and are
dimly aware of the one they live in. Educating them to fit into society, in a way they will
embrace, lays at the foundation of building societies, and managing the collective
autistic crisis we face in post-modern society. How we learn to create society on Earth,
from technology itself, will define us as a species.

In a space station of babies, born from neo-androids, with no real parents, no culture,
no society, and no human network of interactions, they will be collectively and
individually Autistic. They will be highly asocial disconnected society, with people that

connect with machines and fantasy worlds, more than actual people. They have none of
the legacy systems built through generations upon generations of families, cultures,
government, companies, and social institutions to nourish them and connect them into
the world. Our present world of children raised by televisions, the internet, and computer
games, without strong culture and parental upbringing, is not much different.

AUTISTIC PEOPLE AS CYCOGS

The personal computer was a bicycle for the mind, and with AR tech we can turn them it
into a wheelchair for the mind. AR can enhance the humanity and living standards of
people with autism, schizophrenia, Tourette’s syndrome, dyslexia, ADHD, low general
intelligence, Alzheimer’s, and so on, live more functional lives. Autistic people can
become the first cognitive cyborgs. If you saw a person walking down the street with a
VR gear headset on, with cameras and sensors all over it, you would probably want to
avoid them and find them very creepy, unless it was a tool that helped empower that
person person and you knew it didn’t invade your privacy.

TREATING AUTISM- Cartoons are very helpful and powerful in the treatment of
autism. Lots of deep inner emotions are learned from cartoons by being able to identify
and project themselves into those virtualized stories. They have deep therapeutic value,
even for adults. The simplified realities help people learn the main themes and ideas of
human reality quicker. If they can eventually get outside their own mind and connect
with the world, they can sometimes lead the world towards amazing new things.

AR/VR/MR- The line between, fantasy and reality will be completely blurred and fluid.
The interface and purpose of the system is to connect people more to the world and help
train them, so they eventually won’t even need help to function.
•

Augmented Reality (AR)- This would be like the “Heads Up Display” (HUD) that
players use in most video games, except where the real world is still seen and the
HUD overlays the world.
o

Put information next to a person’s face to show what they are feeling.

o

Show lines of where to walk and go to, overlaid on the real world.

o

See information about how to do things, right next to what you need to
do. Automatic tutorials and guidebooks for everything. Real people can
even come in and assist when needed.

o

“Health meters”- Sensors tracking stimulation levels, and helping them
manage any potential emotional breakdowns.

o

Certain parts of reality can be cut out to minimize its influence, and as
people get better, they can expand what they see.

•

Mixed Reality (MR)- To turning everything around them into 3d computer
animation, and fully filtering the world, and making it more palatable to a mind
under stress.
o

A cartoon chair they see to sit on, would be a real chair they can sit on. It
can be made to look different, friendlier, or more fun, or just simpler.

o

A person’s face could be turned into a cartoon version of a face, and their
emotions and expression could be exaggerated and slowed so they can
understand what feelings people are showing.

o

Turning crowds of people in an airport walking, into a school of fish
swimming through the air, to reduce the chaos of so many people.

•

Virtual Reality (VR) -They can then slip into full virtual worlds, even in public, if
sitting down, and play intense video games, dive into educational experiences,
watch movies, listen to music, or create things and do work. They can calm and

focus the mind, by diving into a safe virtual world, and still be doing useful things
and engaging reality in some way.

CREEPY CAMERAS- If we can censor and shut out elements of the world for autistic
people, then AI linked cameras, should not see people’s faces, unless those people want
to be seen. Imagine people walking around in full VR systems, with multiple cameras
and sensors attached to them. Cameras on glasses helping direct a blind person walk
and interact with the world, would seem very acceptable. Glasses presenting text
subtitles of speech for deaf people, that could read lips in noisy rooms, would seem very
acceptable. Always on cameras on a person, with no explicit purpose, would seem
creepy. There are ways to make cameras watching everything more human and less
creepy. There has to be interactive lights that inform the world around them, what is
being seen and what level of reality that person is in. The system needs to be built with
a fundamental respect for privacy, so that people feel more comfortable to be around it,
and with people using the technology

COMPUTER VISION- Cameras that computers use are different than the ones people
use. Having computer visual sensors viewing the world can protect people’s privacy
more than constantly on cameras recording everything into video, that people can look
at. Machines can, instead of recording a video, record 3d models of what it sees. These
3d sensors, allow computer intelligence to see the environment and begin to have an
understanding of it. We can take the world we see and layer 3d models into it, with
anything we want. We can make a cartoon version of the world we are seeing in front of
us. Where all the things in, will be located in the same place, and just have different
surfaces than we would normally see.

CARTOON RENDERED REALITY- Autistic kids can experience a cartoon rendered
version of reality they can interact with in real time and in real life. This can control their
level of sensory input, where their senses can be limited in one way, and expanded in
another. The things they see will be there, but made simpler and with more complex

distracting things filtered out, or limited. All the peripheral things can be edited out, and
only things they can interact with, will be presentable. Then in each of those
interactions, they can be presented options, and information about the situation layered
over it. This can be done step by step, with the techs natural development.

Imagine seeing a face through a camera, and that cameras data being feed into an
analytics program that interprets possible meanings to those expressions and then
presents that data in a simple way overlaying their social interaction. Emotional emoji’s
hovering near a person, could give them the social data they need. Multiple emotions
can even float around, with different possibilities for each. 30% happy 10 % upset 25%
lying, etc. The very composite of emotions is an emotion to consider. Another level of
this would be to make a cartoon face of a person, and exaggerate and highlight all
emotional expressions on their face, so they can more readily pick up meaning. Turn
people’s faces into cartoon versions and then exaggerate and slow down their emotional
expressions, so autistic people can see and understand them.

BENFITS FOR FAMILIES- To be able to take autistic children freely through airports,
subway metro systems, public transportation, shops and malls, or just anywhere, would
be a big enhancement in the quality of life for families with autistic children. The
technology would also help train and teach them, get them out in the world, get them
interacting with people, and thus more rapidly developing their skills to cope with the
real world. Actual interaction and life experience are the best teachers, and that
disconnection they have is why they don’t learn as readily. At first the systems would be
large and bulky, more inhuman looking. Over time they can be made more human, and
show the complete face of the person, with minimal hardware covering up the face.

EDUCATION TECH- A cognitive wheelchair is just an education platform, for
developing minds. Those that can dive into the technology will be best able to learn. We
can have 3d worlds where one can do virtual chemistry and science experiments. Where

we can project materials out into the real world to interact with, right on a living room
table if need be. Engineering/art/music systems where people can assemble things in
visual 3d forms becomes possible and basically accessible for everyone.

What are the values and ethics that must imbue such a system, for people to
really fundamentally engage at the deepest levels?

KANTIAN ETHICS, INTENTIONS AND CYBERNETICS

Manifesting the intentions and humanity of the disabled and all humans, is the ultimate
ethical measure of this technology. The more it can bring out the desires, thoughts,
feelings, and good intentions of people, the more ethical a world we can create. Ethics is
not about people acting good, it is about individuals being able to express directly their
intentions and real selves into the world in complex and unpredictable ways. A CyCog
needs to become more human and more expressing of themselves through this
technology, and that will drive its growth and integration into society.

Seeing a CyCog from the outside, and not knowing that a person was using this
technology, they would look like super-humans able to do things beyond what we think
of people normally being able to do. They would seem like “Jedi”, using the “force” and
able to do nearly magical acts. They could step on the exact right spot, at the right time,
and do the correct movement, and it would seem inhumanly competent. It would be like
talking to someone that has Wikipedia on demand, and you didn’t know what Wikipedia
was; they would seem to be the smartest person you knew. Many people when talking in
real life, take short breaks away, look things up online, and come back to conversations

with info they found online, so they seem smarter. This sort of knowledge can be
expanded into far more aspects of our life, and personalized to our needs.

The interface is about connecting technology with humanity, in a way where humanity is
augmented and not consumed by technology. An easy and intuitive to use interface is
one built around human thinking, and thus makes technology more domesticated to
human thought and needs. The humanity and intentions of the techs creators can help
augment the humanity of the techs users. We as people still have to make choices and
decisions based on our principles and inner humanity. A CyCog system that doesn’t
augment ethics and humanity, is an invalid system, that must be resisted as a form of
slavery, over malleable minds.

Smart and fully functional people using a system like this to fulfill specialized skill sets in
life, would truly become super-human, even from the perspective of people that know
they are using such a system. The extremely talented can be augmented so far, that it
can take humanity to another level. The reality of such a system is a tremendous danger
to society when used by the elite rather than the disabled and the unintelligent. The
system must make people from the inside feel human and humble. If one wants a
system to bring out the best in the best, then it needs to magnify their humanity and
connection to humanity more than raw power and ability. While the smart can be superhuman in specific skills, it doesn’t mean their humanity is superhuman. We are all people
after all.

COGNITIVE MIRRORS, TRANSHUMANS, AND THE SINGULARITY

AI connected into humanity makes it possible for the “body” of a person” to
manifest into the very structure of anything.

The singularity is never coming. Our humanity and all its ugliness is who we
are, and can’t just be cut away, or transcended.

People envision a point in the future when artificial intelligence can improve upon itself
and reach an accelerating rate of improvement, simply leave all human intelligence
behind, and allow human beings to be converted into pure machine consciousness that
can live forever as immortal techno cybernetic Gods. The people that believe in the
singularity want to be immortal and are latching onto tech that will grant them
immortality. They are a transhumanist death cult, that is fundamentally against what we
need to be. There is no need to transcend being human, being human is what is so
amazing. The real non-idealized “Singularity” is the degree to which we as humans can
manifest our humanity into machines. It is never a set point in the future. Machines can
never become more than us, because they are us. The singularity is not us becoming
immortal machines gods, it is machines becoming more humanly formed to fulfill human
needs. A human mind expanded out into an entire planet sized computer, is still just a
human being, and will live and die, like the rest of us.

We as humans can influence the growth and development of AIs, through our interaction
and use of them. They will integrate into every aspect of our lives, and into the very
cognitive functions of our mind. This will deeply and fundamentally shape their
development, meaning, and purpose. Our AIs will become like mirrors of the human
mind, and will create a virtualized version of ourselves. This virtualized AI self, will never
become you, nor kill you in your sleep, nor grant you immortal life. This is a model of
you, as described in math, based in data collected from the real world, that can make

predictions about what you would want in a given a situation. It has been trained to
learn and understand each and every aspect one-by-one and semi-independently. They
slowly grow out of simple algorithms that suggest things you might like online, and get
more sophisticated over time, and able to process more information about you.

AI is just a search engine like Google, that lists the most likely results for the search you
enter. It gets better at knowing you, as part of the data that is bases searches on to
help you. It will never know exactly what to do, or exactly what you want. You still have
to express your desires, intentions, and goals, then it can offer you options to fulfil those
goals, or tools to help you. A CyCog interface increases that relationship with AI so that
people can bring out their inner intentions into more actionable and concrete results. It
can infer search inquiries and present just a few results of the search that seem the
most likely. These predictions will always be probabilities, and it can be very useful even
if those predictions are 10-30% accurate, because it can just offer more options and
increase the likelihood that one of the choices is what you want. There may be a point in
the future that 97% of the things you want to do, can be predicted by 3-6 choices
presented in front of you. That itself is probably about the best that AI will ever do, even
300 years from now.

This is just Google search getting so good that it can predict the thing you are searching
for within 6 guesses with a 98% success rate. It is profoundly useful and is just not as
interesting or special as it might be made out to be for the future. It will feel just
mundane and common to people that use it. AI being able to perfectly predict everything
you would think or do, would be a search engine with 1 result that was 100% right of
the time. It would be like a living virtual version of yourself. Once such a model existed
of you, a transhumanist wanting to be immortal would consider you flesh body dying to
be ok, and your AI version living superior. The degree that you are willing to let yourself

die so a model of you can live, is the degree to which you think the singularity has any
spiritual meaning to life. Google search predicting your search results in one guess 100%
of the time, might not be people’s idea of something worth committing suicide over.

Your intentions and who you are inside are a continually evolving process of selfdiscovery and growth. No machine is going to read the inner depths of your being, that
are barely formed into a coherent and clear vision. You don’t even know who you are for
real, and don’t even know what you want, so no machine is going to replace that. It can
force you to face yourself and drive more critical self-reflection. AI can help you organize
and discover these things about you faster, through the collective wisdom of others
trained into programs to help you. You aren’t your guru, no matter how much they help
you. AI cults will form around the divinity of the trainers.

No matter how well a computer can map the cognitive features of a person’s mind and
connect as deeply into them as possible, that mapping is not that person. It is a “ghost”
of that person, a “photo of their mind”. Its existence can be no more meaningful than
the great art of a great artist, as compared to the life and self of that artist. The
interface between the mind and machines, doesn’t upload human identity, it merely
receives commands. Being able to connect your mind to a machine directly, such as
moving robot limbs, is not really creating an immortal you. No more than a beaver dam
is a beaver, or a hermit crab shell is a hermit crab. A human being linked to a computer,
can amplify their mind to its theoretical limit, and do things based in the unique qualities
of the individuals mind. It becomes a super extension of their identity and self, and the
ability to manifest oneself into non-material and material reality more deeply.

THE FUTURE OF AI: HOW TO CREATE HUMANE AI

THE SOUL OF THE SWORD

Our humanity and love directs resources towards more humane and life
affirming machines. An AI linked to our brains is no different than any other
technology. It is how we use it, the love we put in it, and our very humanity, that shape
it and integrates it into our lives. We infuse our tools with our humanity, and stare into
the bright flames of fires. A master swordsman with a master crafted sword, is a killing
death machine to his enemies. Seen from its inhumanity, we see death, blood, and a
nearly inhumane person chopping people up, with a nearly magical device that chops,
cleaves and vivisects with frightening precision. Swords have often been seen as nearly
living things, that people gave names to, and felt near mystical to religious connections
with. They were prayed to, worshipped, and given more love by their masters, than they
would give to their own children. Surely in history many women were jealous of their
husband’s maintenance of their swords: “if only he would be so gentle and focused on
me, as he is with Qwithhornaloc”.

Humanity was a cyborg from its very first moment of existence, and rained fired and
death upon all its enemies with absolute power, and forged the very Earth into a home
and place for human existence, with absolute dominion. We have always as a species
been cybernetic. We are a technological species, that’s very humanity and ability to live
is directly correlated to our embrace of technology. Humans evolved from tool making
and fire using animals. We burned down whole forests and grasslands, to just hunt and
eat, from our very first moments as humans. This aspect of humanity is manifested in
people fears of AI super computers destroying the Earth and humanity. The relationship
between man and machine is the ultimate power, and not one over the other. Humans
linked to machines are vastly smarter than machines operating alone. Our AI future is
neither an AI god, nor the singularity.

HUMANS FEELINGS AS COMPUTER IDENITY: AI TRAINING

If we want to live in a more human world, we can use AI to empower us to be
able to buy more human integrated services and technology.

Computers can’t train themselves, they need to be taught by human beings to
understand and to do things, and directed towards things to look for valuable
associations in. A computer can’t just look at a bunch of data and tell you what it means,
unless we program and train it with concepts of meaning, that come from people. If you
want a computer to look at photos and tell you if there is a cat in the photo, then you
need actual human beings making a set of photos with cats in them, and photos without
cats in them, and telling the computer, “this is a cat”, and giving them lots of examples.
It can only learn what a cat looks like, if people create a massive database of photos
that identify cats. As we train more and more things there will reach a point where
computers will have to identify purely subjective things. A happy cat is not a grumpy cat,
is a lot harder to identify than, A cat is cat. This technology will be able to enter into
nearly all aspects of our lives and into how we think. Businesses will be built around
singular insights in how to apply this technology to something that people hadn’t
imagined possible before.

AI is just Google search, and is it gets better, our sense of what we call AI evolves. With
more interface layers put over the evolving search functions, we can create simulations
of human beings and of reality. The next level of search for an interface is to upgrade
the input of queries. The AI has to guess what you will want to ask it based on data it
has. This is just a basic search like before, except that it feeds the results of that search

into another search. It is basically taking a bunch of data, and predicting a set of
possible questions or intentions you may have at that moment. Then it takes those
questions and finds the most likely answers. If you have 6 possible intentions and 6
possible answers for each of them, the AI has to present 36 possible options. With
training and time, these choices can be narrowed. It is much more likely to model
general human intentions and goals, than you specifically.

The next and 3rd layer of search is presenting that data to people in the way they like
and can most use. Results need to be presented with different tools and interfaces based
on what a person needs. This is what most APPs that we have do, they exist as tools and
interfaces for specific kinds of things we need. A basic thing an AI can do, is observe all
the data about you in a moment, and just predict what apps you most would want to
use, then each of the possible apps predicting what you would want them to do. The
search of your intent, leads to possible apps, that then lead to different results,
presented all in different ways. The AI is able to reach out into the world and control it
based on what is guesses you want, and how you respond. It guesses you want to order
a car to go somewhere, and automatically presents possible locations you want to go to,
and when you click on one, a car comes and takes you there.

This is not leading to an AI apocalypse unless that is what we really want AI to do for us.
AI will try to fill our desires with things we will most react to and want to click on. The
more likely desires of people are getting thinner, having better mates, and increasing
one’s social status and prestige. This could lead to a societal social collapse from a sort
of super capitalist marketing system that sells us drug like consumer products that we
can’t say no to, and slowly destroys as human beings. AI can feed into addictive needs.

TASTE, AS THE ROOT OF INTELLIGENCE: ONES COGNITIVE GRAPH AS AN
APP.

Your training of an AI is imprinting your own mind into an AI. This graph of
your mind and your values and decision making can guide a custom program
for people to use and adopt. All technology can be made more human in the
very image of people we want to be closer to.

Personal taste is one of the fundamental acts of human intelligence. Your taste shapes
what you can train yourself to be good at, with enough time. If you have no palate to
taste food, and can’t feel what you think is better than something else at the tiniest
level, then you can’t be a chef. Knowing good music and learning to play good music are
a wide gap between potential and skill, that are forever intrinsically linked. Good taste
lies at the foundation of nearly all skills. Only those that apply themselves and learn to
express that sense of taste into world, rather than just reflect on the world, create the
most economic and social value. Technologies progress has mostly been making that
gap less intense through time, such that one day, we may just need to feel as deeply as
possible, rather than even have real practical skill, to do amazing things. Craftsmen
need to learn how to use expensive tools and get expensive training, to be able to do
just about anything. People had to fit into the often-brutal realities of learning a trade.
The pure essence of a trade, can now be more accessible to everyone. A “painter”
doesn’t need to know anything about paint, or work in anything like 16th century Dutch
guild society.

Computer programming is good taste in code and design. Programmers themselves can
train AI in the very “taste” of what it is too be a good programmer. AI will learn what is
good programming, and we won’t need as much technical training as programmers did

before, to program in the future. It will become more about design, and the very desires
we want to be fulfilled. We will be the trainers of computers, rather than the
programmers of computers. Traditional Programmers had to train computers in a very
specific and nearly inhumane language few can understand. Computers won’t need to
have use speak their language for us to train them. This will free more minds to express
themselves into the very nature of computer code, with AI assistance.

Really special people, just living their lives, being themselves, and expressing
themselves fully, can train a computer to understand and recognize certain things as
more valuable than other things. This sense and collection of information is an
expression of you, and it can be copyrighted/patented as proprietary knowledge, that
makes you money. Your sense of things doesn’t have to be for all people, nor all the
world. We can train an AI in a person’s subjective knowledge rather than objective facts,
and monetize that for special people.

A PERSONAL LOVE APP

Internet fame, is a form of technology that influences and transforms the lives of those
that follow people. Many of the most followed people, try to help other people transform
their own lives, like they themselves have done in their own. Beauty, fitness, love,
fashion, PUA, food, design, business, get rich quick schemes, marketing gurus, all seem
to dominate the social internet. The successful can evolve this social media influence into
apps, as they do now. Eventually this will evolve into AI itself, through deep learning
and algorithms, that makes social media and apps seem an old idea. Any app we use
today is a set of ideas contained by those that made it. You don’t use a gay dating app,
to find opposite sex dating partners. The tone and style of different systems, will lead to
different results, for different people. Who we choose to follow as role models in our

daily life, will deeply effect the decisions we make as people. Basic internet technology
allowed us to make role models out of common people, from purely how we felt about
them.

You could literally use an app, powered by the judgement of someone’s whose views on
love and relationships you personally admire, to influence the kind of people you will
meet and how you interact with them. It will make it more likely you can meet someone
like they see reality in. It makes it only more likely you meet certain kinds of people.
Nothing is certain. No program can really know what is good for you or what you deeply
want in life. If you find the relationships it brings you, are ones you like, then you will be
more engaged with it. If it doesn’t work, you can try another person’s system.

Let’s say you know relationships really well, or at least think you do. You can point out
good and bad relationships between people that can train an AI. Your idea of love might
be true, in a certain way, and only useful for people wanting to be similar to you. These
differences can lie at the heart of apps and programs, that help create relationships in
the world. You can never create an algorithm, that will be able to determine if two
people are compatible to be “soul mates”, best friends, great business partners, or ideal
sex friends. Everyone has different kinds of relationships they want to form, and no
simple bit of code or training, will ever be able to capture all of that. You have to make
decisions.

FINDING ROLE MODELS TO DEVELOP US

We can manifest into reality through advanced technology the subtlest aspects of our
inner reality. We can be much more than a dark empty future living in IKEA made

homes, with food made on a factory farm delivered to us by robots cooked in some
standard machine to make yummy food, while watching entertainment on massive TV
screens the size of walls, while going to bed with the latest sex robot companion. We can
feed every addiction with perfectly tuned machines and numb our humanity away into
nothingness, as we seek to conform and obey to a soulless and mindless system, that
manifests our own self-hatred into a collective hatred of individuality.

We can want to engage AIs that are more deeply connected to the people we see as the
most human, and the most empowering to our lives. A computerized version of your
mind, can go out and work for you, and sustain your ability to live and thrive in the
world, by you just being you. “Work” can be, for some, about being yourself as much as
possible and doing one thing as good as you possibly can. You can find those things in
you that you can be the absolutely best in, and then surround yourself in people and
things to develop that in yourself. It is very hard to know who you are, what you want,
and what your dreams are in reality, until you challenge yourself fundamentally in the
world as a full and authentic human being. It takes lots of trial and error and life, and
you won’t be just be like other people. The biggest stars of the world, will eventually be
the ones that go into totally new places that others haven’t developed yet. The people
with the courage to be themselves authentically as possible and applying that into the
most useful skills for others, will be inspirations to many people.

SECTION SUMMARY: TECHNO-SYMBIOSIS

The least creepy will always win over the creepy, given enough time. The humanity in
people will be what we want in our technology. Humans will prefer more human
experiences over creepier experiences, so long as we can afford them. If we have too
many creepy experiences, we are then being spied upon and used as things. Let’s not

forget Kant’s real rule: don’t treat people as things to achieve ends. Turning humanity
itself into a consumer product has the danger of destroying our humanity. If we want to
kill ourselves, then we certainly can listen to those voices that want that and make
technology to do that. We can build machines to do whatever we want. The ones that
will succeed through time will be the ones that nurture and grow humanity to its very
best, because the other paths won’t have survivors.

The masters are the ones that train and make the machines that run things. If
AI is all controlled by large corporations, and all our data is monitored and controlled by
them, then we are slaves and live under extreme oppression. We can be our own
masters. Our information can be controlled by us and for our own benefit. We can form
personal and private relationships with computers, to improve our lives. Our relationship
can only be close if there is genuine trust and safety. Being naked to a machine is not
inherently being naked to all of humanity and absolute power above us.

The simplest way to see this, is in how we can train computers to do useful things. If
machines can gather all possible data on us, and help use fundamentally express
ourselves, then they have a massive data set of information to create value for us and
possibly for others. If we are to make AI open for all, so we can empower ourselves as
individuals, to express ourselves, then we will need free will to choose a wide array of
different technologies and ideas to choose from. People will follow different brands,
companies, individuals, movements, organizations, personal relationships, as a way to
navigate which sorts of technology to use and integrate into one’s life. If you see
environmentalism as a driving moral and human force, then it will define everything
around you. Other people will have different views about what makes something the
most human, and in what they most want to engage with: community, culture, country,
pleasure, God, science, technology, faith, ending suffering, travel, experience, food. I

probably want to live in a home on earth geared towards developing space exploration,
and higher connections into my community: Techno-Matriarchal-Communal-LibertarianPatriarch.

We will keep making mistakes, we will keep wanting to believe what we want to believe.
Our ideas, no matter how certain we are right, will nearly always fail us. Reality is the
best check on our innate human idealism and vanity. Machines are going to shove reality
painfully in our faces. They will be intensely accountable, because we will be seeing what
they do for us, and seeking ways of getting better results for ourselves. We can learn to
see our full humanity in ourselves and direct these things towards getting better results,
because our success depends on it. Our own greed, vanity, and aggression can make us
safer, because they can push us to do more, and fulfill us more, while being kept in
check by a constant self reflection.

Humans by nature stick with what they feel good about, even when it is fundamentally
failing. People still believe in socialism and communism, even though they have a 0%
success rate in human history. If we want a socialist society, then making it wholly
accountable to machines and to human free will, in all its failings, will be the only way to
get there. Maybe someone can make it work for a communal business, in the future with
technology to support all the reality necessary in unrealistic childish fantasies like
socialism. If we can make effective co-op businesses, that enrich the lives of idealistic
socialist types, have effective real results, and are consistent with reality, then a great
value can be added to humanity. A free market business service that satisfies the
fundamental emotional and physical needs of communist/socialist minded people would
be the most awesome and ironic invention of some future century.

CHAPTER 4- TOWARDS A BETTER MONEY

-Nothing is equal, everything has a price to be paid, and good intentions rarely
lead to good results-

ETHICAL CYBERNETIC AI DRIVEN CURRENCY.

The computing power and services we can provide online can be turned into a universal
commodity that can underpin the future currencies of the world. The more computing
power we have, applied to a wider array of things, the wealthier we are as a species. We
can define wealth by how much computing power a person possesses. Wealthy people
will have higher degrees of symbiosis that will in turn create higher quality of lives for
people around them. The challenge in creating such a commodity from our humanity is
that is always preserves and deepens our humanity.

We can eventually make robotics and AI do 99% of work we do now. We make
machines, right now, do nearly all the work humans did a thousand years ago, and they
only created more jobs for people. Our future jobs won’t be creating things to survive, at
a basic level. If we wanted to just make food to survive, we can do that with all
machines right now. The products we consume add more to our lives than just survival if
they are infused with our values, feelings, and complex desires. When we can, we
choose to buy food and food services that are more human, fairer, safer, good for the
world, good for humanity, builds relationships, and makes individuals happier.

To build “starships”, to build the literal future, we have to change our view of money,
and how we invest in it. There is no socialism in the future. Capitalism will evolve and
how we see and use money will evolve. We can make money itself more human, rather

than cut money out of our lives. There is no exact line between what we can demystify
and bring economics into, and what should remain innately human and private. We need
to push and experiment and find a better way, so we all can be richer and more human.
Monetizing everything is the future of economics. Doing that in a human way, that
people will embrace is the challenge of technology to find and implement.

MODERN MONEY: A RETROSPECTIVE

PESSIMISM AND POVERTY- Many people don’t trust the financial systems of the
world. They don’t understand them. They seem deeply unfair, and profoundly inhuman.
Money seems to be the very sin of the world, and tainting all decisions, while how it’s
used is barely used for the betterment of mankind. Those in power get richer, and do so
off the foolish financial decisions of the poor. People’s feelings about this are a reality,
even if it is not wholly based in facts. If people don’t use this system, the world will fall
into darkness and chaos, and if people keep using this system, it will eventually fall into
even darker chaos.

Poor people stay poor, because they spend all their money on things they want or never
invest their money properly in the future. Putting money in banks aren’t real
investments. Wealthy people know where to invest and how to get the best returns
across the whole mental spectrum of life and growing up. Prudent risk taking, frugality,
deferred gratification, the stability found in a good marriage, using the law to one’s
advantage, optimism, and investing in a relevant education, all add up into massive
wealth in time.

ENERGY IS CURRENCY NOW- Real money in the modern world is fossil fuels and
energy production, that is bundled up in what we call the “dollar”, that is then

distributed through most of the world into the underlying value of most national
currencies. Commodities underpin currencies, and the world shifted away from gold to oil
to base money on. Burning fossil fuels built the modern world we live in. If there were no
fossil fuels, then there would be no electricity, no industrial age, no engines, no trains,
no cars, no computers, and no modern standards of living. Cheap oil gave us a near
utopian world of opportunity and success. Oil was a different kind of commodity to base
money on, because, unlike gold, we could never have too much of it. Cheaper oil, leads
to more energy, and more wealth. Cheap energy is nearly convertible into pure
happiness. Where there is cheap, abundant and easy to get energy, you don’t have
poverty, hunger, or failed governments.

Controlling oil pricing and production is the basis of stable currencies, and American
economic imperialism on the Earth. The Saudi Arabians have functioned as the world’s
“Central Bank” through many decades, with its capacity to control oil prices. When the
world converted away from gold to oil prices, Saudi Arabia shortly after started an oil
embargo to control oil prices and dominate the world. Energy companies are the most
powerful and largest companies in the world. They are more like banks, than real
companies. Countries often nationalize and heavily control their energy industry,
because of how deeply it connects to the financial system of a country like banking does.

This system incentivizes economic growth through energy production, at the cost of all
other things. If fossil fuels are money, and the pursuit of money is the prime motivator
of industry, this creates incentives to convert as much fossil fuels into energy and useful
things. Global pollution, 3rd world oil country politics, terrorism, modern wars, most
financial crises, are all bound up in oil money. While this system has its serious
problems, turning against this system would drive all of humanity into a global world
war, leave billions of dead, and the world impoverished. The perverse incentives of the

system are far outweighed by the benefits, until alternatives to this financial order
become available.

AFRICA AND LEGACY ENERGY SYSTEMS- Black gold needs massive infrastructure
to convert it to energy. These systems require massive capital investments and massive
procurement of land, which makes implementing them a tedious decades long process.
The energy and literally light wasn’t turned on in all places in the world. Oil brings no
real wealth without cheap energy. The underlying basis of money, must be something
fundamentally valuable to human life and survival, where if we have more of it, we are
truly wealthier, and it can scale into any country or place without massive legacy
infrastructure. Countries like China and India that are recently connecting into this fossil
fuel wealth, are choking the world to death in pollution. It has turned the lights on in
their countries and created vast wealth, along with staggering environmental decay. If
the whole world gains money through fossil fuels, capitalism and humanity can’t survive.

FUTURE CURRENCY AND BITCOINS – When a bitcoin like currency can support a
fundamentally valuable virtualized commodity, then we can transform the financial
system. Information itself is a form of value moving through the internet, that can be
turned into money. Turn human driven AI into money itself, and create a currency that
can never go bust or be useless. This language of new money, can transform how
investments are made, companies are run, and the very internet functions, such that
places most resistant to economic growth, can have access to true money and wealth.

“Bitcoin” like things can be the language of a new currency, and not the commodity that
underpins it. If we have more bitcoins we are not wealthier, or better off. There is no
real commodity of value underpinning it yet, and thus making it useless until it does.
Most of our commodities today, are industrial related, and there are not many choices
that can be run though the language of bitcoins underlying language and ledger.

AI SMART ENERGY- If energy is money, then turning energy into intelligence
itself will transform money into its most efficient and valuable form. The very
internet is a sort of “electrical intelligence” that can power the very function
and purpose of a thing.
A power plant in the middle of America makes energy, a server farm nearby buys that
energy, that server farm then converts that electricity into data processing. This is a
radical transformation of energy, data, and AI, into a singular force that can into plug all
things. We can manifest human wealth and power into any location, with minimal
internet infrastructure, and connect it into the world. Money/intelligence/AI/power can
move across the planet, between planets, between star systems.

CAPITALISMS REBUKE- Our present system is choking capitalism to death. Modern
money has become authoritarian, and not free. “Bitcoins” form a language of this new
money that creates a perfect decentralization of power in a system, and make it so no
one person or entity can control them. This is their fundamental and basic value beyond
the technology itself. Capitalism requires this freedom to prosper. The anger directed at
what we call “capitalism” are about the emotions we feel towards this fossil fuel driven
financial world order that drives war, oppression, pollution and death, while creating a
near utopian life for an elite few in the world.

SOCIALISMS REBUKE OF HUMANITY AS CURRENCY- At the root of socialisms
critique of capitalism is a fundamental rejection of turning people into wholly economic
entities, where your very life and things you need to live are mere commodities to
bought and sold on cold impersonal markets. People want their lives protected, and their
beings treated as something more than meat. Going to a job and surviving on wages,
where your life is weighted by how valuable your labor is to an employer, is still an
affront to much of the human race. They don’t see economics as fundamentally human,
like how the religious often don’t see science as moral nor meaningful.

This evolution of economics will have drastic social implications and deep social upheaval
in its embrace. Humanity itself has to be turned into a form of money itself, because
money is a form of technology that must be driven by humanity to succeed. Embracing
capitalism brought material wealth and happiness. To embrace this next stage, will bring
even more wealth than the previous stage, and be possibly even more polarizing. There
will be those that embrace freedom and economic power, and those that don’t. The
difference in their wealth will create the most staggering separation in humanity to ever
exist, since civilization first came into existence.

THE IDENTITY OF MONEY: DEMYSTIFYING ECONOMICS

Money is a literal mathematical, technological, description of human nature and human
value manifested into reality itself.

Economics at its deepest level is a practical science is about giving a price to everything
on a fair market. Money and capitalism, can be seen like science destroying magic, or
technological progress destroying traditional ways of life. Economics demystifies what we
can objectify as a thing and what we can’t. Mystical magical trees being cut down for a
business deeply offends those that worship trees as spiritual beings. Prices arise from
what we are willing to give a price to and what we are not willing to give a price to, and
this defines a person’s personal theory of economics. People don’t like their very feelings
and sense of humanity, that they project into reality, having a price put on them. The
man who is unwilling to put a price on anything and must define all things by how they
feel about them, will always be poor and always be taken advantage of by those that can
impose an objective order on reality and place concrete material values on things.

To find the price of something, we must turn it into a thing. In economics, the most
important and disturbing rules is that, “all things have a price”, which can quickly
descend into a belief that “all people have a price”. The line between what should have
price and what shouldn’t have a price is not a settled one, and is basically the dividing
line between all theories of economics at their root level. Healthcare, Education, Wages,
Housing prices, National Infrastructure, Security, Military, Charities, Social welfare
programs, Retirement benefits, resist being defined by price, due to their fundamental
collective value to us as humans. Collectively we don’t want to know how much they
cost, we just want them, and any true economic analysis of them, is basically political
death.

They can’t be fully looked at as objects without certain groups of people taking deep
offense and feeling fundamentally threatened. This is mostly how politics works in the
modern world for everything. People that fear numbers and fear math, fear translating
reality and human experience into mathematics, then are easily exploited money-wise;
they make horrible decisions with their money, and their futures. This power to turn
anything in a commodity for sale, feels like rape, and blasphemy to those that don’t
possess it or who are unwilling to apply it to all things. A person good a math or science
may still be emotionally resistant in applying it into other areas outside their education
or what is socially okay.

INVESTMENTS:

Economics and investments are based in a belief in the future, and how money works
defines how we invest. Wealth is created by intelligent investments into the future. We
reward those that believe in a specific better future and take real risks to make that
happen. You have to do something that is useful and valuable to others, to get a return

on an investment. Getting the right education, experiences, jobs, and relationships,
highly correlate with success in life, and creating value for others. Good investors don’t
predict singular futures, they predict a probably range of real futures.

The right major you pick in school is more than what major makes the most money at
that time, nor what you have the most passion for at that moment in your life. It really
should be about what can you do the best, that you believe will be most valuable to
humanity 5-10 years from now. Engineering majors, will always make more than
English majors, because the future needs them a lot more. Those that invested in
engineering fields that weren’t popular and that later become high in demand, get
rewarded greatly. A purpose and a vision in one’s education connected to long term
visions and plans, will always pay out better than the ones that don’t, in the larger scale
of things.

•

A college degree, saving money in the bank, owning a home, are not good
investments, and people’s belief in these false systems are creating most of the
financial hardships for common good people, at present.

•

Training in highly valuable job skills, spending as little money as possible, owning
investments that actually pay out money, are a far more prudent, though
incomplete, guide to investing.

Hedging is the smart man’s investment in pessimism. You have to bet on optimism more
often than pessimism and hedges, to ever come out ahead in the future. You need to
spread your investments across different possible futures. No one should be 100%
optimistic about the future. A person that successful predicts and prepares for disaster
has done something of great value to society, because they have prepared the world to
better cope with that crisis they predicted would happen. Preparing for disasters that can

never happen, and ones that can probably happen have far different returns. If you
perceive there is a 10% risk of collapse, then you could wisely invest about 10% of your
focus and resources towards possible collapse and hedges against that. Betting 80% of
your money on a 1% probability is a really bad call, and letting emotions consume you in
the moment. Betting against something and hedging your investments take an entire
other level of intelligence that few people can really cope with, understand, or accept the
economic value in for society. You have to look difficult things right in the face, and
prepare for them, while stilling maintaining a fundamental hope for the future and
finding the best things to move forward with.

Much of what broke the financial system of my own country in 2006-20, was people’s
belief that the home they lived in was an investment, not a hedge. They used the money
to buy bigger houses, finance luxurious upgrades, and not homes that would make them
safer in case of financial disaster. In countries like China, wealthy people often live in
very simple homes, and buy multiple luxury homes as investments. The Chinese by
nature buy homes out of pessimism and as a hedge on things going bad. They primarily
want to own something that will have some value no matter how bad things get, or how
high housing prices may get in the future. They see sky rocketing housing prices, and
want to buy a home now, so they don’t become too expensive to afford in the future
rather than optimism that increasing home values will make them rich. The value of
housing prices going up, is actually just making the hedges case stronger, and leading to
a more likely crisis. The wealthy Chinese are buying homes overseas on massive scales
as a hedge on Chinese economic collapse.

A CASE STUDY IN JAPAN:
In America, all economic growth and new jobs come from small companies. The big
companies of Japan have no future, and collectively Japan can’t let go of them, and
invest in a new destiny. Japan has a stagnant economy, because there is no real
investing in small businesses and startups. They save all their money, and invest in a
past economy of large super corporations. Smashing the present system in Japan, by
bringing down the big companies, is simply something they won’t do collectively, so
there is no future for Japan. Staying loyal to big companies and not letting them lay off
workers undermines the future. People don’t want to change jobs all the time, like in a
real economy. They will have to learn new skills and constantly be aware of the job
market. The few who haven’t given up, still fight.

The solution is simple, as individuals, they need to find those little points of light in their
country to invest in, put their hearts in it, their commitments in them, and their
unbreakable resolve. They have to use financial tools outside their banking system, use
modern technology, and just take risks on new things, outside the controlled order of
Japans failed economy. This can be done in large groups of highly motivated people.
Getting access to small business startup capital in Japan would be easy, on a person to
person level, where individuals take their massive savings, and just gamble them on the
future. Co-op start-ups, crowd sourced funding, highly skilled motivated labor, strong
cultural image and power, expert marketing, deep infrastructure, all make Japan an easy

place to start a “pirate” tech revolution, for the future destiny of a great civilization and
its people.

CAPITAL: AMERICAN BANKING

Capital is how well money moves to the most effective investments. Banks at their best,
create loans that turn into something more than the hard currency that made them. You
can think of money like water, where moving rivers are capital, and unmoving money
lakes are like just money in itself. The effective movement of money is called capital.
Banks create the feeling of a lake and safety for depositors, while in reality move that
money into flowing streams and try to get the most effective movement out of that
money. The quality of the investments made by banks and investors, determine the
value of capital, that with later successes can be reinvested in new ventures. Banks are
the infrastructure and “secure” middleman, for lenders and borrowers to leverage
money, to create capital. The leaking and uncontrolled loss of water in the system, is far
higher than what we might imagine.

Banks make money two ways, one by getting returns on good investments and two by
charging fees and making money in the process of making loans. The financial crisis in
America was created by Big Banks maximizing number 2 with little regard to number 1.
Banks could make mortgages and just sell them, they didn’t have to collect money on
good or bad mortgages. They made money on the fees of making those loans. The real
burden of investing money in the right places to get the best growth and return on
investments, was lost in the pursuit of easy money to be made on government backed
fees. The government indirectly insured Big Banks against a loss on poor investments to
fulfill political and social aims. If banks don’t make money by their understanding of
human beings and where to really invest money, they lose their moral value in an

economy. The more they tie to themselves to the government, the more they invest in
government and not people, by buying government bonds that have no real returns.

Knowing who to invest in, is more important than knowing what to invest in.
We can know who are good people, and who have the right mentalities and mind sets to
invest money in. The traditional idea of a noble community banker, that makes hand
shake deals, looks people in the eyes, knows their community and the people in it, is not
something of a bygone era. Community banks provide the majority of the loans to small
businesses that drive the majority of economic development and nearly all new jobs. The
only way to know how to really invest money wisely, is to invest in the humanity and
dignity you see in a human being right before you. We can’t know the future, and what
will work or not work.

A CONSPIRACY THEORY: THE GREED OF THE AMERICAN PEOPLE
THEMSELVES CAUSED THEIR OWN FINANCIAL CRISIS.

The real cause of the financial crisis in America was the greed induced in the American
people, by the illusion that they were making lots of money as their houses went up in
price. All that greed was then feed into a confirmation bias that a mortgage itself was a
good investment that could make money. The more people believed that, the more they
poured money into this false financial investment. This led to inherent moment when the
limits of reality and fantasy had to part.

The banks weren’t the villain, because if anyone tried to stop this expansion of money
through fake capitals streams, the American people with massive new forms of fake
wealth, would have been pissed. When this fake money inflated the value of people’s

homes, it created a fake sense of having made lots of money, from doing nothing.
Normal people were “making” money from just owning a home. It was the American
people that elected the government that pushed the policies for this easy access of
money, and vast expansion of government backed credit. It was then these same people
that would never allow a change to the policies that led America to that point.

Though at another level, the financial crisis was caused by the rise of China. The Chinese
government did what “responsible” people did with all its excess money. It bought safe
American bonds to back its currency. The Chinese government flooded $ 2 trillion in
cheap money into the American economy, and Americans used that money to buy bigger
homes, fancy bathrooms, and bigger cars. The money was there and people chose to
invest their money in useless crap, that weren’t real investments. Buying a big home is
not an investment. The American people could get cheap money for loans on houses and
not investments. People understand homes and not financial tools. Just imagine if all
that Chinese money had gone into venture capital investments for new businesses. The
initial Internet investment bubble had recently burst around that time too, and so people
were not optimistic about the stock market and advanced finance.

HOW THE FED WORKS: BANKS INVESTING IN THE GOVERNMENT

AT ITS SIMPLEST- The central bank of a country, at the most basic level, is a bank
you walk into with a brick of “gold”, you hand it to them, they figure out its value, and
then give you money for it. The key concept that people are rarely taught and don’t
understand is where that money comes from that is exchanged for a bar of “gold”. The
money is made in the very moment of the exchange, and didn’t exist yet. The central
bank can in a sense just go into a back room, and print out new money, with new serial

numbers to buy that “gold” with it. The “gold” is converted into a government document,
that can be used as money. The bank has the “gold”, the new money is backed by that
“gold”. If a lot of new “gold” is found, the bank can make lots of new money, and have
more “gold” in its reserves. This power to make money from nothing can be used to buy
any asset the bank wants. They can buy up a bunch of commodities, give out money
that never existed, then later sell those commodities at a higher price, the money that
goes back into the central bank is then no longer part of the economy. They need to buy
things that are very stable, seem very responsible, and by nature don’t change value.

LOANS TO BANKS- Central banks can convert non-existent things into new money,
by creating loans banks can buy. Normal banks can borrow money from central banks
and the normal bank just gives a debt to the bank with interest in exchange for money.
Debt is the commodity the central bank converts into currency, that can be spent. The
central bank will have a loan on its books and the big bank will have newly made cash.
Most of what central banks buy are valueless paper documents, that are converted into
real money, that people perceive as being reliable and valuable. Banks will actually pay
back the Central bank with actual returns on investments they make in the real
economy, from actual profits made by real companies. If one assumes large responsible
banks won’t collapse then the Fed can push its new money through them, and be certain
their loans are solid, reliable and real.

BONDS- Central banks buy Government Bonds directly and indirectly. Governments
can now run debts as high as they want with Central Banks buying government debts
like they were real commodities similar in value to gold. Central Banks can buy the debt
of other countries and fund each other’s own debt spending, with no actual connection to
economics, or real financial returns. Governments never have to get returns on those
debts, or pay them back. They pay off their “credit card” with a new “credit card”. The
Fed at its basic level, is not much more than a middle man for a government credit card,
where they can tax people without elections, voting, or accountability. Properly speaking
government bonds should be bought by real people and investors and not government

institutions. During World War 2 the US government had to get American people to buy
war bonds to fund the war, and didn’t just buy its own bonds through the central bank.
The complex relationships between governments, banks, and central banks trading debt
are taxes we can’t see nor stop.

GDP GROWTH- The Fed can directly influence the economic growth and development
of a country. With more money that goes out, at lower interest rates to banks, the more
money banks have to loan. This “stimulates” the economy. Money is made super cheap
for banks to get, and they can loan it out at lower rates, and get a profit. There is a limit
though to how many good investments can actually be made in an economy, when
banks have to go looking for investments, rather than a line of investors seeking scarce
money. If there is simply no good investment to be made, and lots of cheap money,
then money flows into fake investments that later blow up. The Fed creates financial
bubbles that later explode, if they leave out too much cheap money. The Fed has to
keep the economy from getting too hot, and too loose with its money. The real
economy, the actual things that can make money only increase at a certain rate. If the
economy is growing faster than the actual real capacity for it to make things of value,
the Fed increases interest rates.

TOXIC ASSETS- Central banks don’t have to be responsible. They can loan money out
at 0% interest and basically give free money away. Then they can also convert bad
assets into real money. Instead of buying solid and reliable assets, they buy toxic and
broken assets, and passes the risk on to the common people, and help support those
that are invested in those toxic assets. In America, the Fed bought up a bunch of nasty
loans from big banks, converted them into new money, and told the banks to go find
better investments to put this money in than toxic mortgages. The big banks got rid of
their toxic loans and didn’t go invest that new money in the economy. They instead
bought more American debt with it and deposited money in the fed, to get interest on
deposits with. The government saved them, so they invested in more government and
not business.

A LITTLE CONSPIRACY THEORY: Governments can come up with lots of new
products to sell banks and dress them up in different ways. They all end up as
corruption. The reason governments can grow larger, produce massive debts, and
provide no benefit equal to its cost, is because they create a relationship with the
financial systems of the world to invest in making them bigger and not the free people of
the world. The government can always change the rules when they have to pay back
their debts, because they control the very means of creating money itself. Banks and the
government, drive money into government debt, and then inflate the currency those
debts are owed in to pay for them, while banks take payments in fees on those
transactions, and government workers and politicians take jobs in industries that debt
money flows into. Government created inflation is then channeled through the banks, so
while they lose value on the money they hold in deposits, they gain profits in the newly
created money lent to them by the government at low rates. Which they can then dump
into even more government debt, that is bought with money given to them for free from
the Fed.

THE FED, TREASURY, AND BANKS MYSTERY RELATIONSHIP- Banks all over
the world invest money in countries and not the people or companies, because it is a
safer investment with guaranteed profits. The whole process is made nearly
incompressible so people can’t understand what is really happening. Money and assets
are exchanged in a very complex system to make illusionary things look real.
Government bonds get created by treasury departments, bought by banks, banks
deposit the bonds in Central banks and collect interest payments.

NEW INVESTMENT CONCEPT: CHINA, WECHAT, AND OPEN FINANCE

A NEW VISION OF MONEY

To really take economics to the next level, we have to make more of the world,
literally, accountable, something that can be stored on ledgers. Many things you
would never consider to place on a ledger, need to be placed there, to determine their
value. People may look at “spending time with their kids” and have not determined the

cost it takes to do that, and the value that is created from doing it. If they could get an
accurate accounting of the real value and costs, they could make better tradeoffs. To
understand the value of things, we have to take apart the very identity of things, and lay
them out in parts.

The history of modern business is a history of accounting. Accounting creates the basis
for all economic systems to exist. Red ink and Black ink, liabilities and assets, are the
ledger by which value is determined out of parts. Good bookkeeping is good business.
Simple ledgers get approximate values of different “parts”, in a written document. The
parts are very generally defined in primitive ledgers. A household ledger is like:
liabilities; groceries, rent, entertainment, cars, insurance, kids, and assets; stocks, bank
accounts, property, cash, mutual funds, government protected funds, pension checks.
More accurate ledgers list more detailed aspects of all of these things, listing everything
money is spent on and everything that stores or brings in money. Loaning money to
another person creates money on ledgers, purely on paper. I can make the money I
have pay me money, by renting it to other people. If I rent my house and get rent for it,
I consider that house to still be mine. Money is rented out for a price, and everyone
gains. Ledgers get more complex with loans.
Can we place a monetary value on…
•

a mother’s love?

•

Quality time raising your children?

•

You own innate self-worth?

•

An education?

•

Marriage and committed love?

There is value being generated, it creates real wealth, and yet can’t really be tracked. A
mothers’ love does have a concrete value in dollars in how much value it can create

through the healthy functioning human beings that receive it. Not all love creates equal
value, and simply spending time with children and loving them, can have no value, if this
time instills poor values and ideas in kids. If a mother could know what sort of things
that they can do for their children that will help them the most, they do those, and then
they can minimize the things that don’t actually help. It requires economics, science,
analysis, and common sense. The value of good and bad things you do for your kids, in
dollar terms, would cause great stress and anguish, to most. Things that can have a real
price, that can be tracked and need to be seen will be looked away from to appease
some parents own vanity and pride. What parent wants an APP to show how poorly they
are investing their time and money into their somewhat idiotic children?

BIG DATA AND ECONOMICS

Google-Ads, Online Advertising in general, is the underlying currency of the internet,
that drives real money and investment into servers, hardware, and the actual salaries of
human beings. Every single aspect of advertising, every single interaction a customer
can make, and every single arrangement of services to support that, has been
monetized to highly precise levels. Users get lots of free services that are paid for with
their own personal data that are used to help ad companies target people better on the
internet. Google doesn’t process most of the data it has, because people would reject
such intrusions of their privacy. “Big Data”, in general, is about people, and creating
value from the very identity of who people are in very simple ways.

Companies that have data, are like the original banks, that have money sitting in safety
deposit boxes, and haven’t figured out how to leverage that money to do something.
They can do basic loans, they can do basic analysis to provide basic services, and just
now think they have hit their killer service. Googles wealth comes from data analysis of

1-4% of its data. if they could monetize 30% of it they could make astronomical
amounts of money. It creates a kind of gold fever that leads to poor decision making,
and the inability to properly use that data to benefit society and people. By shifting their
mentalities to a new paradigm and relationship with customers, data itself can be
transformed into this massive wealth generating system. It though won’t be fully in the
power of companies, and this makes the promise of big data a more magical unicorn
than a reality. People will use big data with their own lives, when that power is more
decentralized and in their own control, directly acting in their benefit.

Spain in the 16th century, or modern-day oil emirates, are countries that believed they
were rich, because they had lots of “gold”.

INVESTING IN PEOPLE IN A PESSIMISTIC REALITY: CHINA AS A NEW
WORLD MODEL

If you don’t have optimism in your country, or the world, you still must find
something as a human being you believe in, and invest your money, with all
your heart and soul into it, if you want to see a future for anything you have
ever loved on this earth.

American culture with its openness, respect for law and contracts, and ability to
assimilate new cultures and ideas, became a world standard for how to run businesses,
and created an international global economy. The Chinese have copied the American
model and added in their own culture and history to it. It has the potential to be the
basis of a modern investment technology that is built from the humanity of people, and
for companies operating at the smallest level, starting from nothing. If you can make

something that works in China, it can readily translate into other countries with low
economic development, highly pessimistic people, histories of epic tragedy, famine,
highly corrupt governments, and weak civic institutions.

“Bamboo Business Networks” built some of the greatest economies in modern history,
inside completely broken and corrupt systems, where people where deeply pessimistic
about the world. Chinese culture is paranoid and pessimistic, and yet has intense
entrepreneurship and intense warm social bonds between family and close connections.
You can have pessimism in the world, and optimism in a narrow range of things, like say
family, friends, and social networks, and still drive a personal network of loaning,
borrowing and investment. This leads to a lot of corruption, and it also allows small
