businesses access to capital they could never get otherwise.

This business culture can create, in an idealized fashion, a business standard for
international finance and entrepreneurship, if we integrate high level technology that can
bypass the inherent internal corruption in traditional Chinese culture. By taking Chinese
traditional investment culture, and backing it up with computers, fraud analysis, machine
learning, apps, or whatever, then those personal relationships can be more freely
invested in, and reach out to a wider circle of connections. You would be much more
likely to loan money to a friend if you could monitor every single aspect of the business
they needed it for, and have guaranteed returns on your loan, if they make a profit.

For Americans, this would be like investing in a food truck, based on your belief in the
person doing the food truck and how you feel about the food. You can invest in a person
and a food you have a passion for. And this feeling can be backed up with actual data,
open book keeping, live cameras of the van inside, machine learning driven fraud

prevention, or whatever will be developed to make those personal investments more
secure, while still being based in our humanity and personal feelings.

WECHAT MONEY AND CHINESE INVESTMENTS.

In China, the largest and powerful app is WeChat. It is a social network, and messaging
platform, that has a financial service linked to it. WeChat is a huge success because it
connects into our humanity to drive its tech development. WeChat began its money
system with just transferring money between friends, moved into being able to find and
pay for dinners, movie tickets, concerts, donate to charity, and any other very human,
social, and connected thing they could.
•

You can deposit money from your bank account into a WeChat account.

•

With this money, you message your friend money, instantly in real time.

•

You can buy many things online with this account too.

•

You can also go into actual stores and pay for things from your mobile phone,
through your WeChat account.

•

Using WeChat wallet has a this very personal and profound feeling that comes
with it.
o

It is not like just using another payment system.

o

It feels very human, and makes using it much more appealing and
engaging, than can readily be described,
§

unless one has such an experience of using a socially driven virtual
online currency.

•

WeChat focuses on using its wallet to increase social interaction, and enrich your
personal life, and not just using it like a super bank card.

•

Most of the things that you can spend money on in its system are socially
connected, or amplify the quality of your life.

The money that is being moved around in the accounts, is not real money. All the money
is just deposited and controlled by WeChat. They have ledgers of where all the money
“should” be, though in reality, people just deposited money to WeChat, and WeChat
converted that money into its own currency, that can move around freely. If you want to
withdraw money from the system, into real cash bank accounts, then you pay a fee,
which is really a currency exchange fee. Money in the WeChat system, moves instantly
around, to where ever you want it. If you withdraw money, it happens much slower, and
is driven by more traditional financial systems, that it has to interact with.

WeChat can also allow small companies to create platforms, for people to invest money
in “venture capita”l. You can play venture capital investment games, with actual
businesses. You can play a Farmville, with actual farms, and not just in China, but in
other countries. Money can move freely, instantly, and socially. You can create apps,
that power investment portfolios, venture capital, mini-hedge funds, or you being a bank
yourself. Just forming on this platform, are tools of advanced finance that can be made
into smaller versions driven by high technology and virtual online currencies.

You can make more personal and human investments. Risks can be mitigated, by fraud
analysis, and real-time data and information on your investments. If you invest in a
batch of a fish-farms fish, you can monitor the farm, by live cameras and access to all
their financial data. These are all new things, and barely developed. Fraud will be
widespread in new virtualized banking systems, sadly, because no one really
understands them, and the real future they have, so bad people gain.

OPEN FINANCE: POWERING THE NEW BUSINESS OF THE FUTURE

“Open Finance” is to open up all the financial data, the complete ledger, in real time of a
company. Investors can do real time external audits and oversee fraud prevention
systems. If there was a “stock market” of companies that had open finance, this would
revolutionize how we invest money, and analyze companies. Companies that want
access to this modern open stock market, will need to use open financial systems and
other open systems from their very start. The systems of open finance must empower
companies that are just starting, by being cheapest, most powerful, and socially
connected platform, that then gives them easier access to financing because of how
open they are to potential investors. If a company from the beginning used such a
system, to lure in investment and create real verifiable trust, they could adopt an open
finance system more readily in their company DNA, and be a different kind of company
right at its founding.

Finance is one of the hardest things for new and small businesses. The most advanced
software won’t make it any easier, unless the very underlying way one does business
and uses money is transformed. Traditional finance and money, can never fully be
represented and tracked online to the necessary levels, as compared to a wholly
virtualized currency. When you move around real money, there are fees and costs
incurred, there is a friction created from the rules and the existing financial order. That
friction takes away a percentage of money at every exchange. Payroll costs money to
transfer money to staff, and uses actual HR staff to do it. By eliminating nearly all
internal cost of moving money around, value is created and smaller companies can now
afford to do things they couldn’t do before.

Everything you buy will also be bought and tracked in that currency, all online
purchasing, with no transaction fees, no credit card fees.

•

The items themselves that you bought will also be instantly inventoried and
tracked, with data.

•

A ledger won’t just be a simple object description with cost and quantity: 200
boxes of Acme Super Pens.

•

It can have machine readable data, that tracks many aspects of those objects
and connects them to a wide array of things. 1/10th of cent values can be
tracked.

•

All vendor, internal, and customer transactions, are done within this one system,
with open data.

It will lead them towards deeper human experience, and make even the finances of a
company a humanizing thing. This also can’t finance organized crime, terrorists, and
revolutions, because it requires openness, to get the money, and thus it would be very
easy for government to infiltrate and get that data, and know all the things a
“company”, was doing. This is oversight, beyond anything a government can do now,
and it is for reasons nobler, freer, and more humanizing. Having all your finances
watched for government ends or for your own ends, is two very different experiences;
one is voluntary, and the other is not.

PART 2: THE FALL OF
CIVILIZATIONZOMBIE WORLD

True unimaginable economic wealth can be made from unleashing the whole of
humanities potential.

We are already living in the apocalypse. Most of the worlds countries live in hell. Within
developed countries mass sections of society are disconnected from the future and any
hope of a better life. We are already dying. Civilization is at its greatest level ever, and
also has more people live in suffering than ever before. More humans today live in hell,
in a single country, then there were humans in the times of ancient empires. Functioning
civilization and society is a rare thing. How we build technology can shape how we
survive hard times when society falls apart. First world countries need their fundamental
systems to all be based in how to build up a society and system from nothing, like the
basic protocols of the internet and its entire architecture. When something can function
from the smallest size and grow outwards, this is how you build order from nothingness.
Decentralized systems, promote freedom and network efficiency, while creating a
framework to build civilization from nothing in any location.

Designing great technology at the highest levels, can be inspired from a vision of the
world dying from massive armies of the undead consuming and killing us. Our darkest
nightmares can be used to guide and create truly human and beautiful life affirming
technology, and connect us to the humanity of the world we are disconnected from. Our
fundamental humanity builds technology, and it is the basis of everything we value. We
are also the ugly “humanity” that exists in a fallen world without civilization or operating
social institution. It is that “humanity” that lies, cheats, steals and kills over nothing,
that we must embrace to fully prosper. We must never cut out this part of ourselves out
of ourselves and civilization, to prosper. We are the descendants of those that
slaughtered every inhuman and uncivilized person they could find. Our ideals of
humanity, and the reality of humanity are difficult to reconcile. Idealism literally and

actively kills people, to create the world of those ideals, and it is how peace has been
achieved through all of human existence.

We often try to help suffering groups, and nearly always fail, because we use the wrong
thinking and principles to help. In many ways imbedded in the very help and idealism to
help the less fortunate lies innate human desires to kill off the vulnerable and less able.
Only capitalism has ever helped people in the modern history of the world, with its
pursuit of individual success. People don’t need pity, they need investment, new
companies, new jobs, and a better future for their families and communities. African
development plans for much of history have been based on inhumane ideas, and have
largely failed on the most massive of scales.

In recent years, people that have been investing in Africa for business, have found
success. Chinese investments are helping Africa grow. The Chinese more fundamentally
understand the collapse of society and what it takes to rise up out of it. They lived
through their own apocalypse and endured some of the darkest horrors of the 20th
century. This gives China a deep competitive advantage over the West. A totalitarian
communist country uses primitive state capitalism to connect to and relate with Africa,
while capitalist “free countries” use socialism and communism, to relate to this region
and its peoples. One leads to prosperity and the other to perpetual darkness, genocide
and death.

Much of the development of the world’s economy, in the near future, will have to be in
some of the worst places on earth, that have been resistant to development and modern
business. As we develop the most underdeveloped places, we can release their latent
potential for wealth generation and prosperity. If done right, the worst places on earth,
provide the most opportunity for investments to get the highest returns. All development

in the modern world comes from cheap energy found in fossil fuels. This system is very
heavy and requires a lot of people and resources to run, and so can’t really solve the
deeper underlying problems of survival. This though can’t just be brought to Africa
anytime soon, not without a lot more development in these regions. We need something
that can be done with less initial resources and can scale readily with demand, that can
deliver wealth and freedom to a dark and lost continent of human beings, based on their
own humanity and dreams for themselves.

CHAPTER 5: JOSHUA’S GUIDE TO SURVIVING THE ZOMBIE
APOCALYPSE

Are you ready to commit genocide for your ideals?

The zombie apocalypse is the release of humanities will to commit genocide in the name
of preserving what people feel is human to them. To orient this to the future. Imagine a
better future, a distant future, and imagine the sorts of people in it, and who won’t be in
it. Your vision of that future, and your ideals, shape the groups you will form in the
present. The apocalypse is scary because people can be revealed as who they really are
on the inside. All the social norms that represses their identity can come raging out. If
you vision of the future doesn’t have certain groups of people in it, then in apocalypse
you will have no problem letting those people die nor killing them to survive.

QUESTIONS:
Consider yourself living in the Zombie apocalypse or any sort of end of the world
scenario.
•

What is your sense of humanity? What is your vision of the future? If you are a
black liberal single woman, would a conservative patriarchal Asian man be
acceptable as a husband? Would you value the lives of people you once hated in
the old broken world?

•

What sort of groups would you want to be recruited into, and what sort of groups
would you not want to be recruited into?
o

Would you enter a group that was a completely different race from you?
Culture? Class? Ethnicity? Sexual Orientation? Political affiliations?

Educational background? Religion? And if so which ones more than
others?
o

Would a French black gay liberal evolutionary biologist want to join a
group of all white conservative American Mormons? Should he convert to
the religion and marry a woman to be a member?

•

Does an ideal society, for you in the future, have……
o

Gays, Straights, Conservatives, Religion, Socialists, Atheists, Israelis,
Japanese, Russians, Chinese, Science, Technology, Capitalism, Money,
Banks, Roads, God, Terrorism, Crime, Murder, Hate, Failure, Ugly people,
Domestic animals to eat, Equality, or Inequality????

o

If it doesn’t have any of these things, then you are probably an extremist,
and your idealism will kill off whoever doesn’t fit your ideal vision of the
world.

•

Should you all dress similar, have rituals, speak similar, have standard protocols
for doing things, and be “patriotic”?

•

Is marriage and child rearing the foundation of civilization? If they aren’t how can
you have a future without family and children?

THE DAY THE WORLD ENDS. GO GET A POINTY THING AND POKE!

Zombies break out in front of you, you are unprepared and don’t even know what you
are seeing. You are probably going to freeze and die. You will hesitate, you will not act.
You will die very soon and very badly. You won’t even be lucky enough to be a zombie,
because you will just get eaten by a hungry fresh herd. The world will be falling apart
before your eyes, and you will see people dying and doing the most horrible things in

order to survive, while armies of the undead lay waste to your world, home, civilization
and everything you have ever loved. See your family, the ones you love, being eaten.
See the home you lived in burning before you, and everything being covered in shit and
dead bodies. Anything you have ever imagined as sacred or real, will be smashed. Any
imaginable cruelty that can be done to a person, will be tried. If people can imagine it,
then it has been tried, and will be tried again.

Staying calm is the most important thing, and remember you have a future you want to
build and be part of, from the essence and soul of your being. You will need a weapon,
armor, supplies, and a shelter. Your goal will be absolute victory, and nothing less. The
Greeks defeated vast zombie hordes in the past, and you will have to learn how to do
this again. Get yourself a back pack, and start getting the things you need to live. In
these moments of utter clarity, there is nothing to fear. Star straight at life, and run for
it.

GETTING BASIC SUPPLIES. BIKES

You are going to be making yourself into a light skirmisher. A scavenger tinker.
You will be adept at range, tactics, speed, and using your surroundings.
Bicycles are your best friend. There will be plenty of them, with tools and parts to
repair them. Bikes will always be faster than any zombie, can go over most imagined
terrain, be easily carried, be taken into buildings, be a storage center for tools you
collect. Start collecting rope when you have a bike. Rope is a tool, a weapon, a wall, an
escape route, a home, and civilizations best friend.
Eat everything in sight. High fat food is the best. Drink all the water you can. Food will
be easy to get at first. Don’t worry about getting fat; you should try to get fat. Forget
any notions of a diet, that you once had.

Get a backpack to carry things. First aid kit. Canned food, water. Cooking oil. Pocket
knives. small common tools. Saws. Light axes. hammers. Duct tape. Light rope.
Containers to hold water. Basic camping equipment. Bullets. Vodka (put in plastic
bottles). Screws. Bolts. Wire. Sewing kit. Fire making tools. Small bottle of fuel and a
lighter can get most fires going. You won’t need lots of fuel to make a fire, if you know
the basics of fire making.

WEAPONS:

•

You are too weak to fight, and should avoid direct combat, at all times. Get
Poles that can push people off you and to get away with. Distance, range, breaking
knee caps, running away, are the way to fight. In that moment, right in front of you,
just find something to keep people off, and get away with.

•

The gun store is not some genius place to go, it will be a bloodbath of
human on human violence. If you have a gun and lots of bullets, don’t use them
or show them. Think of every bullet you have as being money. Guns are not as
useful as you think, unless you want to die yourself.

•

The more your weapon can also be a useful tool, the better. Tools make you
more friends, than pure weapons, and are far more useful. Start building a tool belt
or a bag of tools. Getting tools, being light, being fast, and good scouting are the
most important things. Framing hammers seem to be about the best common kind of
weapon/tool out there. Light “tomahawk” axes are another useful tool/weapon, that
can help you in nearly all situations.

ARMOR:

Think about comfort and how things feel on your skin. Don’t be immune to your
senses and emotions. Comfort, breathability, sweating, and mobility all matter. You
need something you can wear all the time. Heavy bullet proof Jackets are awesome
unless you have to hike in hot weather for 10 hours. Police riot gear is at some level the
perfect armor since it is designed for zombies.
You will need to start gathering parts to assemble armor. Gathering a large tool
kit will be essential: knives, heavy scissors, pliers, wrenches, bolts, wire, nails, glue,
sewing equipment, wire, straps, duct tape. Gather the best materials to wear on your
body: Ballistic nylon, gortex, leather, spandex, hemp, linen, silk, straps, cording.
Scissors, and straps can make quick armor out a back pack or suitcase, made from
strong materials.
Wear gloves forearm guards and boots with shin guards all the time. Boots are
armor and a great weapon. Kicking and stomping, will be most of how you fight, not
punching or swinging things. You can readily do push kicks and stomps, not martial arts
spinning and flying kicks. Kick to get away from a fight, and cripple a knee as much as
possible. You will need to build up armor around your shoes up to your knees and on
your forearms.
Helmets. Find one that works for you, and find better ones, when you can. Police riot
gear helmets are probably good enough. Your helmets are far more about social
meaning, then they are about defense. They will form the social collective identity of a
group and of individuals. Your helmet says what kind of person you are on a battlefield.

THE BASIS OF HOPE: YOUR FIRST WORKSHOP AND GROUPS

You need to organize around bases, and develop your bases in size and location through
time. Your very first few hours of survival, will need its own temporary base. You can’t
plan, build, rest, or prepare without a base, no matter how small.
Workshops and the culture of work are the basic humanity and technology to
create civilization from nothing. Investing in the future is created in your work, and
preparation for it. Your temporary base of operations will be a workshop to make things.
Get a location you can defend, wall off, and escape vertically from easily. Acquiring your
initial group will be based in reality: family, friends, co-workers, classmates, members of
community organizations you belong to or have belonged to, or public servants you don’t
know. The hardest situation will be apartments in dense cities. Since most people in
cities don’t even know their neighbor, organizing a building for common defense is
unlikely, and being locked up in your room, makes you an easy target. Your house may
seem safe; it is in reality a dangerous place you may need to move from quickly. Get all
the things you need in there and move. You never had a real home to begin with.
You have to start making people that are all equipped with basic gear and a
workshop. Go get people and lead them to places to manufacture weapons and armor.
You will need to find people near you. Get your people together, and have a plan for
after you get together, before going out. Basic organizing of people, that haven’t lost
their minds, can save you, though don’t depend on them.

WORSKSHOP AND TECH SUPPLIES:

Technology is going to be critical to survival. This is not a return to the stone age. At
worst, you get back to a pre-industrial society level of organization, with all the
infrastructure already built for an advanced society. You will have your mobile phone and
messaging apps. If you happen to have the time convenience, then you can also gather
up computers, routers, phones, cables, networking gear, because these will be the most

valuable things you can own, with the right set up and software. Saving IT guys that can
run this stuff will save your entire world.

SUMMARY OF GEAR:

You might be alone or with a few people. You are going to need to move
yourself and your gear, that you can travel with, on a bike and on your back.
Eat fatty foods.
All this basic assembly and gathering of equipment can be done in a few hours. You
shouldn’t go anywhere, until you have the basics. In large cities were most people live,
there is a societal collapse already, that is held together by social norms and simple
prosperity. If you take away hope from a city of people with no real connections to each
other, no basic trust, then you will have a brutal reality descend on you. You will have to
forge groups of people to work together, in order to survive. There is no lone wolf
survivor, of any real significance nor meaning. Surviving is not enough to survive. You
need people to build a new world with, and to create life with. If you plan only to survive
with no long-term vision of the future, you are dead already. Zombies and the
apocalypse are when people have no individual vision of the future, and the societal
institutions that binds these goals together in an overall sense of hope and purpose.

GETTING TO YOUR LAUNCHING POINT

MAKING A LOCATION TO MEET YOUR FAMILY:

You must arrange where to meet up. It has to be a place you know well, have access to,
and possibly someone in your group even owns. You should consider places you can

make things as ideal locations, because manufacturing supplies is a central task. It can’t
be a famous location, or a place with heavy resources. You need to be on the side of
resource rich areas, be out of sight, and have a defendable location with many ways to
retreat. It can’t be some obvious place other people would go. I should be along major
transportation corridors, with lots of things to survive with. Your sense of the familiar will
attach you to certain physical locations, and this feeling can kill you. Your sense of
personal attachments though can save you, and help you form larger social groups.

TRAVELING TO FIND YOUR FAMILY: SCOUTING

Sensitivity is a survival advantage, if you aren’t going to fight directly. You are
going to have to move some long distances to form into the groups you will need to
survive. Random people nearby are far less valuable than close relationships within a
day’s journey. Traveling is not so hard, and not so scary. The world has plenty of places
to hide, and there will be so much chaos, that you can disappear. Open your senses, and
feel the reality of the world around you. Let it flow through you and around, and don’t
resist it.

Stay in contact with your group in a group messenger chat, as you navigate
where you are going. Tell people everything you are doing. Send photos. You won’t be
smart, because of fear and uncertainty, and you can get other people looking at your
situation. If you are one on one chatting, then you are more likely to get bad advice. Get
ideas and information from people, not advice. You have to trust your own judgment and
decisions, with others giving feedback and insight.
Don’t tell people what to do. Be mindful of how insecure and unconfident young
women are going to be. You are not going to help them by reassuring them, you will

help them by giving them useful information. Peoples lack of self-confidence will make
them very vulnerable to listening to everyone around them, and not trusting their own
instincts.
Environmental awareness is key. Expose as little of yourself as you can: sight,
sound, smell, taste, touch. Use your senses to feel and avoid danger, rather than
become terrified and overwhelmed. You always move from points of cover to points of
cover. High ground, and places with multiple routes of advancement and escape are
useful. Use mirrors and or cameras to look around all corners, so you can move from
covered location to covered location. Rope is useful.
Always scout where you are going. Every street, every intersection, every
destination. Scout them and plan for escape, at any given moment. You will need to get
to a meeting point with people, and pick others up, on the way. This will take planning,
and foresight. People in a newly falling civilization, won’t have the mentalities to focus on
all the tiny details of route planning. “I am just going to run if anything happens” are the
words of the pre-bitten. If you are running or fighting, then you have already failed.

YOUR SECOND BASE

You may need to sweep a whole building before settling in. Don’t kill the zombies.
Simply lock them off. Enough melee battles will eventually end in your death. Securing a
location is not that hard. Taking out stairs and getting up high, make safety easy.
Apartment buildings can easily block off a first floor, and access to higher floors. Ropes
and ladders can be dropped from second floors and then can be easily pulled up.
You will make a short-term base, before heading on a long journey. Set up a
more complex workshop of many people. Get mostly women and children, sewing, and
making light armor. Everything is about mobility, ease of repair, redundancy. You need

to make your workshop portable. You will need to scout and scavenge. Avoid obvious
places. Avoid people. Don’t build anything outside.
Lay traps for escape routes. String wire and rope across certain areas to trip people
or zombies as you go out, you lay traps for the route going back the way you came. You
then can run back along your route, and be reasonable safe. Intelligence and future
planning can easily defeat those that have no planning and vision of the future. It is why
killing them is so easy, and why you will win.
Bringing strangers “home” is a bad idea. Don’t bring people to your base, that you
meet scavenging. Your base is to gather supplies, so that you can leave the place you
are in. You can help individual people be prepared and suited up: weapons, tools, armor,
food, water, bicycle, and so on. Build a model of survival and organization that can
replicate easily around you, and in your interactions. Close relationships and trust take
real time and real work, and can’t just be assumed because you want it to be true. In a
group, trust is a great thing, and it can be taken advantage of by outsiders.

WHERE TO GO TO START OVER

Supply up, make a plan, and get out of the city in a group by bicycle. You will
have bicycles, armor, back packs, weapons, tool kits, first aid kits, sewing and armor
kits, internet gear. You will probably need to travel 100 to 30,000 km to get to a suitable
location. You will need personal connections in that place, if you are to go there. Good
places will be easily fortified and keep outsiders out. You may need to develop a leap
frog plan of base building, along a long route, within the social network of people you
know. You will eventually within in weeks or months, reach a location to settle in for the
next few years.

Small towns are the obvious places to go. Resource rich. Fenced off farmable land.
Independent sewage and water systems. Can block off entrance by zombies with just 46 barricades across the 2-3 streets that will run through a small town. Fences and
properties will create natural boundaries. Towers and scouting can help organize
defenses, readily.
The wilderness may seem ideal, but it lacks in resources, unless you know how to hunt
and live off the land. You will most likely become a raider that lives in the woods and
scavenges nearby cities, if you move there. Homeless, starving and ready to kill anyone
to survive, is not the best way to be living.
Farmland and ranches will provide everything, and have all the means to survive on
their own. These locations are rarer and will be taken. They will be away from people,
and large dangers. You may have no clue how to survive in such a place, and they don’t
provide plentiful resources to really build a future. If you know how to live there, then go
live there. Make food and live. Farming is the foundation of civilization and why it even
came to exist.

ON COMPASSION AND GROUP COHESION

Having a plan, with a future is important to keep a group together, and keep
people focused on what they are doing. Focusing people on the task at hand, will
take compassion and good communication skills. Humans are going to fall into despair
and get lost. You have to hold your group together, and tend to emotional wounds in
people. Groups will not win based on how well they can fight, they will win because of
how well they can plan for the future and hold together as a unified group of people.

Your natural inclinations to comfort people, needs to be transformed into
empowering people with the means to survive. Kindness isn’t always soft on the
outside. Focus all communication and actions on things that will lead to winning.
Sensitivity gives you awareness, and knowing how to use the least force to achieve
something. True compassion and kindness requires brutal and direct strength.

BEFORE YOU LEAVE, LAST THINGS, AND NEW PEOPLE

FAMILIES ARE THE BASIS OF CIVILIZATION.

-Everyone must have a family or seek to build a familySingle men are the largest danger to society possible. Men need people they are
willing to die for, and direct the purpose of their lives towards. People will need to form
families, and get closer to their own. All adult men must have partners, and people they
are responsible for; these connections need to develop quickly. Lone survivors roaming
the wastelands of civilization are the very people that won’t be that relevant. Civilization
was not driving by men out in the middle of nowhere by themselves. Society has groups
families working together, and men sacrificing for their future.
Families are the foundation of civilization and the most efficient ways to use
resources. Wealth in all modern societies is created mostly by the money saving
features found in the efficiencies of marriage. Single people are not needed. Boyfriends
don’t leap on grenades for their girlfriends or strangers. Men sacrifice their lives for what
they love, and feel a permanent bond to. New marriages, and old ones surviving and
getting stronger are true measures of a group’s overall social fitness.
Pick a leader fast. Groups of families will form into basic groupings. You need to form
up with who you can work with and have a basic operating trust. Arguments over

hierarchy and leadership, need to be settled quick. Get each individual person focused
on tasks they need to accomplish.
Everyone needs to have connections in the group, and these connections form a
network of identity. You will form a base group of 5-9 people, family and close friends.
Then form larger groupings (bands) of people from within your social network of 30-60
people. This might only have 10-15 able bodied men, that can fight. You can’t rush this
group formation, and it has to be driven by real connections that exist between people.
Adopting children, siblings, and even parents, might be crucial, where people have new
brothers, sisters, moms, dads, uncles, aunts, and grandparents. Social institutions to
deal with homosexual marriage are not clear, and in certain conditions could add to the
survivability of a group.
Respect and friendship can form marriages. The idea of love and feelings defining
marriage, will have to be abandoned. Responsibility, community, family, self-sacrifice,
and other similar values, will define marriage at the end of the world. People that don’t
want to form into family like units and have loyalty to others and be willing to die for
others, are not worth knowing, or being involved with. Mutual profound respect for
another person, can create a deep, sincere and meaningful relationship, that will give
you greater power and ability to survive and prosper.
Adopting children with no parents, will show a commitment to humanity that is
bigger than oneself. Children need families and stability. They need a vision of a
future being built right in the relationship in front of them. We have to create the future
before our children’s eyes, so they know how to live as good people, and bind
themselves in love to others to build the world. People that leave children they know, to
die, don’t deserve to be part of the future.

SAVING THE SMARTEST AND BEST PEOPLE

•

You must go out to find and recruit, important smart people as a moral
imperative.

•

An elite computer programmer can have more value than a doctor.

•

Visualize the future

Your business and professional networks can now be tapped to build your
group out. You will need to get engineers, scientists, doctors, biologists, accountants,
mathematicians, and businesspeople, to get your group strong. They will readily join
your group, if you sincerely help them for the future of the world. Protect the top people,
even if they don’t join your group, and give them as much as you can afford to spare.
They will be more likely to join larger and more stable groups with strong social bonds
and long-term visions.

If there are other groups recruiting the same people, then you might want to join up
with those groups. Those groups have a clear moral vision similar to yours, and probably
will be good to work with. A group all decked out in weapons, ready to fight, informs you
of their values and what ideas they cherish. There won’t be slavers out looking for
engineers at the start of the apocalypse. Slavers like hot women and dumb manual
labor, because they seek to feed their own aggression and vanity, with instruments of
power.
Respect and intelligence can bind functional social groups together. Intelligent
high functioning people will be naturally inclined towards civilized society. Intelligence in
many ways, is the capacity a person has to function in civilization and large groupings of
people. Smart people can adapt more readily, and have experiences to empower other
people and not just themselves. A person that can take mobile network towers and
reconfigure them to make a local area network for all mobiles to tap into, might seem
unimportant at first. We won’t have enough electricity to power a lot, but we can easily

make enough to power mobile phones, mobile towers, and basic servers. They can add
the most value to everyone in the tiniest action.

TECHNOLOGY BASED LEADERSHIP AND WOMENS PURPOSE

The people that can rebuild the world, and have the knowledge to run and
create infrastructure, are the ones that must lead. When looking for the most
useful people in groups, combat ability should not be what defines a groups hierarchy.
Fighters should be near the lowest people in a group. Does the group have engineers,
scientists, computer programmers, doctors, nurses, auto mechanics, carpenters,
welders, metal workers, petroleum engineers, mobile network technicians, farmers,
veterinarians, military officers, cops, fireman, small business owners, entrepreneurs,
middle managers in companies, and so on. More educated and trained people will be
able to form larger groups of connected people, with rational organization systems.
Women have a power in themselves beyond anything any power on earth can
compare to; they carry the light of civilization and the future, in their very
beings, flesh, and will to survive. Women’s survival is more central to human
survival then men’s survival, and this plays out in deep cognitive ways in how we
connect and think as human beings. Women give birth to children, and are vastly more
likely to be able to love babies. Men and women are not equal, not the same, and not
ideally suited to do the same things, and this reality needs to understood. Women are
more inclined cognitively to minimize risk, seek certainty, and value dominion over
themselves, due to their inherent physical vulnerabilities, acute senses, childbearing
capacities, and lack of leadership training. Women are inclined to prefer certain types of
power and behavior out of men, because they are useful for female survival and
minimizing their own exposure to death. Men’s identities are formed around female
choices.

Fearful people obey leaders readily, by human nature. Your own fear will draw you
into following those that can make you feel safe, reduce uncertainty, and seem in control
of the world around themselves. Deep commitments to humanity combined with a strong
technical vision of the future, is the basis of good leaders. A raw capacity to kill will not
create the future. Your world is filled with technology and having the vision to repurpose
it and use it, will determine your survival.
Religion can also help form large groups. People will naturally go to civic service
organizations to build a network of people that can work together. Community leaders,
church leaders, government leaders will form natural groupings around them. Societal
leaders without a strong mix of real brain power, will make a group weak, in the long
term. Civic leaders can’t be the most valuable people; HR heads shouldn’t become the
CEO of a great company.

THE JOURNEY

Your group will have to survive through a collective challenge of a long-distance journey
to a new home. That journey will form the community, its bonds, and what really works
and doesn’t. Groups that have a challenge, will survive better than those that have it all
from the start. Culture needs struggle to form character, and not too much struggle
where no real progress or development can occur (Toynbee). You will see death; you will
see tragedy. The world isn’t a movie, and big things just don’t happen at random that
much. Most of the time things will be very uneventful and with sparse and intensely
shocking moments. Even in most violent wars, soldiers spend most of their days like
prisoners, with nothing happening, where boredom and loneliness become more
dangerous than bullets.

You can’t save people on this trip. You are traveling to save your group. When you see
horrible things, you can’t just go running in, or running away. Ruthless steady reason
must prevail. Think about what is good for your family. Would you send your own child
to go help?
•

If you see common people, needing a little help, then certainly help them.

•

Get people set up, and with a plan.

•

Spread organization to those that you readily can.

•

Pick your route to avoid major points of interest.

•

Stay off the main routes humanity will take.

If you do run into functioning units of society, aid them, don’t follow them. Your own
fears will make you willing to be controlled and follow anyone with the apparent ability to
protect you. In this world, you need to maximize your own capacity to face fear and
make something, rather than turn to authority to protect you. If you are a strong group,
gangs and raiders won’t pick on you. There will be plenty of weak humans to prey on, for
human predators. Be something that good people are attracted to, and can see a future
in. This is a brutal world, and this journey will be disgusting.

BUILDING A SETTLEMENT

Build a larger unit of people that are your people. You need to live with your people
and people you will fight with next door. Build up your family and the groupings of
families that you bond to. Real feelings, and real relationships, will save you. Build
groupings of homes together. Have strong home units for a family, and then structures
to protect a group of families, and prepare to defend yourselves. Build defenses from the
inside out, and not from a large wall in. You live and die on your own, in the end. From

each place you stand, you will have to fight to survive, organize with those around you,
and implement the structure of your surroundings to survive.
Voluntary organizations are much stronger than mandatory ones. You need to
build a community, and do community work. You can’t just work for yourself. You will
have collective duties, that arise out of community commitments, that arise themselves
out of your own home, and your own family. Your community is worth investing and
everyone that belongs in a community must add time and work into that community. It
is voluntary, and it must be strict. You work for yourself, and what is yours is yours.
Your duties though extend to the things around you that sustain your life. Your selfinterested actions need to function and support a community.
Fences and walls, make good cities. You will need to build fortifications from the
inside out, and based around your own closest bonds. People need to first fortify their
homes, then groupings of homes, communities, to small cities, and so on. Strong homes
make strong cities. Making one big wall is a bad idea, and will inherently fail due to
human self-interest and nature. Slave armies build massive walls. Lots of internal
defenses and structure will create a stronger and more sustainable society.

CAPITALISM WILL SAVE THE WORLD

•

If you aren’t investing, your time, resources, and love into something
more than yourself, there will be no future for you or the world.

•

Capitalism is the Solution to the Zombie Apocalypse, and all societal and
economic collapse in the world.

The solution to defeat the apocalypse is simple, first you make strong families and
communities. Those communities then push for capitalism at its highest levels.

Capitalism is about decentralized and unregulated commerce. A healthy capitalist
society allows people to start any sort of ethical business anywhere with the least
resources. They follow contracts, property laws, and basic civil society. Don’t cheat,
steal, or murder evolve into more nuanced ideas. Society collapses when we ignore the
fundamental principles that have created all success throughout human history. There
are no socialist or communist success stories ever. Capitalism is voluntary and doesn’t
require violence or force to be run. All other systems are run at the end of gun, and with
the threat of death. In places with no hope, there is always someone to gamble the
future on, something to put your time and money behind. Building civilization from the
ground up, is not about charity.

Progress comes from struggle and individual choices. Hard work, entrepreneurship,
frugality, family, sacrifice, duty, character, values, and freedom are things that will
always have fundamental value to the individual character of those that build the world.
Countries with trade, economics, and freedom, have prospered the most. Surviving
zombies is about building a company, that provides valuable services to your customers,
and getting paid accordingly for it. Contracts, deals, negotiations, trade, money, HR,
management, product development, sales teams, customer service, and all the rest, are
always central to real life, no matter what.

THE WORLD HAS ENDED--- You don’t escape having a job, just because the world
ended. Creating a functioning economic system is the most important thing a society of
people can form. If you don’t have economics, business, money, and trade, then you can
only have raiding and conquest as the primary form of intergroup interaction. Life won’t
be pre-industrial farming, with raiders and monsters coming to kill you, if you choose
capitalism. You will have high technology to create new options to survive. Some will
want to make a utopia and end the failed ideas of the previous world. Editing out the

failure is an impossible task. Strong visionary leadership, with bold plans, are safer, than
people’s natural reactions to close off, and minimize danger. Closed societies will perish.
Open societies with no rules will perish.

Capitalisms growth and development creates the same sort of reactions people have to
change, new technology, and the destruction of their former way of life. People need to
fit in the machinery and logic of capitalism and its technology or die. People have to be
domesticated into technological machine worlds ruled by money, numbers, and exact
processes. It takes time and is very harsh looking. Helping the rest of the world learn
how to work in factories is not immoral, and it is something we may all have to return to
one day, if our societies fail. The “apocalypse” could just be the day fat lazy office
workers having to work go back to working in factories or farms. Weak minded
westerners are mostly too proud to face such a world and would rather die than do work
they consider beneath them.

GREAT INVESTING IS ABOUT INDIVIDUAL PEOPLE. The future is built by
individual character. If we try to collectively build up broken societies, we will all
inherently fail. Nearly all aid to Africa fails, all welfare to intrinsically poor people fails,
and all pity thrown at people leads to no adulation. Tech can give us the power to find
and empower any human on earth. Great people will do things in ways that have never
been done before, and be more deeply connected into the reality of things as they are
now. Those that are “without”, are more aware of what we need. Tech can’t just think
about a vision of the future, it must have a connection to the present and how we are
living now. Our orientation towards the future can be guided by data, by guiding us
towards the best people to invest in and the best ways that we can live and organize our
lives. Data itself is a social living entity bound up in who we are as individuals, in our

relationships, and in the direction, we lead our lives. Analyzing big data is about
something far deeper than just targeting advertising to people.

SAFE EXTERNAL INVESTING- If we invested money into an African company
before, their very business and profits could be harassed and pillaged by local corrupt
governments and gangs. Technology can empower us to put our humanity into places
we couldn’t before. If the world could save Africa with $10 trillion investments, and we
knew it would work 100%, we would make the investment as a people. Most help only
harms those that receive it. We didn’t invest in companies properly. The same
technology we use to invest in Africa, can also create a better internet, a better
capitalism, and make a system that can life up a society that collapses. It is a system
that makes society zombie proof, so long as people want to live.

Building companies in the middle of horrible places, can be made easier with the
virtualization of company infrastructure into computer services. People can invest in a
company’s future from outside the country, by building out an investments IT side, and
drive new companies into using the most current management tools. The whole of a
company can be managed and run with apps, being powered by servers in distant
countries, with investors from all around the world. People with nothing, can bootstrap
from nothing, have greater access to investment, and have most of their business online
and untouchable by local forces, even if they barely have a functioning internet.

AMAZING JEWELS HIDDEN IN THE DARKNESS. We as individual people have to
be accountable to our own conceptions of who is human and who is not, in our own
eyes. There is nothing wrong with loving your family more than other families, loving
where you live more than other places, loving your culture more, or loving your country
more. We have to invest in people. If everyone in the world cuts themselves off from a

place, there is no network of relationships and business into that place to build it up.
Poor inner cities, undeveloped countries, penniless rural farmers, and dirty humans with
barbaric thinking, are places we don’t invest in enough. We aren’t connected into them
socially. We as individuals have to build up the world around us and use technology that
builds up the world and systems around itself.

CAPITALISM FOR HUMANITY SURROUNDED IN ZOMBIES

HUMAN NATURE- The societal and government institutions to run businesses at their
best are rather simple and straight forward. They have been evolved through millennia
of human history, and are the cultural wealth of history bestowed upon us from those
that lived before. The people lucky enough to inherit such ideas have known great
success. Human nature doesn’t change much anymore, and the ways to deal with it are
a form of social technology. We can spread this power through technology and modern
institutions. Marriage, rule of law, education, frugality, honesty, humility, hard work,
individuality, sacrifice, ethics, and freedom, are legacy treasures passed down through
time to succeeding generations.

MARKETS- The term a “free market” is the literal meaning for the freedom to open a
shop without impediment and sell what you want to sell at the price you want, and not
be shut out to favor those already in the market. Free markets are about the shop
keeper’s freedom and not the customer. One is the foundation of the other, and not the
other way around. Restrictions on being able to open markets and market places lead to
tyranny. The challenge of free markets is in growing businesses and more markets, that
compete against each other, so outsiders can shop around for the best markets and
shops in them to sell and trade their goods. Those that interact with your community,
can trade things with your community, and both sides can get the things they need the
most, and there can be a win-win relationship. If your community has products and

services to sell to people, that are actually useful, then people will come buy them, and
respect what your community can do. It is hard to raid a community that makes things,
and not just simply hordes supply. By allowing a “free” market, where people can trade
good at market stalls with no interference, you could create the greatest prosperity for
the people outside of your community.

You can imagine a flea market/bazaar like situation, outside the wall of a community,
were locals and outsiders engage in trade. Multiple markets could exist at different gates
to the city, with no central management or control of all the markets. Outsiders could
not enter the city, and market owners could enter the gated city after the closing of their
shops for the day. Warehouses could all be inside, and made safe. Virtualized markets
are still possible in a world with no society and order, so long as you have a basic
internet system set up for people to connect into.

GOVERNMENT CONTROL OF MARKETS- Free markets need to have few rules,
because rules will always increase to favor those in power. The more power there is in
government organizations, the more businesses will tie themselves to that power to take
out their competition. Limiting the trade, and the formation of companies, is a natural
and common government exercise, because companies come in and petition the
government to stop competition on their business. The shop keeper doesn’t want to
restrict their customers from buying, they want to restrict others from selling. The south
side market gets the government to make rules that hurt the north side market. Modern
slavery over western people in western countries, controls people through the rigging of
prices, and who can even make a business in a society.

People don’t even realize they are enslaved because the systems of control are placed on
those that run businesses and not common people. They see the bad practices of

companies and blame the companies, and not the governments who created that conflict
to grow their power. People can imagine themselves to be free, while all their decisions
are defined and controlled by external controls of prices and the ability for new players
to enter a market. One cannot make effective rules to regulate a future business that
has never existed, one can make rules so a future business never exists. It isn’t up to
you as a community leader to decide what sort of companies will exist. You can’t know
everything, and you can’t know what will work or not work. Over time, though, your
community will have wealth beyond any neighbor.

PRODUCTS FOR BOREDOM- Services that bring hope, excitement, joy, and vibrancy
to life, will always be successful and essential products to sell in a “zombie apocalypse”.
The weird things people will really want, are beyond anyone’s real imagination. Boredom
will probably be one of the biggest problems, in a world with nothing to do. All you will
mostly do will be to work, fight zombies, and eat horrible food, while living in horrible
conditions. The primary punishment of going to prison in our modern world, is the sheer
boredom that rips through a human mind, where stabbing someone seems a good idea,
just to make a day more interesting. Humans random will to commit violence for no
reason, can consume a society, as just a form of entertainment to break the
monotonous and boring conditions of survival living.

When people have no vision of a better life, they will implode and descend into madness,
extremism, and violence. You can understand nearly all the issues in dying ghettos,
Africa and the Middle East through the lens of this paradigm. The denial of capitalism
and prosperity for people leads only to mental insanity and death. They have been
fundamentally deprived of the cultural wealth of freedom and its underpinnings. With no
future, no joy, no exploration of possible realities, their souls die and descend into

violence. Nearly all entertainment exists to soothe our failed dreams and lack of a real
future.

SELLING THE FUTURE AND CIVILIZATION- Most places in the world, have never
been developed and never know true freedom. Delivering prosperity, as a business in of
itself, is the greatest product to sell to those that have nothing. To build up the hopeless
with the knowledge and power that you possess, is a moral and profit seeking
imperative. Spreading the institutions and ideas that make you strong, are ways to
defend your community, by surrounding yourself in allies that have built themselves up
from the values you hold. Cultural conversion of your neighbors comes from success.
Pure assimilation of other people into your society will not promote and grow civilization.
Conquest is unnecessary with the modern inventions of capitalism and its technological
liberation. We don’t need to conquer and pilfer the world to be rich. We don’t need to
invade countries and steal people to enslave into manual labor to be rich.

THINGS YOU CAN’T SELL- Beating slavery means, you make something that people
want, and they freely come to you to buy or trade for in an open free market. You don’t
sell addictive things, that control people’s minds. Drug dealing is not a real business. The
people interacting with you should feel gratitude at the chance to get things they
normally couldn’t get. Great services like Wi-Fi, mobile data plans, the internet, apps,
farm seeds, information, critical tools, water purification devices, pretty bedding, home
décor and even fashion can all make for great businesses.

ENERGY AS CURRENCY- Fossil fuels and electricity bring people out of
darkness and into modern civilization. Those that control the energy and electricity,
control the economy of a society. The real wealth of nations that we have now, is the oil
and energy that backs our global currency. Drilling for oil and gas, is the best product
any society can go after to get rich. Smart people will go after oil rigs and refineries,

rather than food and gun supplies. You can bring dangerous neighbors to your door to
trade, if trading with you is far more profitable than fighting with or trying to steal from
you. Natural gas and fracking might be one of the easiest ways to get fuel, when large
oil refineries are rarer and hard to obtain. Being able to control a gas field, and process
gas that can be sold to people, is a huge power. It is easy to get normal gasoline
powered cars and motorcycles to run on natural gas. Electricity and stable supply of fuel
for vehicles, creates the foundations for massive wealth that machines can bring us.

With energy comes clean water and sewage treatment. Making these system work and
get new parts for them, is a large challenge. For a fallen western country this is easy, for
a country with no such infrastructure, these are hard to get services. Machines that can
make these parts, or any parts that are needed, are world changing innovations in
technology, that are being developed right now. These are long term technologies that
can protect the world from collapse because they will allow it to develop up from any
level. Universal manufacturing machines can liberate humanity from any stage of
desolation and collapse, if they have the energy to run.

ZOMBIE INTERNET: TRANSFORMING ENGERY INTO DATA

Mobile internet first for everything is the key to making modern solutions that
can scale the world and into the most resource strapped locations, and defeat
marching hordes of the undead.

If you really thought about it, the one thing people would want more than anything at
the end of the world, is a good Wi-Fi connection for their charged devices. Wi-Fi is the
most valuable thing you can have for the smallest amount of energy, currently. The

basic infrastructure of the internet can be a commodity, at any stage of societal
development. Network processing power, storage, bandwidth, cloud services, are
reaching a point of such development, that they can almost be a currency, in of
themselves.

A peer to peer, bitcoin, and block chain, run economy and internet, is an anarchist
unicorn fantasy. Things have to actually work and be useful, and not just random wideeyed fantasy. We make things inspired by these ideas to drive innovation, and not being
concerned if some perfect ideal is achieved. It is a driving force and not a defined
idealistic end. An African business still needs real money to run a business, people still
need bullets to shoot zombies. A large cloud service company with idealistic intentions
for a more open and free internet, could be a strong driving force, to help push forward
the protocols to make such a system work, and make people more likely to engage with
the system.

Instead of a society armed with guns, they will be armed with computers and the
internet. Money can be stored virtually and secured. The “gold” would be the actual
network, services, and data. In a broken society, the best way to get rich, would be to
go get as many computers linked up into a network, with the best connectivity, and
support people getting connected.

People should be able to “harvest” computers and network equipment, and it should be
as easy as shoving a thumb-drive into a USB port. We build large central servers
because they are easier for large companies to make money and control content. Netflix
could run off everyone’s local computers, and not even need a large central server, with
peer to peer (p2p) networking, like bit torrents. The internet is the technology that can
build the world from nothing. Companies that want to build for the future, need to

consider how their technology could run, in a collapsed society, without any large
companies to maintain them. The software of running a government, a business, a
community, are all awesome services to sell to your neighbors over a fully running
zombie world internet.

At some level, we need a wireless internet that develops from peoples own homes and
devices, and not a centralized telecom system. We can use Wi-Fi connections to build a
whole network, where half the bandwidth of a router or device is used for connecting to
the network, and the other half is used to build the network. The system would bypass
most of the centralized systems, and yet connect into them, to create a larger internet.
It would supplement the current internet and vastly expand the supply of access, which
would reduce prices for people. This can use the existing devices and tech people have,
and we as individuals build an internet. This will work better in denser cities with people
living closer together. The system can have seed routers, that help maintain a basic
system, and then new devices add in and amplify it all. Cars themselves could be wired
in be like moving Wi-Fi towers, and a whole see of driverless cars moving through a city,
could themselves be part of the very arteries of an internet.

Most all countries don’t offer real choice in people’s internet and mobile phone plans. The
companies are all government backed and or controlled, with prices and services all
regulated. This sort of conflict can even exist in the zombie apocalypse. Hating your
phone company can be universal. We won’t just get over comparing the different mobile

phone plans, we have available, even at the end of the world. The internet is a business
we can bring to people and sell them, it can’t however enslave them into a narrow set of
choices. A single company controlling access and content, is not free, and won’t grow to
its maximum potential. Beware of companies like Google and Facebook trying to bring
the internet to the world for free.

Monetizing internet IT companies, apps, webpages in the apocalypse will be hard, since
there won’t be a large enough market for the advertising systems we use now. Branding
and advertising companies could, with the right vision, be useful. A new form of
monetization, branding and advertising can be achieved in such circumstance, with a
proper imagination and a desire for a capitalist future. Free people using free markets,
can do anything in the worst circumstances. Virtual goods and services can create the
backbone of a post/low-civilization society.

Devices all linked to each other can create an internet in of itself free of all masters. We
can just buy devices and the very devices contribution to the network pays for its
internet access. We could pay for internet with the amount of computing power and
connectivity we put into the network. We all can be partly responsible for the network,
and this changes the future considerably. This can build out from local networks like
those used in companies. You could nearly run a whole business just using mobile
devices to access everything, and connected together by a small local server. Meetings
could be made hi-tech with the just all the devices of the people in the meeting, being
linked. You could make teleconferencing cheap, easy, and seamless. Everyone has
cameras on smart phones. You could run just about anything, with the right software,
and devices linked up into it. No large IT costs.

This is a very useful platform for the apocalypse, with the right software installed. Many
apps, like messenger apps, would need to be able to run on local networks, with no
stable internet connections. Larger versions of apps could have server versions that
make them run more smoothly with people using those apps over that network, rather
than have to rely on a more distant unstable server. In Africa, data connections could be
very unreliable, so software will have to run inside the local network, even if connection
to the internet drops off temporarily.

With colonialism, you could conquer and country and manage everything internal to that
country. This was inefficient. With imperialism, you could control all the laws, trade,
police, border, and effectively control a country, with more distant forms of power. With
neo-imperialism, countries could be controlled by just controlling the money, like
America does with the world money supply being backed by the dollar. With the internet
of things, that connects all things and people into the internet, you can control the root
nature of humans with little resources and maximize their potential labor output based
on the individual potential. The agency that controls the access to the data, controls the
system, and thus controls the world. Data is money, data is power, data is the ability to
control people with the least amount of effort or resources.

A NEW KIND OF INVESTMENT

My main idea is not in how to turn the internet into a commodity to underpin our
financial system, it is how to use that resource to make a new kind of smarter
investment, that is profit motivated. If there are $10 trillion in profit motivated
investments to be made, with about 10% of that intention being noble and good for
others, versus $200 Billion 90% nobly invested, then the more capitalist profit driven
investments have more overall nobility and kindness in them, on the whole. There is just
so much more money that can move into black society, if we can make an effective form
of investment, that will get results. Profit motive mixed with nobility can achieve far
more than either alone. Pity or pure exploitation have not worked.

If you loaned only virtual money, that could be used for online services, this would make
for a much safer and smarter form of investment, into a company. From the start, force
the company to be fully high tech in its internal infrastructure: all online finances, HR,
management, inventory, everything online. We can drive the entire business into using
internet tools for everything. This will open up the whole company’s finances and
information for analysis. Investors will be able to track fraud instantly. This will make it
safer to invest more money, and make companies more likely to succeed. Intelligence
and computer power can be transferred into companies, with little physical infrastructure
around them. They can have access to the very best online resources to run a company,
even if they have little electricity, running water, or even stable government.

If you were a company, and you had a bunch of virtual currency, that you couldn’t spend
on real material things, the most likely thing you would spend that money on, to build
your company, would be online internet services. Basic cloud based servers would be a
minimal thing, anyone would buy. We can run tremendous amounts of a company from
just online tools. We can greatly reduce the cost of starting and running a business, with
modern technology. You can manage a lot of life purely online, and thus the services

provided by a purely virtual world, can be of fundamental value to survival. Virtual
currencies that exist online, and are based in the power of network, create an interesting
economy.

APPLYING THIS TO AFRICA:

Finding the best returns on investments is not about greed, it is about finding
the best places and people to put money into. We need to invest in the best people
in Africa, and not “Africa”. Black people are a group of individuals and not some
homogenous mass grouping. There are more super geniuses in Africa, then there are in
Japan. They are just more spread out and harder to find. Individuals need to be helped,
so that the best people can rise up and create something for their society and the world.
The greatest charity a person can do, is believing in someone and making high risk
investments in them. It will always be the person, and not the plan, that matters more,
when investing. We must find the best way to invest that money, so it can’t be wasted,
stolen, or mismanaged, by the shattered societies around them.

If someone wants to invest in African companies, it is very high risk. They are in
unstable societies with little rule of law. People that have been wanting to help Africa
have kept donating to charities, and those have had little benefit. Governments are
given money by western countries, and nearly all of it is squandered and stolen, and
puts countries in deeper debt. Financing poor places leads mostly to more problems,
rather than greater success. Black people need money invested in them, all around the
world, and people don’t loan money to them as readily. While high percentages of black
people are the lowest performing people in the world, among them are some of our
greatest minds and brightest lights in our world. No matter what group of people there
are in the world and no matter how low their intelligence is collectively, there is always

highly intelligent people with IQs, general intelligence, and gifts, greater than nearly all
other people on earth among them. We search the world for black athletes, musicians,
and social leaders; we rarely search for black mathematicians, inventors, and
exceptional entrepreneurs. Genius is human and transcends all racial boundaries and
collective identities.

GOVERNMENTS AND PHONE COMPANIES AT THE END OF THE WORLD

Even countries could be run this way. Instead of giving countries money, we give them
online internet services to run their countries, and force them to have all open data.
Open Data is good for everyone, except the group that doesn’t want their dirt to be
seen. Open standards that are driven by putting everything that an organization does
online, with usable trackable data, is good. It makes investments easier to make. People
will want to even pay taxes more, if we can track the all the money the government
spends and then see the results of that in real time. We can build investment systems,
that can see everything, and make organizations truly accountable. The way to build
this, requires building something that would work with zombies and a completely failed
society. We need to build from the smallest level up: individuals, families, communities,
business, local government, social institutions.

If you are a boss and you have all your employees linked into a system all the time, that
can track them, you can gain control over them. You can use these devices to ensure
security, building access, and even network access. By being able to monitor and control
everything, this creates greater incentives to invest and greater opportunities to extract
value from people. In a broken society, all this monitoring can increase safety and
replace many forms of public service. People that are linked up and monitored, will be
more civilized and committing less crime.

CHAPTER 6: THE MORAL VALUE OF SLAVERY AND THE BIRTH OF
NEO-CAPITALIST SERVITUDE

Slavery is considered the evilest institution in human history. We as people love slavery,
and use it a lot. The world we live in today, is filled with millions of slaves. It is not a
black and white institution with clear lines between what is a slave and what is not a
slave. Englishmen once lived as serfs on lands owned by nobility, and had to do
whatever their lords told them to do. They had many freedoms, and could do as they
liked in most day to day things, there overall life though had no power over anything
more than their immediate surroundings. They couldn’t pursue power. They couldn’t rise
up to be more, than what they were born as in this life. Nearly all of humanity has lived
in bondage and slavery for most of their existence, or as uncivilized and wild human
beings outside the very story of human history. The very story of history is the story of
the dominion and enslavement of humanity to serve the needs others and their own
personal values. We cull and kill people readily that we don’t see as human, and call it
noble.

We just create different names for the kinds of slavery we like. The word “slavery” has
more to do with kinds of slavery we don’t like. The kinds of slavery we like we call things
like good government, welfare, open borders, immigrant rights, or social justice. If tied
to things we don’t like then it is rather easy to see the slavery in it: wage slavery,
capitalism, globalism, elites. Saving humanity requires bringing people into humanity,
and not simply treating them as human. Reality and results matter than being nice to
people you look down on. To be human is to have a purpose and a future, and those that
do not, can only be called useless, savage, or monsters. Genocide is widespread in all
countries across the earth, as we choose certain groups of people or humanity itself for

extinction. This is not a conspiracy, nor all that complex. We are just dark nasty
creatures that don’t like to admit it to ourselves.

ZOMBIE WORLD SLAVERY

People often imagine in the apocalypse slavery being a common institution that will
return. The collapse of civilization doesn’t mean we have to make all the same mistakes
that people made in the past. We can never truly return to what we came from. We have
too much cultural innovations and technology around us, to ever really lose everything
we have made. If we really believe that slavery is evil and one of the great social
mistakes in the history of humanity, then we need to develop ways to live that don’t
require it, if civilization were to fall. Our modern cultural innovations should be able to
improve the quality of life and the humanity of civilization, at any time or stage in man’s
development.

The real moral challenge is whether or not slavery is really bad. If slavery has a function
at some level of human development, then it is a moral institution. Using outdated forms
of slavery when more modern ones could be implemented could be viewed as the
problem and not slavery itself. People that like being safe and not dying, more than
being free, often like to be enslaved. They find being well fed, a warm shelter, and work,
to be better than living in a dangerous wild world. Finding ways to deal with the “good”
reasons slavery happens and the moral dead end it leads to, might be impossible. Fear
drives many people into asking to be enslaved. The majority of Americans, white and
black, before the American Revolution came to America as slaves. Many of them entered
slavery voluntarily, most didn’t survive their contracted time as slaves. In nearly all the
world, before the American Revolution, the vast majority of people on earth in all places

existed in some form of slavery. America was the first country to begin the war against
slavery and usher in new ideas of how people could live in a country.

THE ROOTS OF SLAVERY

In a barbaric world if there is war and then those people waring against us surrender, we
can either kill them or enslave them. Releasing enemies back out into the world, that
can come back to attack you, is simply not realistic. If you are living in a village and
raiders come and attack you, and your defeat them, should you kill or enslave the
survivors? If you imprison people and make them work, that is slavery. Once you start
to take slaves for the most justifiable of reasons, your society will be more inclined to
take slaves for other reasons. Your other choice is genocide. Slavery seems more
justifiable then killing every man, woman and child. In history, cultures faced these real
dilemmas, and they can’t be wished away with idealistic thinking.

When western people plundered Africa and enslaved people to work on plantations.
They, at some level, justified this by the horror of life in Africa and how little those
people were using their potential to work. The people themselves were an underused
resource that needed to be channeled and used for better purposes than random chaotic
jungle life. Slavers actually saw themselves as helping those people, as compared to
them living a life of savagery and uselessness. Slaves in America lived better lives than
people in Africa, and were already themselves enslaved by their own people, in the mass
African slave system. Nearly all slavery in Africa was done by Africans. They sold them
at any markets they could, and took anyone a slave they found valuable.

The internal African slave trade is not a history that people get taught. North African
slavers invaded Europe and enslaved white people. The black male slaves they sold to
the middle east, in massive numbers, were all castrated. There is not a clear message or
story here, that can fit into historical narratives of civilization, progress, or whatever.
Humans liked enslaving people, and it wasn’t America behind the slave trade. Hating on
America is about the only unifying aspect of teaching the history of slavery and anything
that doesn’t fit into that narrative is censored out and made racist. It was in America
that full humanity of blacks and the full savagery of slavery, was made apparent to the
world in images, pictures, books and art. It was America that first started the movement
against the slave trade, though took longer than other countries to end its practice
internal to their country.

A western slave trader could rationalize that moving slaves to a better world, was a
moral improvement over slavery in a more backward and dangerous place. If you
believe slavery to be wrong, then you will need to find a way to run a primitive society
without it and be based in the reality of the world around you. When you are trying to lift
up a people with no stable civilization around them, it is very easy to end up enslaving
different groups of people for different reasons. It is easy to rationalize these
enslavements as being more just than the alternative.

CLOSED PLACES WITHOUT SLAVERY

In a zombie apocalypse community, it is rather easy to govern a group of people that
share the same values and all want to come together. People will resist in less developed
people into your society that don’t share your values, culture, or even basic intelligence.
Eventually people will come to trade with you, want to join you, and/or steal from you.
How you manage these people without slavery is far more difficult. You can close

yourself off from new people coming in, only for so long. The ideal society, in a zombie
world, is made of members of the highest value and usefulness. You want people that
can all work together, trust each other, and provide useful skills to the whole group.
Different people will be good at different things, and form levels high specialization.
These sorts of societies are easy to not have slavery, because you simply don’t have
people that could even be made into slaves enter your community. Idealized northern
European countries are racially and culturally homogenous societies, with little to no
immigration throughout their history.

Challenging Questions:
•
