Are countries that are rich and successful, yet closed to letting outsiders in,
morally justifiable?

•

Can we treat a country like a company hiring the best workers, and not wanting
people that can’t work well?

•

Is it better to live in...
1. A village at the end of the world, that is happy, prosperous, closed to
outsiders, and that doesn’t have slaves,
or
2. a society that is open to outsiders, even ones that have attacked them,
but makes them into a second-class group?

I really don’t know what is right. If I was a person that was in a lower class, I might
prefer to be a second-class citizen in a safe place, than a first-class citizen in a harsh
dying landscape of armies of the undead hunting me, with little food and no real chance
at a better future. Though if I lived in that “good” place as a second-class citizen, did
good work, and was a good person, I would want a chance to be part of that society,
and if they didn’t embrace me, I would feel resentment and not gratitude. At a moral

level, it appears that a functional society needs to be able to bring in new members who
are not clearly useful to that society and provide them opportunities to rise up to the top
of that society. Any sort of inequality in access to opportunity would itself undermine a
society.
Another possible answer is that we trade things and not people across borders. Strong
borders, with strong trade, and an open economic system, can mitigate many issues,
and might be how societies have to form. Creating a government that leads to prosperity
and safety for your people, while not enslaving those that can’t assimilate into your
society, is probably only possible with highly prosperous capitalism. If you are able to
freely trade with people, and sell them something of value, that will give them a better
life, than you don’t need to integrate them into your community to have moral value to
the world around you. You can sell “freedom” to people.

BROADER CLASSES OF SLAVERY

Any system that holds people back from highest levels of attainable power, that
rules over them, have enslaved those people.
Slavery is a not a black and white line.
•

If women can’t hold power in a society, are controlled by the men in their families,
and made to do work, then they are slaves.

•

If people do jobs where they are kept from getting higher education, higher
positions, and their children never rise higher, then they are slaves.

•

Migrant laborers exist as a form of voluntary slavery, where they are not allowed to
integrate and rise up in the society they work in. These kinds of workers are even
denied the right to even fully live in the place they work.

•

Companies that employ people and don’t let them freely change jobs or have any
say in how they are led, are slaves.

•

Countries that turn their people into serfs, that work the land, while the elites rule a
country, are slaves.

•

If the rules of system are rigged against you to eventually possess power, you are a
slave.

•

If you follow ideologies that never empower you to live a better life, than you are a
slave those ideas

•

If you are addicted to lifestyles that trap you from becoming more than you are in
your life, than you are a slave to those addictions that consume your life.
o

If addictions are fed to you by organized institutions then those
institutions rule over you.

MIGRANT WORKER SLAVERY

Migrant workers all around the world live as slaves in societies that want their
labor, and not them as human beings.

Mexicans illegally enter America to work in millions of jobs that are waiting for them.
They have no legal protections or rights, and work for the lowest wages with the lowest
level working conditions in America. This life though is better than the one they risked
their lives to escape from. Is it good to let them work and have a better way of life,
make them citizens of your society, or send them back to their country? In the real
world with real consequences, such choices are not so simple. If you have millions
around the world waiting to enter America legally, and these illegal immigrants become
legalized residents, it undermines the rule of law, for the whole world. Having a
slave/serf underclass undermines society even more. In China, over 150 million people

work as migrant workers, and this cheap labor partly fueled the economic growth of
China. They built cities that they would never be allowed to live in. Eastern Europeans,
East Indians, Indonesians, Latin Americans, and countless other groups of people are
marginalized in varying societies and live as functional slaves all over the earth. This is
the modern face of globalization and its modern slave markets that drive its profits.

THE MORAL VALUE OF SLAVERY

We tried a lot of different things through human history as way for strong rulers to
control and manage a group of people. We have seen success and failure. Certain ideas
were very popular before, and we now no longer find acceptable. We found better ways
to do things. Certain things from the past are good practices and others are ones we can
never use again. The line between them is not clear.

•

If we returned to a level of pre-civilization, of man at war with man, what sort of
systems that we thought we had evolved past, return?

•

What sort of society would you make in the rubble of fallen and dead civilization?

•

Is slavery a justifiable institution ever?

If we want to make the most ideal systems, we can pretty much figure those will fail.
Idealism in of itself never gets results, because it has no relationship with reality. Good
government has a lot of nuance; good systems develop over centuries and millennia.
Humans are utterly uncreative and can only identify and use things that have already
been thought up. People are incapable of creating new ideas, no matter how obvious
they are, until they are made apparent. No one person can fully understand why certain

rules exist, how they came into functioning existence in world, for anything, ever, in all
circumstances.

There is an intrinsic randomness that creates things, and is at the root of all
effective creation, change, and evolution. We do not control how things come
into being. We do not control why certain things work and why other do not.

In peaceful societies people forget the rules and systems that lifted them out of conflict
and poverty. There are fundamental institutions of society that are harsh and very
realistic. They evolved from the absolute reality of human nature. People go to jail, and
get killed by their own governments justifiably. Systems of government need to be
always conscious of the possible fall society and how to continuously rebuild it from
nothing. In all places, there is a nothingness that we cannot control, that we cannot
ignore, that can stimulate and give birth to the new. The more we try to control
uncertainty, the more it grows into an absolute nothingness that envelopes an entire
society. The more we deny the essence of being human, the less human we become,
and thus arises the very breakdown of society. Step into uncertainty, darkness, fear,
human nature, and reality, in order to create, find meaning, and lead yourself to a life of
greater power and mastery over the earth and others.

The greatest danger to power, is an entire society, system, company, country, economy,
collapsing. If you have nothing to rule, even with absolute power, then you have no
power over this world, but your own self. You must create systems of power that lift up
society and govern humanity, in order for your life to have any sort of meaning or hope.
Power flows from the amount of people that have power, and that power arises from
each individual’s place in life. You as an individual can change the world around you and

the life you live, by your choices. In a fallen world, your choices will determine the
future, for yourself and those around you.

CHINESE EDUCATION AS SLAVERY

In China, the education system is supposed to be the great equalizer. People can rise up
and get good government jobs, by how well they do on standardized tests, that are
taught and prepared for in schools They can go to the best schools and get the best jobs
in China, with just high scores on certain exams. High test scores can lead to higher
power in a society. If the testing system is not fair, then the people rebel in enraged
anger, at the unfairness, and inability to escape their circumstances. Testing is a
fundamental social institution of Confucian societies, that promotes social peace and
prosperity. It creates a system by which people of all classes can obtain power through
the merit of their own ability, study, and habits.

The exam system is only one institution that keeps corruption in check and creates a
perception of fairness and opportunity in China. In reality, positions of power in China
are given out to those with connections and personal relationships and not by a clear fair
system of rules and test scores. Those with connections still need high test scores to go
the highest levels in government. The system is not wholly corrupted in the sense that
the sole basis of power is personal connections. If the Chinese government doesn’t
correct this perversion, then their very hold on power will collapse and the best people in
society won’t struggle their hardest to rise up and be the best. As a principle, you want
to lead the best people, to be the most powerful. People that feel like slaves don’t
become super intelligent and don’t reach for the highest level of human being they can

be. The illusion of upward mobility can create great developments in a population of
people, over time though if that promise is not delivered on, it creates the foundation for
societal collapse and revolution. People study hard in China because they truly believe
that is the way to succeed in life. If they stop believing that, and people stop studying,
the consequences would be world changing. The reality is that so many people invested
their sense of reality into education as the means of personal advancement, that any
system that doesn’t promote that will be crushed and will have to evolve.

What happens to a society if its best and brightest people don’t rise to the top of that
society?

In China, the testing system is the very power of that country. Testing controls
everything. It is in most ways the very ruler of China. The rule of law, at its most basic
level is governed, in China, by the national testing systems. If those systems are
completely fair and without corruption, they can still have serious problems. Fairness is
only one consideration in how to make a good testing system. Making it fairer for all with
little corruption is fairly straight forward. Reform of this system is probably one of the
most emotionally charged subjects in Chinese life, short of housing. The system itself in
its ideal form, still only promotes a narrow range of human potential and ability, to the
highest forms of power. The people that don’t fit into this system, are wasted, and have
to find others ways to advance themselves in life, if they have any.

Making a system that nurtures the best out of people and raises them up to be the best
and the brightest is the fundamental problem. If the test can’t capture the abilities and
talents of great people, then those people are being oppressed by that testing system.
Chinese tests are mostly singular and only focus on narrow parts of human intelligence
and ability. They demand certain ways of thinking, and don’t deal with other ways of

thinking. If tests can’t ever capture the full potential of human beings, then they will
always fail as a social institution. The testing system itself becomes a form of slavery
over the minds of its people, and limits the full potential of people.

Massive amounts of human potential are destroyed. A country becomes poorer because
of this. The people that can’t rise up, that should rise up, hold deep resentments and
anger and never contribute fully to their society. They are mentally enslaved by a
system, that traps them out from power and success in life. Their discontent can shatter
worlds. The education testing system is so deeply ingrained, that it has to be evolved
and not replaced. It is their culture and it is their history, over throwing this in the name
of some idealized system that people believe will work better, will fail. China will always
have exams, so long as it is Chinese.

There will need to be different testing regimes that use entirely different kinds of
thinking and rules. Expanding the tests to include more kinds of abilities and intelligence,
is one way to modify and not over throw the system. For instance, China can use other
countries national testing systems, for some of its citizens as a way to balance out their
own system. Internal cultural competition can be a source of vitality. The central
management of this system is a source of great power. Over micro-management of the
testing system, only leads to a systemic failure of the whole society. Governments don’t
like to let go of absolute power over their people’s minds.

People though will rejoice at the chance to take very different kinds of tests, that don’t
fit into traditional molds of Chinese education. Most Chinese people that have money and
can’t succeed in the Chinese education system, go running off to other countries, and
spend all their time in China, studying other countries tests, so they can get into those
countries systems. Normal Chinese people don’t have those choices, and thus live

trapped in a system that doesn’t represent them. Only the most intelligent and or
wealthy, have any choices over their education, and their future prospects, since they
can more readily leave China for other systems that will better develop them as people.

Testing to get government jobs and the right to be a leader, will still be narrow and
nationally controlled tests, though these exams could learn from other countries
government testing systems, and include a broader range of intelligence and knowledge
to test. People need the ability to be able to rise up in the institutions that rule over a
society. The Chinese government needs to get its best and brightest into its leadership
and have diverse kinds of thinking. If everyone thinks the same, and has the same kind
of high intelligence, then the government overall is less intelligent. The desire for a more
powerful government can drive the opening of a testing system, because it will bring in
more diversity, intelligence, and awareness of reality. Diversity of thought is rare in
nearly all institutional powers around the world.

In America, nearly all elites go to the same schools, learn the same things, and are
indoctrinated in the same narrow ideologies. Risk taking and raw intelligence is never
valued in any countries leadership. The best and brightest don’t go to even go to
Americas top schools, or any top schools in the world. Over a certain IQ and the more
that IQ goes up, the more those people have diminishing success, and higher aversion to
integrating into society. IQ isn’t even a measure of intelligence; it is just one narrow
kind of intelligence that is most associated with obedience to government. Kids that sit
and do what they are told, get higher scores and go to better schools. They then can get
positions in government, where they can rarely actually perform well in the real world
that is ruled by chaos, uncertainty, and true randomness. Self-confidence is the power of
an individual to face personal uncertainty; those that sit and obey, will never possess

this power. They can only possess hubris and arrogance, which veils their own sense of
inner personal failure and nothingness.

All governments face the problem that many of the best and brightest will not want to
work under leadership with shitty bureaucratic management practices. No test can
capture leadership. Leaders that rise up in government, are profoundly different than
those that rise up in real life, from real experience in the world. Studying management
and getting good scores on tests has little correlation with actual leading. People don’t
seem to be want to be led by individuals that did well in life but didn’t go through the
highest levels of education. Nearly all countries seem to associate intelligence with going
to elite schools. So nearly all countries have inherently failed systems for getting the
best people at the top. Actual life performance is rarely rewarded with government
power. These education elites can also come to dominate corporate business cultures,
where business and government are tightly linked. These are fake business people
whose job is to minimize uncertainty for a company, by manipulating the government
system to their advantage, against the rest of humanity. Corporatism is a false form of
free enterprise that blurs the line between government and freedom. Unaccountable
elitist education systems will nearly always lead to government and large corporate
tyranny.

THE SELF AND BEING UNDER CONFUCIAN EDUCATION

The other and even darker side to east Asian Confucian education systems, focused on
tests, is that they leave deep scars in people’s minds. Those that don’t fit into the
system, are beat down to fit in. The minds of Chinese people are tortured and abused in
high school to learn things they don’t even need to learn. Their entire sense of personal
dignity, their hopes, their dreams, and even sense of self, are smashed out of them. The

system is a form of mental slavery that rips into people’s minds and souls. This has
many advantages overall for certain kinds of people, and for the most part is beneficial.
It works great for people with no education and from poor families. It creates better
futures for those who have the least. Creating prosperity for people with nothing,
balances out the emotional sacrifices and cost. If you look at poor countries, you will
often find education systems that can barely achieve the results of a Confucian one. If
for instance Africa adopted these sort of education practices, it could lead to rapid
societal development in short time, with millions of the poorest people lifted out of
poverty and systemic oppression. Confucian education excels at mass scale
preadolescent education.

The real driving force that will reform Chinese education, beyond the government
wanting smarter people, is parents realizing what sort of harm that system can do to
their kids’ minds. They remember the abuses and suffering of their own personal
education experiences. Chinese people have more resentment towards education, than
just about any other thing on Earth. For richer families with choices, this will often lead
to more fun extracurricular education, and kids doing more creative things. They give
them more freedom, and less hours of study so they can live happier and healthy lives.
Studying 12 hours a day without break and minimal sleep, can never be good for real
learning or health, though parents continue to push this while knowing in their deep
hearts it can’t be right. Initial reform will happen that reduces the amount of study to
levels that don’t physically harm people and leave brain injuries. Understanding how
happiness and health can maximize education results will take time. Balancing out all the
different needs of people to achieve reform is not simple. There will be a lot of failure
giving to kids too much fun.

The real world has very demanding requirements. Getting children ready to face the
world is fundamentally important.
1. Get them learning actually useful things.
2. Have room for different kinds of intelligence and abilities
3. Embrace creativity and peoples’ dreams, to a certain degree
4. Don’t damage their minds with bad study methods.
5. Learn and test in a variety of ways
6. Get them set up to be able to achieve real goals and real success.
7. Let kids take risks, have fun, explore, make mistakes. Play.
8. And more than I can say.

If you want to be a good ruler, then you need smart and able people to rule, that are out
doing good work. The Chinese government should consider only how to maximize its
own power, by better utilizing its citizens and creating a better education system that
brings that out. The people that will rise up in that government need to be better than
the people that are presently in it, so that the government is only getting better year
after year. A system doesn’t protect people, have fair rules, and promote prosperity will
become weaker in time, and have no real power. Reform in China can rise up from the
self-interest of its own government to be more powerful. The people’s desire to protect
their children from harm and brain damage, can help drive things from the grassroots.

THE HUMAN EXTERMINATION PLAN: MAKING ZOMBIES

Killing off large sections of the human race has been a long deep held dream of mine for
decades that sickens me fundamentally as a human being. There is this cold harsh brutal
reality to the world and the needs for our collective survival that requiring taking out a
lot of the people, on the Earth. The Earth isn’t overpopulated in people, it is over
populated in people that have no future. The myths of overpopulation nearly always end
in a need to reduce the human population, and ironically only drive down the population
of the most valuable members of society, and push up the numbers of the most useless
people, and only creates even more populations problems, more environmental decay,
and an overall better future we are even farther away from. Killing off the weak, stupid
and inferior became an unacceptable option for humanity to openly admit wanting to do,
so any and all programs to do so, had to be done indirectly and in a more “humane”
way. The sad result of these programs, we have now, is that they have made the very
people that can save the world childless, depressed, hopeless, and living in dying
countries.

Population control and eugenics are expressions of the same overall theme of our
collective survival as a species. Population control manages us as groups, and eugenics
as “individuals”. We can collectively ignore the damage caused by population control, far
easier than with eugenics, because there are no singular faces to show as victims, the
damage is done to collective society and not to individuals. We don’t even know if we are
victims of population control, or even if we are beneficiaries. There is no real way to
measure results in the immediate present. We have to look at decades long demographic
trends to understand. In all places with strong population control, societies face an
existential crisis that will most likely end their existence. Eugenics had the decency of
murdering you to your face as an individual when it found you to not be human.

Genocide is better when it is more personal, and in your victim’s face. The reality of all
forms of population control and actual eugenics programs is that are all based on group
identity paradigms. The kind of thinking that wants to manage humanity as a collective
entity also sees people as collective identities. Eugenics reduced people into sub groups
of overall humanity, and then did population control on other “species” of people. It
organizes people and the sum of who they are into false categories like race, which has
no bearing on a person’s actual potentiality as a person innately. Population control can
target sub-groups, with overall trends and macro manipulations of public policy.

The machinery of genocide has to work based in individual characteristics and not one’s
group identity, to possibly be effective. The exact line between what we consider
desirable and simply unacceptable has to be more clearly defined in a realistic way, that
people can accept. We all believe in some form of genocide, and only differ on what that
line is in humanity. Certain people we consider less human, and when they die, we don’t
care, or even inside celebrate a little. A mass murderer, terrorist, child rapist, drug
dealer, or a low functioning down syndrome child, gets killed and few people will cry for
their lives. We can watch news of a one person in our hometown losing their home and
cry, and see have half a million people die in a far-off country, and we call that just life.
Killing off “others” is far easier, than things we see as similar to ourselves and more
human.

SUB-HUMANS

It is hordes of dumb single men, with no possible way to have sex, get a job, or have a
future, that are the greatest threat to any society or country. Single men with no future
rage with violence.

People on massive scales believe at some level that certain people are less human than
others. The issue is how to deal with this kind of thinking, and not if these ideas are
correct or not. Only the definitions of “sub-human” have evolved, not the thinking. By
nature, people create an otherness and rationalize it with whatever sources of authority
they can. “Zombies” are these people, and real hordes of them run over countries and
leave them in the throes of death, and render the world in chaos. These are the
uncomfortable facts of life. Any plan for the future has to deal with these things, and if
they don’t they are just idealistic fantasy. When faced with a horde of the dumb, angry,
and armed, there are brutal choices one has to make in that moment. The “zombie
apocalypse” is about how to kill these people and not feel bad about it. Compassion
doesn’t breed real solutions. Bringing zombies into one’s home and country, doesn’t cure
the problem. It is a denial of reality. Much of this book is about trying to save these
people from those that would come to commit genocide on them. And to save ourselves
from idiotic plans to “save” these people based on a poor understanding of the problem.
They are not poor and futureless due to education inequalities, persecution, colonialism,
patriarchy, and so one.

If people don’t like genocide in their lives as a basis of civilization, then they need to
consider the fundamental problem seriously. If non-civilizable people breed in high
numbers and live off a system they can’t create nor run, the world will die. The issues of
who needs to be managed is contentious and a good debate over who is more of an evil
asshole. The underlying problem is unescapable. If we imagined colonizing space, not a
single person would suggest sending out our dumbest and breeding them on mass scales
to fill those societies. Now the person wanting to select what they imagine to be the best
in society and sending them out, is also in a false paradigm that will fail. There is no
such thing as genetically superior, in the larger scale of things. When we try to match

the world to our ideals, we cut out what we find ugly, and that ugliness isn’t inherently
bad.

People with sub 83 IQs are basically non-functional. There is a certain point in
intelligence where a person can no longer function in the world, without massive
amounts of help. They can barely even do the most basic work. 1/6th of the human race
is nearly useless. Above such an intelligence level, we are all basically equal. More
intelligence doesn’t denote more humanity. Sentience is sentience, once a person
crosses the threshold of sentience, they are fully human, and people who don’t cross
that, are not fully human. No one would really cry that much if a special needs school
filled with the most mentally disabled kids, all burned to death, as compared to a normal
school. If a stranger, with a family and children, severely risked their life to save a down
syndrome child, few would find it noble. Being kind and loving the cognitively nonperforming members of society, takes the best and most noble people to do so. Most of
us deep down inside just feel pity and wouldn’t mind if they died. It is a sign of one’s
humanity and kindness to show warmth and love to them. In their eyes, we can see our
own humanity and dignity reflected back at us and have our lives nourished by that.
Families that have raised down syndrome children often call these children blessings. We
are human, and reminding ourselves of our humanity is a deeply meaningful and noble
thing. Any person wanting to create down syndrome or “special” children intentionally is
not noble. Any person wanting to create genetically superior super humans is just evil
and deeply deluded.

The greatest scientists and all the smartest most educated people on earth, once
believed in the truth of racial eugenics, and the absolutely need to cull and limit the
existence of black people. There was a time when people literally saw other races as
different species and where certain races where inherently incapable of higher forms of

thought. They saw black people as like high functioning apes, that could never have
someone of the highest levels of genius another race could achieve. While in reality, if
we took 10000 black people and 1000 South Koreans, there would be more geniuses of
the highest levels of intelligence in the group of black people. Culture plays a more
important role in intelligence than race. If a certain culture values less intelligent people
and they have more kids, the culture will become dumber in time. If a culture makes
intelligence the highest form of status, and those people have lots of kids, they will be
more intelligent over time. Race has nothing to do with intelligence. Certain cultural
groups have severe problems with low intelligence and can barely function in the world,
because their smart people aren’t valued and respected in their culture.

Many of the failed countries on Earth, simply have too many dumb people to even
prosper. The best and brightest in these failing cultures, can’t rise to the top. Within
even prosperous societies, certain groups just stay poor and dumb, and it has little
correlation with race, and more to do with the value people place on intelligence.
Breeding with family members is also a common cultural problem in many of the
dumbest places on earth. Many Muslim countries have people marrying their first
cousins, and this just creates failed genetics. The American lefts desire for gun control is
mostly connected to an image of zombie hordes of inbred hillbillies armed with rifles
descending upon them. While the right just wants more guns to kill off the zombie

A GENOCIDE SYSTEM

If we look at society, and say wanted to kill off 20% of the human race in one go. There
are many ways to approach this, based on differing principles and “ethics”.

1. Disease- release a virus that has mass causalities rates. This favors rich countries
and kills off poor ones. No matter how deadly or virulent a disease is, they can be

contained by the social ordering of a civilized modern society. Disease targets and
kills off uncivilized regions and peoples, even within rich countries.
2. Random- Everyone has to play Russian roulette. Play once and you are given a
certificate of survival: “Certified Survivor”. This certificate can be given to
anyone, and not only the person that played. People can play more than once and
pass on certificates to more than one person. This will favor families where
people will sacrifice for another, and create higher death rates among those not
bound in family structures or where others would risk their life to save yours. Lots
of the elderly will die off, in such a system
3. Death Melee- Put groups of people into an arena and when a certain target ratio
of people dies, then the game is over. This can have similar dynamics to a
“certified survivor” system. This will favor those that want to survive, vs those
that are willing to give up. Strongly motivated people, will overall survive a death
melee. Social and organizational skills will be favored over pure killing power.
Asocial people will die.
4. Kill to be Free- Kill one person and be a certified survivor. Fringe elements and
sociopaths will be killed off. 2-5% of the nasty people that everyone wants to kill,
but can’t, due to law, will get killed. Criminals and the such will die, because
there won’t be a vengeance cycle nor stigma. Tribalism will form with “good”
groups vs “bad” groups. This will take out more uncivilized “tribes” in a society.
a.

“The Purge”- Making murder legal for a certain period of time, will not
lead to that much death, because the law has little to do with why people
don’t kill. The law functions to stop vengeance, and cycles of killing. A
purge will just prolong vengeance and make people plan things out more.
Social stigmas against killers will still exist. Humans will still form into
natural defensive groupings of decent people.

5. Tests for the Best- Make a collection of different tests, where high scorers get to
survive. Society can base these tests on anything that a person could possibly be
good at. The top percentile that is saved would depend on the amount of people
wanting to be killed off. This system favors people with valuable abilities for
society. It can be, math, language, art, music, athletics, knowledge base,
creativity, being good looking, healthiness, and so on. Save the top 5-20% in
range a set of categories.
a. Just be good at something, in order to live. People that are good at
something have a certain focus for the future that is valuable and
contribute to society the most.
b. If you can cheat the system, and escape, you also deserve to live.
“Hacking” can be a skill set.
6. Combine all of the above- Don’t kill the low scorers on tests, put them into
different paradigms to get a certificate. You can see all of these systems, as a
kind of “test”, and only high scorers will survive. A normal family with strong
bonds, would easily survive and the elderly in their family would mostly be culled
to save the younger people. The elderly, anti-social, uncivilized, criminals, and
extremely lazy and useless, would be most targeted for death. While the poor
face deadly disease driven culling pushed on them by elites.

Now having a state with the power to enforce such a system would, by necessity, require
that all criteria favor the survival of those closest and most valuable to the state, and
those farthest from the state, to be targeted for death. It would be mass human sacrifice
by the state to ensure obedience to it, and the creation of a more civilized future. The
state has always been doing this since the first ones came into being 6,000 years ago. It
is the basis of civilization. Creating a more systemic form of killing of the unobedient and
unmanageable would only grow the absolute power of state control. All large states with

high levels of power, commit mass genocide. Human nature demands purges. This then

If death seems to extreme, the consequences of failure can be sterilization and or

THE MATRIX

Intelligence is just how fast you learn, and anyone can learn anything, given
enough time and patience.

The “Matrix” can be made real, and it can save the world and its 1 billion idiots. It can be
fully voluntary and people can be fully aware they are in a system like this, and still want

to be a part of it. They will be the “batteries” for AI, and create a useful service for the
world. The real challenge in the face of AI and our zombie apocalypse of sub 83 iqs, is
how to bring the two together into one solution. AI seems to make this threat to
humanity and making people useless extend up into even higher IQs where average
peoples skills will never be useful.

We need to create jobs for people at the lowest levels of intelligence, and feed the
growth of AI to its maximum potential. Low IQ people and low performance people can
be put into a AR/VR world, where they train AI algorithms to do basic things, and the AI
trains the people to do more and valuable things for its own growth. Even the lowest IQ
people can tell a cat from a dog, and applied to everything in the world, we can find
endless things even the dumbest can do. AI training makes it possible to create work for
any level of intelligence. People can specialize in things that they most like and are most
useful. Dinosaurs and porn will be labeled to perfection, down to the tiniest detail.

AI is very simple at present. Anything you can for certain identify in 1 second of thought,
is something AI can probably be able to learn. These inherently simple tasks you take for
granted on a daily basis, can actually be work for people, that rewards and develops
them as people. Education itself begins with things like a picture of a cat, and child
saying “Cat!”. We expand the number of things they can label, and inverse the problem,
where they have to be given the label, and find the correct object. Teacher says “Cat”
and student points to a group of animal photos and finds cat. This can evolve into more
complex things. Red cat, pink cat, happy cat, Siamese cat, jumping cat, sleeping kitty,
old kitty, kitten, jumping Siamese happy kitten in a white living room. A system that
pushes people to generate such results will want more and more evolved and developed
concepts. The system itself will want to improve the people in it to be smarter. There are
nearly endless things we can use the lowest levels of intelligence of people to train AI for

decades to come. The key is to find the things that have value now, and that can be
monetized, and grow from there. The people in the system will become smarter from
using the system itself, enjoy it, and feed into an expanding possible income. It all has
to be made into something a person would want to do, and has a future in doing. It
would be like living in a cartoon world of video games, and being able to make money,
have real friends, and eventually lead a much better more independent life than possible
before, by doing humble gamified labor.

As the system evolves it can also help people integrate into society and be useful. It can
help people to do the most basic tasks and then use whatever talents they have that AI
can’t do easily as the real service they provide. AI is being trained as it bridges a human
being into the world to do functional tasks with AI aid. An AI can’t be a human with joy,
love, and a smile, creating quality services for others, ever. You could see this like AI

Instead of putting robots in fast food chains, we can put people who now aren’t even
smart enough to flip burgers.

The centralizing of power to manage such a system is the fundamental danger of this

out of people in the most profitable way, that makes the workers themselves in the
system benefiting from it. Harm done to people will always be an excuse to take over
the system by larger more powerful groups. Making the system inherently decentralized,
in its very nature will be a fundamental and necessary feature.

To shift welfare systems from genocidal human slaughtering machines to humanity

SOLUTIONS 1-5

Solution 1: Take an existing welfare system, and change nothing. Add in work
requirements to receive welfare. Have them do any job with a fixed and set schedule, in
order to get government help. There has to be an elimination of all work regulations,
taxes, and wage requirements for people, in such a program. Companies can create
positions for people, if they can pay them any wage they want, and have them work in
any way they want. If a company treats their highly subsidized workers poorly, welfare
workers can just go do another job, and change readily. Many industries can create work
for people, if the government is paying large parts of their salary. As people get better at
work, their value as a worker increases and then they can change jobs, or negotiate for
a higher salary, while still getting benefits. This solution is ideal for low skilled
unemployed people, that just need to learn to work.

Solution 2: Pay companies to employ people through the tax system. No welfare benefits
are given to the worker, and this is not a subsidy to a company. The company taking
this money is performing a service for the government, and being paid the amount of

money needed to get them to want to do it. Vary the amount of the subsidy based on
the problems the person on welfare has, and how much companies don’t want to employ
them. Former felons, the disabled, and the mentally ill, can be better served by such a
system. Employing certain people costs a company more money, than a normal worker,
and increases risks for that company.

Solution 3: Doing community service to get welfare. People that have worked in higher
positions and have skills, are reluctant to work lower end jobs. Peoples sense of prestige
and status have to be maintained. Many competent and able-bodied people receive
welfare benefits. The elderly, temporally unemployed people. The benefits are usually
paid through insurance like programs, like in America’s, Social Security, Medicare, and
unemployment insurance. The longer these people don’t work the more they shrivel
away, and often end up on drugs, chronically ill, and dying. Their illnesses then drive
them into needing more welfare, and being unable to return to the work force.

Community service in one’s local area, that is non-political, and focused on community
services, can be a rewarding experience for anyone. Communities without much
community service opportunities will naturally grow them, as peoples demand for them
grows. When people need some form of employment in a real job, or in community
service to get benefits, they will go out and get them. They can be involved in things
they care about, and connect more to people and be valued in society. The same money
will be paid out by the government, in the same way, and there will be massive
increases in societal benefits, and vastly decreased healthcare costs.

Solution 4: Some economists have considered inflating the money supply by giving out
the money as basic income to the poor, rather than to large banks. Central banks
instead could inflate money supplies through small business loans done by small local

banks. Small banks get money, and are more connected to local economies, which make
jobs, rather than big banks that feed money into existing large companies, that create
no new jobs. New jobs are created by new companies, and most new companies start as
small businesses. Most people end up working in small community businesses.
Empowering the system that feeds into real job growth, creates a system that doesn’t
even need welfare for workers to get back into the work force. It also feeds a start-up
revolution, where people can feel pride in the companies they make. There will be more
start-ups, and more failures, some will work out.

If you were to use inflated money to run the other solutions that modify existing welfare
systems, it would be better to drive the money through a community bank, and then
into community service programs and local businesses. The exact way to do this, I
haven’t figured out. The main principle though is that money has to flow into localized
community systems, through accountable agencies that prosper and most profit from a
strong local economy. Small banks and businesses will inherently be less able to
manipulate the system and profit from corruption on large scales. Fraud at small levels,
will specific cases, rather than wholesale systemic fraud. Problems will be localized and
specific, rather than broad and general. There will be some scandalous localized stories,
and not a large centralized monster, whose failures are rarer and more massive.

Solution 5: Integrating new people into a community is a problem, not addressed in the
previous solutions. Immigrants need to learn a language and culture in order to fully
connect into a society and prosper. People trapped in failed communities need to escape
and move to new growing communities. We have local emigration and national
immigration, that need services to support them. Both are an education issue. To get
people to get an education they need, then we need to pay them for the education they

get, not the education classes they take. We pay for a result, and not the classes. If they
need to move to a new area to get good work, we pay them to move to a new job in a
new place.

If a person is in a bad area, we can pay them if they find a good job, at a certain salary
level, in another distant location. The money can cover moving costs, and help instigate
moving people out of dying off areas, or places with no future for them personally. They
only get money, when they get work. This then can be tied into training programs,
where they also get paid when they get certified in a real job, that connects into in
demand job skills, with waiting jobs for them, if they can complete the training. No free
training, no free handouts, no welfare, is being given. People study to obtain a new level
of ability and are paid when they achieve results. There are many jobs in any economy
waiting for people with the skills to fill them, and it takes motivation to get stuck and
hopeless people moving towards the future. If you pay people to stay where they are,
and not get educated, they will stay where they are, and not get educated, no matter
how many free education programs you offer them.

CHAPTER 7: OPENGOVERNMENT

USING THE POWER OF OTHERS

You are most powerful as a leader, when the people you are leading have the
most possible power, because the overall amount of power you can manage is
maximized. If you want to rule a small community, a company, a country, a galactic
empire, or the universe, the basics are the same. If you have power, you can do
anything you want with it. Power can be made larger by how you use it. Intelligent use
of power, leads to having more power, and bad uses of power to less. Micromanagers
control everything and don’t let other people have power, and thus they have less power
over all. An absolute ruler of a poor country is much less powerful than an elected
president of a rich country. A society that divides power among the most people, grows
into a more prosperous and successful place. The strength of leadership comes from the
quality of people that want to follow you, and your capacity to create an environment
that brings out the best them, and uses their abilities to their limits.

The best people that live in countries that stifle their freedom, leave and go to other
places. Great employees don’t like to be over managed, and when they can, they leave
bad companies and bad management, for better. If you develop procedures for who gets
promoted in a company, and everyone works with that in mind, and then someone uses
personal relationships and secret deals to get a promotion, it undermines the authority
of leadership and the rules themselves. Systems that try set up rules for how power is
used and minimize personal abuses of power often fail, because rules can’t manage
human nature out of existence.

You can certainly do whatever you like to do and use power however you want. There
are times when the system and the rules don’t work, and things need to get done. No
system is perfect. We pick leaders to lead us, because we understand that a system
can’t work all the time. Leaders aren’t supposed to follow the rules. If the rules and
systems worked perfectly then a society is solely ruled by laws and doesn’t really need
leaders. Well run companies and governments mostly just have good administrators that
run the system of rules that make things work. These are not leaders, and rarely ever
become great rulers. The head of HR and the enforcer of company policy are not leaders.

LEADERSHIP HAS NO RULES

Breaking rules makes people love you. When you break them to protect their lives or
create more prosperity, people will respect this. If the rules are going to cause people to
die unnecessarily, then breaking the rules is a moral imperative. There are those that
would let innocent people die, rather than go against rules. People will not even see such
behavior as illegal and might actually perceive it to be more lawful than pure rule
following, because it is fulfilling duties that they perceive must be fulfilled. In politics one
side will see you as a hero and the other as having done something very wrong. The
only real difference is just how they define a leader’s duties. If leaders do what we think
government should do than it is “awesome”.

Most of global politics is like this, where we have to establish rules and then often break
them. Just wars, just torture, just invasions, just genocide, just stoning to death of
women for being raped, are the oxymora of political reality. Traditional international law
basically says countries have to leave other countries alone and let them do whatever
they want inside their own countries, except when they have behaviors inside of “bad”
countries that can justify other countries attacking them. Developing weapons of mass

destruction and genocide are about the only reasons for just invasion. When we fight our
neighbors, we have to do so within the reasons we have government in the first place,
jealousy, rule of law, safety, and prosperity.

Invading countries for them dropping the world-wide supply of critical resources, is in
reality how real war is done. People not using a resource well, nor developing it fully is
nearly always a just cause for invasion or the seizing of peoples’ property. We just don’t
frame it in the real terms that leaders are really thinking. If the duty of a state is to
maintain a prosperous economic order for all, then a lot of things are going to have to be
done outside governmental rule making systems. You can always go take what you
want from others, so long as it serves collective idealism and fits into the duties of a
state. Even if you disagree with this, it is reality. The moral math of it can be explained
in maximizing the economic value of property, and in how that collectively benefits
society over the individual. In the case of countries with valuable resources, they are
being invaded in order to liberate those resources for collective uses around the world,
and for the benefit of the people in that country.

PLUNDERING FOR GOOD

“Good countries” develop themselves and their resources to their best potential or risk
being overthrown from within by its own citizens or from the outside by another country,
based on the belief prosperity is a governments duty.

One of the most common reasons to go to war and invade people, is to support
prosperity. You want something, someone else has it, you go take it. This is what
governments existed for in history. Governments maximizing plunder for its people is

how civilization flourished, and how everything we have now even exists. The world
before had very little and the only way to be successful was to conquer others and take
what they had. Enslaving and plundering countries used to be standard politics, until we
developed the technology to produce more wealth by cooperating, rather than fighting to
the death over limited resources. Humans still operate on forms of politics that
rationalize plunder as noble, across nearly all political ideologies. Only capitalism freed
us from this barbarity of inherent plunder. Socialists countries only survive on war and
plunder, even the northern European ones, as they did through their whole histories up
until the present.

In our world, there are sometimes things that we still need to invade and fight to the
death for, in order to create global wealth and prosperity. Plundering others can be done
for noble reasons, that don’t directly benefit the ones that to the invading. Let’s say you
have a country that has a special resource that the world needs for the world economy
to run, and that country isn’t developing the means to harvest that resource ideally. This
is a justified reason for invasion. Governments use this sort of reasoning to take land
and property away from their own citizens. The underutilization of a resource is a form
of conflict with neighbors. This is where common peoples’ idealism and political reality
often conflict. At the root of nearly all justifications to take others property is that they
are underutilizing it to its potential, and collectively society would benefit more if
someone maximized it. If a person is sitting on a gold mine and not mining it, has prime
farmland that is never farmed, oil fields untapped, a one-story house surrounded in
skyscrapers, “excess” money they don’t need nor use, they might just need some noble
plundering.

We don’t sell this idea to people very well. We don’t have rules and clear laws to govern
it, so the system doesn’t work when it meets these very real issues. If there were more

clear rules to justify conquest for collective prosperity, than different groups of people
would be far more inclined to develop what they have, for others to buy from them. The
clear defined threat of invasion to maximize a closed country’s poorly utilized resources
could drive that country to develop those resources. International law, with strong
threats of violence and absolute death, have a way of getting people to comply. Selling
invasion and war, based on resource development, just requires an idealistic definition of
a resource. With an idealistic enough cause, plunder can always seem morally acceptable
to nearly anyone. Not developing a resource well, is a very abstract concept, and yet it is
a reality of why we have justifiable conflict with others. Leaders that want to be more
powerful, need to develop all the resources in their society to their fullest, as a means of
protecting themselves from hostile neighbors, and to maximize the consent of being
ruled by the those you lead. Prosperity is an intoxicating drug that can rationalize nearly
any behavior. People like being richer, even if they are less safe.

The main point is to maximize your power as a leader. Get as strong as you possibly
can. The tools of power though don’t allow individuals to use them as freely as they may
want. Systems of laws make a ruler more powerful by giving everyone equal chances.
Strong individual people and groups make a society wealthier overall and safe-happyhealthy citizen create civilization. We shouldn’t overthrow bad governments. We need to
teach bad governments how to be more powerful in a step by step gradual way. Certain
types of leadership and management just don’t work. Certain economic systems and
rules have been shown not to work. The main problem is that other societies try to make
worse societies then theirs, behave like they do. Democracy and freedom is not for
everyone at every stage of human existence.

The mighty rule over the weak and drive out of them all their resources, for the
collective use of society and the maximization of the power of those who lead.
Developing humans to the their fullest and getting the maximum performance and work

out of them, requires feeding them their basic political needs and minimizing the things
they resent the most. Plundering the earth and humanity, is the natural state of
government and living as a human being is just finding the best slave master to
dominate you and not kill you too readily for disobedience. A little freedom goes a long
way to make those under your dominion achieve peak performance. Just remember that
in real life, if you don’t pay your taxes, people armed with machines guns can come to
your door and threaten to kill you if you don’t pay, even in the most civilized and
developed country, over less money than it even cost to send those people to collect
that money. They sometimes even drive tanks through people’s houses in America, over
taxes. It is rare, because that power exists, and people have that fear ingrained into
them so deeply that they don’t even realize it exists.

OPENGOVERNMENT

A country of laws, can be a country of simple codes, that we all can understand.
Government can be a computer human hybrid, that uses the fewest and best people to
run a state. Government itself will eventually be able to be upgraded with software
upgrades if we make the whole government accountable to machines. We can have
“more government” with less actual people running it. Smarter people with more
machine power can do a lot more than a large group of above average minds. Making
government accountable, will be hard for people to accept, rather than its traditional role
of making more jobs and power for itself. Every system, all information, has to run first
and always through computers.

The mobile revolution is quickly turning into the internet of things revolution and
governments are just a barely using desktop computers to do most tasks. A band of
people, in a low civilization place, could set up servers, link devices and computers into

them, and start to run a village, with little effort. They can use basic solar power and
minimal energy to run everything, and probably have a better government from the
start than most developed countries.

Government can’t hide when the very system is designed to expose and hold everyone
accountable. The top levels of government need to be run and lead by people that
actually understand how to use computers and implement them on a large scale. The
“head of IT” should be higher than the head of the governments police force and even
military. This is not like some corporate IT manager out controlling the whole
government, with old fashioned IT management. Government by nature is risk adverse,
and so they often take what they perceive to be the safer route that will cause them
least individual possible embarrassment, while in the long run, creating systemic failure
and highly risky collective behaviors. Opening data is way to push back against these
natural tendencies and bureaucratic thinking. This is not some one step solution, it is a
continuous evolving integration of technology that grows out of industry and
organizations. We have the solutions in their basic form already. We can step by step,
get these implemented and then evolve them through time. Capitalism and not
government makes these things possible.

Things to consider when looking at a “OpenGovernment”:
1. How quickly they upgrade
a. Are workers using the latest hardware and software?
b. Are they implementing new things fast and often?
2. Accessible real-time information with analytics interfaces
a. Numbers that add up and make sense
b. Is there anything being hidden. Does it need to be hidden?
c. Do intelligence agencies really need 70-year-old secrets? 40? 20? 10? 5?

3. How simply you can access and get what you need
a. Layers of bureaucracy can exist only in code, and not in your experience
b. Simple, direct, and pleasant experiences
c. Customer service should be excellent
4. Easy to get information that makes people in power look bad.
a. Can get information from the police that normally they wouldn’t want to
give
b. Are real scandals being exposed and people being held accountable
c. Are those in power getting away with abuses of open data standards
5. Are there real IT people at the top or just yes-men that enforce policy?
a. Do engineers hold high level positions?
b. How many elected leaders of a government have technical educations and
work experience? Engineering, math, technology.
c. does the IT department have its own police force that is actually kicking in
doors and locking people up?

ELECTION OF LEADERS

In this section I am going to present a very novel and new way to elect
government officials in a democracy. This is also a solution to problems like
campaign finance reform, that troubles American elections so deeply. It gets
cronyism money out of politics by putting in the system even more money, than
they cronies can pay. The size of government is an irrelevant issue. If it can do
something of benefit, and we want that, then we should let the government do it.
There are just few things that a government can do well, without causing more
harm than good.

The Iron Rule of Life: All things have a price that must be paid. We must pay for
what we want.

We get what we pay for. Instead of just voting for candidates, our votes should be
matched with money. Who we vote for, gets paid by the number of votes we give them.
Salaries and whole budgets of leader’s offices should come from money bound up in our
votes. if we elect someone to lead us, all their salary and all their staff’s salary, will be
connected to the money they get from the votes they receive. We should pay our
leaders the top possible wages so we can get the best people leading us. Leaders are
incentivized to promise a lot and deliver very little. We elect people based on how much
we like them, and in how much we want to believe the things they tell us. Humans by
nature prefer good intentions over results. Over time this lack of real results leads to
systemic failures that certain groups of people, can no longer ignore. When people
become disillusioned with government, and pull away, there are no consequences for
those in power, if they can stay in power. Open data can make leaders more
accountable, and make us more willing to invest in them, and the government projects
they push forward. We can regain our faith in the ability of leaders to lead, when we
have the personal power to hold them accountable at every single level. Getting elected
with 12% of the voters, vs 60% of the voters, is a huge difference in money.

THE MEANS JUSTIFY THE ENDS. We prefer humanity over results and doing really
good job. Corruption always begin with the noblest intentions and starts small. We
forgive vast amounts of corruption, because we like corruption that seems to try to help
those we like. Government has to be intensely human and connected to its people, in
order for it to work well. The art of modern government is in creating the most targeted
manipulation of key groups feelings, to get them emotionally behind a leader, and
maximize their re-election, rather than actually working on running a government.

Elections are where most of the corruption of government comes into politics. People
want to get elected and they need friends to help them get into power. They make
relationships with people that can help them get elected, and if they get elected will help
them back in exchange for their help.

CAMPAIGN FUNDING AND SALARIES

Elections and politician’s salaries can be funded by the peoples votes.

The low pay of government leaders and staff only drives them to be more corrupt.
People often hate the government and try to minimize how much people get paid. Their
wages in government office can easily be made much higher than anything they would
be paid on the outside. Human beings in power, being paid little will see themselves in
comparison to the rich and powerful around them, and by nature feel lacking in their
own lifestyle, and self-image. Humans will always be petty and most frivolous with the
smallest differences between them and their immediate peers that live around them.
They need to be paid more money than they make now in corruption, when they get
high paying jobs after leaving government service.

Change doesn’t require massive top down laws to change these things. It can be done at
a local level first. It should begin from the smallest units and work up to the largest.
Local changes can lead to a mass political revolution. We can take money out of
elections, by paying for them with the number of votes a person gets. Each vote can
correspond to an exact amount of money, and it shouldn’t be small. We can require far
more transparency in how they do things, because if they want the money, they have to
be open. Campaigns can still raise money the traditional way. We only pay vast amounts

of money to them if they run an open campaign with all money only coming through the
voting process.

Paying them from votes will turn their focus towards their voters, because have to work
on getting more people to vote to get more money. The more people vote and are
engaged, the more they get paid, and the easier it is to get elected. If we want high
voter turnout. Than we pay for it, by giving more money based on turn out. Even the
people that vote against you, can add to the overall money you can receive. Getting paid
for the people that vote against you, may seem counter-intuitive. We don’t want leaders
repressing the vote of their opposition, as a way to win. Paying for higher voter turnout
means paying our leaders some share of the money from the votes they didn’t get.

AMERICA AS AN EXAMPLE

“Every vote counts” needs to be replaced with “every vote pays”.

The biggest problem with American federally elected officials, is that America pays them
far too little. The second biggest problem is that they have to spend most of their time
getting money to run for elections. The third is how these two previous things converge
to conclude, and create systemic corruption. In America leaders and their staff plan
heavily on how to make lots money after they leave office. Voters feel that their vote
doesn’t matter, and that candidates are beholden to special interests. These elections
have low participation, and don’t represent the people. If we want politicians to care
about every voter, and to try to bring as many people into the election, then we should
pay them to do so.

1. All votes are backed by money that pay for campaigns and salaries. The
amounts for both need to be huge.
2. Candidates can choose to use the full government financed version, or raise
money themselves. If they want the large salaries, then they need to use the
voter financed election process
3. Primary votes for a party go to the party winner. Gets all money needed for a
campaign. More overall voters coming out, more money for campaign. More
contested campaigns should have higher turnout.
a. $10-15 per vote, per position: Congress, Senate, President
b. $4-8 million dollars for a congressional campaign.
c. $6-60 million for a senator. Depends on state
d. $1-2 billion for a presidential campaign.
4. If candidates are running by raising money and running with large campaigns
independent of this system, then the amount being funded needs to increase
5.

General election votes will determine salary and staff pay. They get money for
every vote for or against them. Higher turnout, more pay.
a. Representatives will need about 1-2 million in salary. 200-400k for key
staffers
b. Senators 6-20 million. 400-600k for key staffers
c. President 50-100 million. 1 million to 2 million for key appointed
positions.
i. Can be a billionaire if they win 2 elections. This will reduce
corruption and the desire to seek out money for personal
fortunes.

a. If the budget isn’t balanced, no one gets paid.
b. If we go to war. Pay is cut in “half”
c. If GDP grows by over 3%, $1 million for each percentage point to each
official.
i. 8 percentage GDP growth. Get a $20 million bonus, for everyone,
staffers included.
1. $1 million for each 0.1 % above 6%. Paid out over a 20year performance window.
2. Maybe half a million for each above 0.1% above 4%.
3. And if you receive bonus pay, can’t work in any
government connected job outside, or any lobbying. Bribe
them to not work against America for their own profit.
7. Parties and Registration
a. Possibly pay parties based on the number of people registered to them.
Don’t let them raise outside money.
b. Help finance elections before primaries
i. Party registration funding could allow parties to fund who they
want, or at least organize events for interparty competition.
ii. This though gives insiders and the party too much power
iii. Can have a no campaigning rule before primaries and force
candidates to compete in open debates.
1. Shorten Americas long election process

iv. If someone doesn’t want to pay a party, they can fund a “super
PAC”, and support a specific cause or issue.
8. Reform can be done state by state at first, and then eventually be passed as
federal law.
a. A state can pass a law for its representatives and senators. And finance
the federal government themselves.
b. Make Washington answer to the states and congressional districts they
represent.
c. If people want real reform, they will need to pay for it, at their local

i. Use your own local money and power to save the world, and not

country.

Because it would require federal law to fully regulate such a thing.

if a candidate agrees to not accept donations from people and
businesses in that state. Though that is not an ideal solution.

9. Evolved form. People in order to vote on something have to pay a set price for

a. A system that pays itself, will always be a bit corrupt.
b. The poor can be given money by the wealthier to vote, and the votes a
person makes can still be secret no matter what.
c. Communities could raise voting money, to give to people on demand, as
a sort of “charity”. This would require a very developed society, with
