HUMAN RIGHTS AND CITIZENSHIP

The right to kill someone is the basis for the power of the state and for contracts. All real
laws and contracts are enforced by threat of death. If jaywalking is illegal, then it is
possible for a government to kill a person to enforce that law. When we sign contract, it
means that you consent for it to be enforced at the threat of death. Putting our name to
a contract is a serious matter than must be understood in absolute terms of life and
death. The terms of agreement on a contract matter. Contracts are voluntary, and the
laws of a state are not. States that try to align themselves with the voluntary nature of
contracts more, are ones that are ruled by laws, tradition, and constraint. The more laws

that are passed and the more laws are passed without the real consent of its people, the
more government rules with the power of death, and a police state. Modern policing is
problematic because the primary job of police in an authoritarian state is to enforce tax
laws, and increase the power of the government. Cities that help fund their budgets with
tickets are authoritarian.

RIGHTS AND THE US CONSTITUTION

The size of government and how much power we give it is irrelevant. Power defines
government, and people pursue power as an end in of itself. The laws that govern a
nation, can be anything a government wants them to be. There are rules, traditions and
institutions, that constrain how these laws get implemented. The process by how laws
are made and enforced is fairly controllable. The intent of laws, is far more flexible, and
easily perverted to meet whatever ends people want, based on changing sentiments and
intentions.

Americans have a clear constitution that lays out all these rules for government, that the
government doesn’t follow at all. People complain, and think fixing the problem is
getting government back to its constitutionally defined powers. All the rights in the
constitution are not individual human rights, they are constraints and rules on how the
government uses power. The US constitution is more of restraint on power, than an
entitlement to power, since all governments by nature have the right to absolute power.
To restore constitutional power and authority to the American government is simple, and
people don’t want to do it. The leaders didn’t break the constitution, it’s citizens did.
Americans can fix their government and restore it to its legal and traditional settings, by
simply following the law on what the government has the “right” to do and what it
doesn’t, and no one wants to do that. People love all the things the government does

that are fundamentally illegal in the constitution, and being a “constitutional lawyer” is
the art of creating rationalizations people will believe and accept.

The law is often divided between “Natural” and “Positive” law. At their essence, these are
ideas of what rights are in a society. Does the government give people rights, or do
people give themselves rights? Most legal systems get these all confused and mixed up.
The government has duties and rights, the difference between different legal systems, is
the differences in the rights and duties between them. Both in reality are the rights of
power, that exist in this world.
•

Natural rights are the rights that an individual person has to do whatever they
want, so long as they don’t truly harm others

•

Positive rights are the right of government to do whatever it wants so long as it
protects and doesn’t harm its citizens.

Some people think that Americas first amendment gives people the right to free speech,
religion, press, and peaceful assembly, when in reality it doesn’t. The bill of rights
constrains the power of the government to take people’s natural rights away from them.
The bill of rights are all positive laws enforced against the present government by a
more supreme government existing in laws. Americans at the time of their founding,
believed they just had rights, that God gave them, and if anyone were to try to take
them away, this was justification for conflict. If you want rights as a citizen, you have to
take them, and reduce the power of government above as much as possible. All
centralization of power is a threat to individual power, which is by nature spread out and
divided among many. Governments have the right to do anything they want, laws exist
to constrain them, and define how they use that power. In an age when people have
forgotten the basis of rights, they believe the state gives them to them, because the
state is their God and highest form of power.

US SUPREME COURT

To understand the US supreme court is not that hard, if you understand the law in this
way.
•

Anything that grows the power of the state is 90% most likely unconstitutional,
and anything that gives rights to the people and their communities is 90% likely
constitutional.

•

If you are dealing with international affairs, and then the government can
basically do whatever it wants, even slaughter entire countries for sport and sell
their bodies for gold.

•

The US government owns the borders between all states, and the border of the
country itself, and it has absolute rights over these things. Inside states, the
states own all the land, and can do with it as they please. States can just take
anyone’s land without any reason necessary, because property is an illusion.

•

“Property Rights” are more good contract law with the government. There is no
protected right of property in the United States.

•

Taxes are rent payments. The government taxes things, labor, and people, which
means they own you, and have the right to collect rent.

Anything that can be

taxed is not owned by the person being taxed.
•

The fundamental tension between the left and right side of the court is whether
Jesus or the state is God.
o

Those that see the state as God, see that the future is created by
government planning and vision, and that no progress can emerge from
human beings unmanaged.

o

To those that believe Jesus is god, they believe individual choices create
the future, and a holy country is best at achieving the future.

If Americans would like to have the right to own property, they could pass an
amendment to the Constitution, and that would make all property taxes and income
taxes illegal. If you are an American and you think you own your own home, then why
is it that the government can tax you for owning it, unless they actually own the land
and are just renting it to you? Clear definitions of what Government actually owns and
doesn’t own are not clearly stated, because people would seriously constrain that
power, if they understood what it meant to be taxed on something.

Most everything the current US government does is fundamentally unconstitutional. In
the past, they had to pass amendments to the constitution to enact any large changes,
and currently such large changes can be done with barely even voting by the congress,
much less using an amendment. The government took over the whole health care
system, and made a system that would lead to universal health care, and didn’t even
try to pass an amendment to the constitution, and in the process, led a country to near
civil war, and at present in my time a brewing fundamental war against the very system
of the government.

THE ILLUSION OF RIGHTS

Rights can be a constraint on government power or a duty that it must perform
with its power. These rights live in inherent conflict. Rights are only about
government power and have no real individual basis.

Most of humanity at a local level of human organization live in barbarity and with
absolutely cruel relations between them. Stoning “unclean” women to death, is a

“natural right” in many societies. It is easier to reform bad laws, by appealing to an even
higher form of law, that can rule over the flawed local one. The more we turn to central
government power for necessary survival and to overcome problems locally that won’t
go away, the more we lose the power to adapt change and grow. Rights are a bit of a
silly thing, that most people have very different ideas what they mean, at the most
fundamental of levels. The reality of rights, is that they come from governments, they
come from power. Good uses of power connect into and understand human nature, and
the fundamental humanity of the people they govern. Local power is far more connected
to immediate human emotions and human nature, and thus a far more personal form of
rights, closer to the individual. All humans since we first existed have lived in
communities of people with rules to govern how they behave between them. Making
rules for people that go against their natures and undermine human dignity, just don’t
work.

Good laws embrace humanity, and its fundamental nature. Bad governments try to
change people into things the government wants them to be, so they can be controlled
easier, and follow a select few peoples’ vision of reality. Human civilization flourished
when primitive local rights were subsumed by grand collective societies and empires.
The rights that individuals feel when free of government are illusionary rights, and they
are in reality a product of their relationship to the communities they live in and that
community’s rights to control them as individuals. Natural and positive rights are a
conflict between local power and more universal centralized governmental power. There
is at some level no such thing as individual rights, since we as people never actually
exist as individuals. Local power vs central authority, is about the only real conflict that
exists in rights and law itself.

GOVERNMENT DUTIES

“Positive Rights” or “Modern Rights”, are the duties a government has to its citizens and
it is expected to provide.

The government should be as big as possible, and do as much as it can for its people. If
it tries to do too much of one thing, it fundamentally limits how much it can do of
another. The more the government wastes on one thing, the less it has to do other
things. If a country could get twice the results for half the price, for anything, it should
pursue that. Massively inefficient systems undermine a country, and the effectiveness of
government, no matter how noble that system may be, and no matter how much good it
does. It is difficult to measure the damage done to society by the things that never had
the opportunity to prosper. Governments main duty is to protect our lives as citizens,
support a prosperous society, and contain the savagery of humanity. Military, fire and
police services are the minimal positive rights. Politics is a disagreement over what
duties should be provided to its citizens, and what should be left to freewill and human
choice. All economic growth comes from freedom, and if the government takes all
freedom to provide for everything, there won’t be an economy to pay for anything. If
you think the duty of government is to make the most free and prosperous country you
will find another government whose duty is to make its people happy, healthy and
connected, to be the most disgusting possible government. Government that makes
happiness a duty, has to define what happiness is and eliminate human freedom.

Few issues can more polarize people’s views on politics than medicine. It gets at the
fundamental ways people define what it is to be human, and their idea of what a
humane society should be. For many, a society that lets its citizens die from disease is
failing in its duties; a government that makes a socialized health system undermines its
countries prosperity and economic future. Finding the means to protect all people from

death and not undermine an economy is a very tricky feat. Government duties to
provide healthcare of their citizens can be structured on very different principles.
Protecting them from death, and major illness, is fundamentally different than providing
for every possible thing they need or protecting them from every possible unhealthy
thing. A society not fighting for the lives of its citizens is failing. A country paying for
healthcare for the bad decisions of its people and actually increasing bad behavior, is
failing.

Governments at the large scale, with positive rights governing how they think, are
judged on how organized, civil, and healthy their citizens are in that country. Democratic
socialist countries are often judged to be the most superior. They have good trade-offs
with success and overall social health. There is an inherent decline in overall possible
prosperity in these countries that leads to inevitable collapse. Economic growth is a

central duty of a country, and no government can actually run an economy or make a
business that actually works. A single percentage point less per year in GDP growth adds
up into an enormous amount of lost money over enough time. In communist societies
that difference between potential growth and real growth could be over 6%, which is a
staggering sum of money over just a few years. You can double the entire wealth of a
country in less than ten years with 7-8% GDP growth. The cost of lost economic
opportunity is easily hidden and its victims have no face to attach them too.

DECENTRALIZED BUSINESS INNOVATION. TECHNO-PIRATE
COMPANIES.

Human nature is biased to organize around certain types of political organization. As
best as science can tell, people are born left wing and right wing, with tendencies
hardwired into their basic cognitive structures and how they see reality. Any type of
person can be any type of political affiliation. These cognitive natures only make
inclinations. Then within the left and right, we can be more authoritarian or
individualistic. Humanity has four intrinsic ways of politically organizing, that exist in
inherent tension and disagreement. We evolved a diversity of ways of thinking to adapt
to and organize the world, because different kinds of thinking are advantageous in
different situations. If anyone type comes to dominate a system, that system becomes
unhealthy and people resent the government.

People have to learn how to integrate all 4 into an effective government system, and not
blindly try to impose their own system on everyone. We don’t have to have a
government that treats everyone the same, in order to be fair and functional. You can
see these basic forms of power laid out in my basic descriptions of the 4-different ethical
and moral systems, in Chapter 3. What made the US government so successful is that it
was a fusion of the left and right working together, to make a functional government.
They were anti-authoritarians who rejected centralized power, and depriving individuals
of freedom, while also being upper-class elitists. Those that love freedom and resent
state power, live in great tension with present day modern governments. There are
some simple things the government could do, to make this group of people happier and
contribute to society on vastly larger scale, while not upsetting or changing the lives of
those that like being dominated and told what to do by others.

Deregulating three main industries would great increase the happiness of freedom
seeking people, and let them make any kind of business they wanted. Medical, finance,
and small business start-ups, are places where more freedom would benefit everyone,
and radical changes are unnecessary. There needs to be a space for just totally free
businesses whose business practices only effect the people that choose to use them.
Deregulating highly polluting industries or ones highly entangled with international
affairs are entirely different sorts of issues to deal with. There could be businesses that

just operate outside the legal system, and don’t use any government systems for help or
structure. Customers have to make a choice if they want to use these “unsafe”
companies or not. If you eat food from an unregulated street vendor, you are eating at
your own risk, and should have a right to live with the consequences freely. These sorts
of businesses need to be labeled like cigarettes: “This business is unregulated and can
kill you. Only their word and their promises can you hold them to”. Murder, fraud, theft,
and slavery, are still illegal and these businesses must be honest.

Nearly all problems that can happen in these person to person (p2p) businesses can be
dealt with in the contracts they use to run these companies.
•

Normal disputes can be settled outside of courts with private arbitration, that will
simple look at the facts of the case and come to a binding settlement as fast as
possible. The kinds of arbitration service a company uses can help determine even
what sort of companies you do business with. They must clearly state such things
openly and be easily seen.

•

Most business can be monitored and overseen by private inspectors and people can
pick the sort of businesses they deal with, by the quality of the inspection services
they use. Inspectors have every reason to maintain their reputation and brand name,
because competition can easily step in. Fraud and malicious companies and services
can be stopped with privatized systems.

MEDICAL SYSTEM

Innovation happens in spaces with the most freedom and least government intervention.
We can radically innovate medicine by creating free spaces for individuals to do

healthcare however they want, and have them live the consequences for themselves.
Often the worst effective solution is the best solution for most people. Increasing supply
is the only way to decrease costs, and the only way to increase supply is to have more
medical workers, medicines and services, and the only way to increase that supply is to
allow lower quality solutions compete with higher quality ones on an open market. Let a
certain part of society buy any medicine they want, from any doctor they want, from any
source they want, without any regulations. The only thing they need is contract laws and
rules against fraud. They harm no one in taking medicine made in another country that
is unregulated by America, without the permission of government approved doctors.
They will do this at their own risk, and it is no different than people thinking marijuana
and alcohol should be legal. If laws against narcotics don’t work, then laws against real
medicines certainty don’t work.

You can have universal health care, a regulated state medical system, and a completely
freedom based anarcho-medical system, at the same time. Any country with universal
health care could make a pirate healthcare system legal to operate in their country.
There is no reason to not allow people in any country, even ones with socialized health
care, the freedom to arrange their own medical system, that doesn’t use any
government regulations. These different systems will help feed into each other and make
the overall medical industry more efficient. If people want to exist outside the system,
they should have the right to, and their innovations could launch huge new tech
industries. A revolution in medicine can only happen in a free economic system, where
companies can just do what they think is best and experiment. People can use their own
personal judgement to choose which sort of medical services they want. They can go
with safe, static and old or vibrant, evolving, and risky, based on their own needs.

The first western country to really deregulate their medical industry for those that want
to live outside of it, will have a tremendous business opportunity to make world
changing global tech companies, and bring radical advancements in health to the human
race, everywhere. They don’t even have to undo their existing system, or threaten the
safety and ordered society of any of their citizens. In many places, even with this
freedom, many people would not risk or even try a totally new kind of way to get
medical treatment, and they won’t be forced into such a system. Only in place where
people want that, and would dare try, would a market and new industry grow and
prosper. As people see the positive results of such a system, more people will want to be
involved in it, and it can grow gradually with success, and not in any sudden
revolutionary way. Seeing results will lead people to adopt such a system, and no force
or manipulation is necessary.

You can see it readily by just imaging big tech companies or large pharmacies organizing
a freedom based medicine system. Different companies will appeal to different customer
bases. If you got medicine through Amazon, you would probably get home based
medical tests mailed to you, talk to doctors online from home, and get medicines mailed
to you at the lowest prices from the best sources in the world, with no boundaries
between countries in selling medicine. If it was Walmart, you could imagine going in
person to a store, getting blood drawn in person for testing, going into a private booth
and chatting with a doctor by video streaming with devices in the booth to help examine
you, where the pharmacy could make up your order, and give it to right there.
Companies we trust, can make new systems to serve us and keep us healthy, and would
have zero reason to not do their best to provide the greatest services. All the start-ups
and people going to work in them, will be driven by a desire to change the world for the
better and help people, for the most part. Creepy companies, and creepy technology
don’t survive long.

The price of the exam and medicines would be vastly cheaper than just a prescription
you get now. You could get an online medical exam for less than $10 from a qualified
doctor. Both systems could be maintained and monitored by the highest quality call
center standards and have outside inspectors checking them non-stop. They could be
90% cheaper than what we have, and be vastly safer, with lower quality medicine and
lower quality doctors. Not everything needs the best to be cured. With massive increases
in supply in doctors, medical services and medicines, prices by nature of supply in
demand, will severely drop, and fall every year. We can expand this slowly even into
medical procedures and surgeries. Now most people for life and death surgeries will
want the best services, and a socialized medical system, might be more what people
want with life and death issues. A medical system that protects against serious deadly
problems, is far less an intrusion on freedom, than one that monitors all. We can keep
this socialized system in check with a healthy free system, running alongside it. People
may find buying insurance against death, that provides top level services still preferable
to socialized health care, because it can be faster and more adaptive. All depends on
individuals. Universal healthcare itself will evolve and focus more on the real duties the
state has, rather than just controlling everything.

FINANCIAL FREEDOM

Allow for totally unregulated banking and financial services for people to use, and power
them with crypto-currencies, to create a financing and internet revolution. This will
create backbone financial systems to run most all online tech businesses, and companies
of the future. Being able to move money around freely and instantly through a system,
will have extreme benefits for tech development. People will have completely free will to
choose to use such systems, and most of the people able to even use such modern
finance, will be fully aware enough of the system to make an informed decision, and not

be cheated. Using money with no government backing has extreme risks, and it presents
an opportunity to create new ways for money to be used free of all previous constraints.
In a narrow part of the economy new models of economic behavior can be experimented
with, and can possibly develop into world changing technologies. We can’t deregulate
after there is an effective alternative, because it can never truly develop unless there is
the freedom to make a new system freely.

Governments are presented a great opportunity to strengthen their own financial
systems and currency with such new freedoms. If the new money takes off, a
government can just buy up parts of it and convert that into its own currency, and then
underlay the state currency with a more vital and free virtual currency, in a gradual and
steady manner. Government don’t lose the power to inflate and manipulate currency.
The new currency though can create a different kind of reliability and performance for
companies, that can’t exist in the present. Imagine a world with no large banks being
necessary to power finance. All the services would be online and require no physical
banking buildings, atms, and infrastructure. Banks require tremendous amounts of
money to run, and nearly all those costs get past on to customers and tax payers. Purely
online ones will develop slowly and only deal in narrow things they are good at, and as
innovations develop can expand and create a completely new modern feeless banking
system, that is incorruptible. It will have new risks and not provide all the same
advantages of the old. If people want to pay the higher costs of old fashioned banking,
they will have the freedom to do so.

ANARCHO START-UPS AND A NEW LABOR UNION MOVEMENT

One of the great ironies is that unionism is best served in a system with the least
government power. In modern societies Unions mostly exist in government jobs and not

in the private sector. Private work force unions could have a new revival if they changed
their form to better match a new political age and economics, and not relying on
government force to achieve their goals. Large amounts of government intrusions on
business lead to more expensive products of lower quality and less people able to create
a company and jobs for other people. As unions pushed for more government control,
they killed the very companies they worked for. Unions didn’t die, the companies they
worked in died.

The freedom to make small businesses that provide services to people locally is the key
to creating a new Union movement. The freedom to make small businesses with no
intrusion allows them to be created and organized based on any set of values. If people
want to buy the values you are selling, they will buy your product more readily.
Companies able to form with less regulations can self-regulate themselves and use less
resources to start their business. More cash strapped areas, can start a business with
less capitals. Groups of people can work together to fund, start, and run a business
together. The regulations themselves make it so only those with access to large amounts
of money and more formal business experience are able to even start new businesses.
Every regulation and new imposed cost, makes a new business less likely to exist, new
jobs less likely to be created, and poor people less likely to create something for
themselves that empowers their lives and those close to them.

Not all companies have to be high technology and advanced fields, like engineering,
programing, medicine, law, and finance. As we deregulate more industries newer kinds
of companies and businesses can come into existence and serve people. Change and
rapid development can’t happen in regulated economies. One of the ways to regulate the
quality of unregulated businesses, is self-regulation and outside inspectors and
standards. We as customers will need to become more aware of the sort of companies

used to inspect industries, and go with the ones we trust. Food service with no
government or private food inspection would be questionable for anyone to eat. You may
actually get safer food with a private inspector, than a government one, because they
are highly motivated to create the best reputation for the inspection company, and
empower companies to be sincerely trusted by customers. People like making money,
and no company has any motivation to hurt customers and lose business.

Small companies simply can’t organize massive misinformation campaigns to manipulate
society. They are connected to their communities and make money by how much people
feel locally connected to them. Build up your communities and social connections, and
use this to drive a local business, that people want to see succeed and feel an emotional
connection to, while delivering superior services at competitive prices, in order to
succeed. Capitalism is the freedom to use whatever value your system you want. People
just prefer cheaper over more expensive and this creates a pressure on companies to
compete in ways that normal people just don’t like. Modern technology can help run
small business at lower costs and make the overhead for all the internal management
costs vastly cheaper and with high tech tools that can drive constant business
improvements. When people fail, it will not be easy on them, and not everyone has the
heart and will to make a business, even in a big group.

People have to get licenses to do just about every job. New shops in a city have to get
permission to open, and not cause competition with existing businesses. You can’t go
selling flowers on the street, when florists stores go complaining to the government to
arrest you. Much of what you will see is utter chaos and businesses opening up out of
vehicles and right on streets curbs. It is not pretty and offends the eyes of those that
like ordered and disciplined societies. You can imagine and inner city of a western
country covered in street businesses, food, music, local art, dance, creating a local

energy and space that people want to go into and engage this freedom and new vitality
of culture. Poor areas could be freed to do whatever they want, and open any sort of
business they want, and this will draw in customers as these business hustle with
customer service and personal connections. Often the finest food comes from the
humblest locations and from people most in love with life, people, and freedom.

It is better to allow certain areas freedom, rather than let them be desolate and
regulated centers of hell in utopian western empires. With freedom, the kinds of ideas
and innovations that people will create will be unimaginable to a single person’s mind. In
an age of new technology, new ways for businesses to be run are emerging that make
highly decentralized small business competitive with bigger and more organized
companies. Online marketing can connect customers and business together in deeper
and more complex ways, that no large company ever could. Fast food chains might
become things of the past, when you can get the best food made at the lowest prices
from real people, that you respect and want to see succeed.

CHAPTER 8: THE ORIGIN OF CONSCIOUSNESS

HUMAN EVOLUTION

Humanity is different than animals. Human evolution is different than the evolution of
animals. We come from animals. We evolved step by step from animals, and we are still
animals. The vast majority of the evolution that created humans, is no different than
what created all know life in this universe. Our sentience greatly influences how we
evolve as a species, and human evolution works in a different way than normal
evolution. One day something changed, and that allowed us to evolve ourselves.
Sentience has evolutionary value beyond just intelligence, because it can control and
shape the evolution of human beings. Humans gained a power to control their own
evolution, and direct this towards a purpose and sense of meaning. We can manifest our
identity and self into things, and have things manifest identity and self into us. Our
sentience is itself evolving, through culture and how we organize ideas, where only
certain things can work and prosper through time. Sentience is the root of technology.
We manifest our living minds into things, and those things manifest into us and propel
our prosperity.

I would hypothesize that, sentience could arise gradually out of our sense of
what is human and not human. Our sentience is an emergent property of instincts,
and very specific aspects of our cognitive biology. It isn’t just some random feeling of
self, that we have, it has at its root a conception of certain aspects of reality. This is a
sentiment that could develop from very basic levels, and gradually develop into
something what we call being human. The instinct itself, is independent of the content of
humanity. Being able to recognize members of your own species, can evolve step by
step, into more specific and complex things: species, group, family, basic needs,

hunger/fear/danger, good member, bad member, similar to you, different from you. A
sense of self emerges from objective reality and observation, that encodes itself
sequentially through generation after generation of evolutionary adaption. This system
projects itself into things in order to see if it is similar to your or not. This system then
could evolve into projecting into things beyond even humans and see “humanity” in
things. Sentience is the moment we can see things as human and change them into
more human and useful to us, rather than just social animals imposing social order into
other members of a “pack”.

We had this feeling inside of us, that we call “humanity”. This is the most magical and
wonderful feeling that we can have as human beings, it is filled with everything we
consider good and noble. It is nearly impossible as a human being to step back and
objectively look at this sentiment, and its primitive origins from our evolution from
animals. We don’t truly control this instinctual and primitive sense of humanity. We can
deepen and broaden our conception of humanity, while never really changing its root
reality, that exists inside of us. We all grow up with different life experiences and will
value different people and different cultures, as more human to us. Beyond the surface
cultural conception, there is a deeper inner animal like sense of self and not self. This
shapes how our sentience and sense of being develops at a day to day level of living. In
the end, humanity, is what survives, and survival must lie at the root of any conception
of being human.

In the definition of humanity, there is an inherent corollary, in what we call not human.
Inhumanness is something we label people with, not animals. To call a human being an
animal, that lacks humanity, is the most fundamental attack on a human being
imaginable. They go from a thing of divine dignity and beauty, to a thing that we can
smash, kill, use, and consume, like any other thing on this Earth. We create this intense

social in-group, and an intense social out-group, that we can kill. Human sentience may
arise out of our instinct to avoid that which is not human. In modern humans, this
aversion evolved into possibly genocidal instincts. We are by our fundamental nature
social animals. Only social animals can evolve into sentient beings, with feelings, and a
sense of self. If sentience is an emergent property of social instinct, then by the very
nature of social values and social formation, there is a root sense of who is a member of
a group and who is not a member. This social sense of belonging and group identity, in
sentient beings may at its root have a very narrow and specific way of thinking. This
instinct may be the only way creatures ever form into an ever evolving and growing
species. A sense of time with a directionality has its origins in our social instincts, that
give rise to our sense of humanity, and in turn create the very intelligence and sense of
self and reality, that we call sentience.

TELEOLOGICAL PURPOSE DRIVEN EVOLUTION

We direct our own evolution with purpose and direction. When humanity first learned of
evolutionary theory, and how animals came to be, they immediately made it all about
themselves, and in how we came to be as a species. Normal people conceive of evolution
in human terms; they conceive of it with purpose and direction. Many people took their
“human” ideas of evolution and applied them into society, government, economics,
family, and all other domains of human existence. Evolution made science and not God
the creator and ultimate judge of things. Power itself began to define how we see
evolution. It isn’t that the science of evolution was bad, it was that the people used that
science, to justify horrible things.

Evolution inspired tremendous evil in human beings. If were to judge evolution by the
morality it inspired in others, and by the things they did with that, then evolution might

go down as one of the evilest ideas in human history, along with communism. Marxists
themselves would also take evolutionary ideas of how to best evolve and develop
mankind, and then would go out to slaughter millions. Communism was the merging of
progress, science, reason and politics, and it ended up being the single greatest manmade killer of human beings in all of human history. Human evolution as we humans feel
it in our souls and from the reality that we see is something very different than the
normal kind plants and animals have in this world.

Animals evolve through random chance. There is no real direction to their evolution. You
can’t really describe anything in nature as more or less evolved. We can say things are
more adapted to their environments, or less adapted. We can think about bigger
concepts, like if a species has the ability to adapt to change and new environments and
not just to the stable one they live in. The capacity to change and adapt to the world,
defines life. Humans are different. We don’t think of evolution as random, rather we
think of it direction and an end goal. At some level religious people, reject evolutionary
theory, because they see it as inhumane, and not connected to the reality and sense of
being that they know. This was wise of them, at some level. We don’t evolve like
animals, that much, anymore.

LINEAR EVOLUTION

We domesticate things, and domestication itself is a form of evolution arising out of
human sentience, which tries to project its reality into the future towards an end
destiny.

Humans see evolution in a line. It is singular and directional. We evolve as a group. We
as people kill off wild human beings. We domesticate plants, animals and people to
makes us as individuals survive. A beaver builds dams to build their homes. Many
animals build and create things around them, as machines that extend into nature, and
expand that animal’s capacity to thrive in nature. We as humans seem able to build
anything around us, into something that reflects our own self, survival and being. This
capacity to consciously, domesticate our environment is the greatest power to ever come
into existence, in the universe. Consciousness, as an objectively measurable thing, and
is about how we shape our environment to our own survival. The patterns of our minds
and our thoughts are imposed into the structure of our objective reality. We can embody
humanity into things. We can replicate thoughts into structures around us, that in turn
can replicate and grow themselves. We can conceive of cities and systems that grow and
evolve like living entities, of concrete and steel that serve human life.

People that have more consciousness and overall awareness, have a greater
power to control and shape their environment. We can choose what we build,
measure the success of those choices, and modify those things, at any level, to
work better.

In evolutionary science, many people have tried to create collective theories of
evolution, where whole groups work together to survive. This is and will always be
bullshit. Nature doesn’t evolve with collective consciousness or some grand
interconnecting sense of being. There is no mother earth, no magic energy binding
people and things together. There is self-interest, competition, and brutal domination.
We imagine feelings and meanings into animals, trees, and the stars themselves, as an
individual function of sentience. Mother bunnies don’t love their babies. It is just
hormones and programming. People want to see in evolution a cooperation among

members of a group to thrive as a species. We create this delusion by projecting and
injecting our humanity into the environment. At some level, there is collective evolution
because we as humans through culture, our humanity, project a collective reality into
our social groupings. This can drive aspects of our cultural and cognitive evolution, which
then can drive our biological evolution. We are all so similar, so we project similarly and
are programed by others and the environment around us. The “humanity” in things,
creates us and, we in turn can create it, and this creates the tension between collective
and individual values.

HUMAN COGNITIVE PROJECTION

Projection of human consciousness into things, has an evolutionary pattern similar to
genetic evolution. It builds on itself through trial and error. Its code is virtualized into a
form an intelligence that can rewrite itself faster than genetic adaption. Our realities are
composed of nearly all things made by and altered by human will for human living and
being. The people and things around us create us, and we in turn create them. Humans
live in spaces that they modify and are surrounded by other human beings. We are
social animals, that by nature must be able to influence and be influenced. We impose
our internal mental structures onto the environment, and our very minds are shaped and
defined by our environments. We see ourselves in everything around us, and when
things don’t fit with how we feel, we want to change them to match how we feel inside.

We project our humanity into the sciences and into evolutionary biology. The underlying
origin of imagination and ideas to solve scientific problems, arise from our own internal
sense of humanity, and who we are as people. We push forward ideas that we feel a

deeper intuitive connection to, over those that seem disconnected from us. Intuitive
smart people feel good or bad about certain ideas, and the very structure of how their
ideas are formed, is based in how the mind thinks. The scientific method itself is a
projection of human thinking processes into a formal methodology that actually works.
Everything we create arises out of the patterns our minds can form.

We are animals, struggling to survive, ruled by biological instinct, hormones and innate
cognitive biology, that is all shaped by the environments we evolved out of and adapted
to living in to. Culture itself is just a reflection of the humanity we projected into the
physical environment we lived in, and that helped us to survive in that place. Different
cultures arise out of different environments and conditions. The delusions that arise out
of humans projecting human feelings into things that don’t feel, has a realistic limit, and
has to be more precisely controlled and contained. When we are faced with things we
don’t understand, we always fall back on projecting humanity into it, at some level.
There are some projections that end up working, and producing amazing results through
the ages of time. Most things felt are just absurd mental crap.

THE WILL TO VALUE

Nietzsche saw humanity as ruled by a will to power, and I think that is just one
reflection, of one aspect of what a human can be and express. A will to power can be
more properly be expressed as an innate will in a person to be individual and define their
own innate identity. This is only one half of the innate will of the human mind. A broader
sense of this will to manifest self into reality, and to experience the world as one’s self,
is a sense of value and not just identity. We can also possess a “will to value”. We can
have a part of us that is valued in of itself, from itself. The will to power and the will to

value are systems that need no external object to be what they are in of themselves.
They are the very teller and organizer of your story.

People are designed by humans to fit into a collective society. Evolution is guided
by intelligence and will, when it comes to people. We are intelligently and consciously
designed in our humanity, by humanity. Linear evolution is the conscious and intelligent
design of a species to shape reality in itself and around itself to nurture its own survival,
beyond just the flesh and blood of individual human beings. Sentience gains the power
to domestic both nature and humanity to its will, from primitive evolutionary processes
to sentient human controlled processes. The evolutionary process that leads to sentience
can only evolve from social animals, and is thus inherently social and collective.

We are not individuals that can survive on our own. Humans gain power in groups, and
can think collectively as groups. We don’t have magic powers to connect our minds
together. This “magic” is just a feeling in how a person can experience external reality as
an immediate and personal thing inside of themselves. When we see who we care about
in pain, we feel pain, and certain people can feel what that person is feeling inside, as
their own emotions. Our projection of self, and the projection of self from others, all
blend together, into something more. With close enough groupings of people, that live
together long enough, these boundaries fade away, and our certainty rises a great deal.
Social intelligence is more precise in closely bonded groupings of people, with little
change in their immediate surroundings. The more we know people the more detailed
and accurate our understandings of their emotions are at any given moment.

By our very natures we will always feel more humanity in things closest to us, and
bound to us in memory, self, identity, and life experience. Families that are close will
always be more human to each other than strangers. Humans evolved in small groups,

very closely connected to their own families, and culture. Everything in our world around
us, was simple, singular, and all consuming. Our parents can appear like gods in our
consciousness, even when we hate them, or have been dead for 50 years. We pass that
love and sense of being, self, and identity into our own children, even when we vow not
to be like our parents. This chain of family creates human existence and culture. Our
minds are built out of the things that created us. We are our parents, we can feel them,
see into them, and even be them at some level. Our communities, our land, our friends,
and our cultures, define us and create all the potential for us to exist as humans.

Our sense of self is created from before we are even born. People are different. There
are patterns to these differences, and they all come to work together, quite well.
Different people are better at different things. By themselves each person is not so
useful, together, they can do a lot. We as humans have specialized minds, that are
better at doing certain kinds of things more than other kinds of things. This cognitive
biology is far more elegant than what random evolution might “imagine”. If we were only
products of our environment, then we would quickly have everyone thinking and acting
the same, and thus we would not be collectively intelligent. That innate individuality is
foundational and irreplaceable in sentience and being. Without it, you are just a
machine, with no purpose, no meaning, and no future. We have an innate value and
identity born out our innate individual wills.

CONSCIOUSNESS

Consciousness has a consistent form that arises out of nothing and randomness.
Humans experience the world around them. The feel it in their bodies and beings. We
don’t see a rock on the ground. People feel that there is a rock on the ground, and try to
infer meaning and purpose in it being there. There is always emotion infused into our

sensory perception of reality. We can’t conceive of things, unless there is a self to judge
those things. Different forms of humanity can be projected into reality, to both perceive
it, and to control it. There is not a singular sense of humanity, that we as people project.
We have variety in people, and their different emotions are projected into reality.

Our sense of and control over reality must be based in reality. These judgements and
perceptions must actually work and correlate to the world around us. Our projection of
humanity and self into them, is not a distortion of true reality, it is realization of a
different kind of reality. Consciousness exists not just as awareness of being alive, it
exists of sense of being greater than, and innately bound to the earth beneath our feet.
We feel more than the world we live in; our own personal self is more valued than any
material thing in the world. We are not a thing, like the objects around us. Objects of
value are more valued than objects with no value. We infer value into things based on
how they affirm and support our own life, and how they connect into the future. Our own
sense of self transcends even our own body and being, where we can be willing to die to
protect the very humanity we identify and connect into. Dying to save your own child is
little different than saving yourself.

Consciousness is a framework of the mind that seeks to preserve the future over our
own immediate survival. We can sacrifice our lives for a sense of our own self living into
the future. Immortality itself is never a physical state of being to seek. It is a state of
mind and a way of living one’s life to the fullest and engaged in creating a future for
what you feel to be humanity, and which in turn sees you in something fundamentally
human. If our sense of value in things, is completely out of sync with reality, then a
person doesn’t live long, nor maintain social relationships.

Survival itself is reality. We care more about how people think of us, then we think of
ourselves, or even the things we can own. Social interactions have serious
consequences, if they go wrong. Our interactions between people have to actually work,
and make sense. Patterns of thinking that can’t form communication, that others can
understand, can’t be the basis of consciousness. Inside our own heads we talk to
ourselves, and this communication forms our identity. Brains have multiple personalities
in them that form conscious thought. The two sides of your brain are like two
independent minds. The more you can use both sides of your brain, the more ability you
will have in understanding and communicating, with other people. This is why women
are better communicators then men, because they use both sides of their brain and can
more innately understand other people’s thinking more. They learn language faster,
because they talk to themselves, and this in turn makes women more indecisive. Women
are more conscious and more able to manifest self and being into their environment and
in turn are more influenced and affected by their environment. This sensitivity, vitality,
and being define femininity, and make it something more innately human and worth
protecting than non-feminine life. Female identity and being is survival, and the tree of
sentience, from which all reason and thought emerges.

AN INTENSE AND VERY LONG AUTHORS NOTE

We seem to have innate structures in our mind, that greatly correlate to the highest
forms of thought we have developed as human beings. One of my core presumptions
that I had to make, from when I was a kid, was that a theory of the universe and a
theory of humanity could be solved with a single theory. This presumption is not based
on anything rational. I just wanted it to be true, so I made it true. My own desire to see
a cognitive model of human consciousness relate to the universe itself, is rather strong. I

am very skeptical that such a thing is possible, though at a root level, it just seems the
most obvious thing.

•

The way we run society, develop ourselves, build starships and understand the
universe, should all be driven by the same theory, because in the end it is the human
mind that has to make all these things and we exist and live in a universe, thus our
minds are defined and created at all levels from its reality.

•

We can only create a theory of the universe from our own minds, and that system
will be a reflection of human thought itself, because people made it. Our own minds
are themselves born out of existence in this universe, and it is consciousness itself
that can create a functioning model of reality in science, that will then itself need to
have a fundamental correlation and connection to the rules of the universe that
created it.

“Only possible things can evolve. What is possible to exist and evolve is
narrow.”

I came up with a clever trick to get around dualism, and magical thinking. Our minds
evolved into conscious minds with a certain pattern, because that is the only pattern it
could evolve into and form consciousness. Evolution comes from purely random forces.
Our minds evolve from purely random mutations. The mutations that work, are very
rare. Over time they begin to form into the image of something, that can actually work,

and get more and more refined in that system, through time. The sheer complexity of
human thought had to evolve from nothing, and be bound by something. We don’t see
reality; we see a simulation of reality. It has to correlate to reality, and the real world,
because if our vision didn’t correlate, we would die rather quickly. Our minds play tricks
on us, and don’t fully capture the reality of the world outside our brains. They work to
make us survive. They are formed in relationship to reality, and the very complexity of
the human mind is formed from fundamental patterns in the very fabric of space and
time.

We as people have all these variations in how we can see things. Evolution built out
complex mental structures out of a big mess of competing systems, that sort of found a
way to work. Personality is an emergent property of that, and evolved from how we
project our own identity into reality. If that projection doesn’t work right, then that
system fails. We are blank slates. It is just that the blank slate isn’t flat, and not all the
same texture. There is an innate terrain and geometry to the mind, that has inclinations
to have certain things imbedded into it more than other things. You can use the sort of
intelligence often associated with art and painting, to learn math, if you try hard enough.
Visual minds create more visual mathematics.

The fact that certain personalities can form amazing and functional theories of physics,
and that the universe can be intelligible by math, is one of the greatest mysteries in life,
that at some level, people just accept as being normal. Math doesn’t pre-exist human
imagination, nor is it some magical thing we discover floating in another reality. Math
that is useful to human beings, correlated to how we think, and actually works in the
real world, is the one that evolves and grows. It is functional shape and terrain in the
“blank slate” of the mind, that certain things, like math, form and imprint more readily
into. If people can’t understand it, and can’t conceive of it, then it doesn’t come into

existence, no matter how accurate it is in its descriptions. We can make math from
many different cognitive structures, and use it to fulfil very different human needs.

Most people don’t like math, because their personality has a hard time projecting itself
into it, and having math project itself into their minds. This is not a problem of math
itself, it is a problem of having too narrow and limited expression of what math really is
in its reality. It is a far more human, emotional, and meaningful field, than most people
know. In the end, we can only conceive of things we can project our minds and self into,
and thus our very selves, emotions, sentiments, and minds cognitive structure, at some
level must conform, and be structured on reality itself.

Our personalities define what is possible to create, because they favor specific forms of
thought over others. Emotions are not some random and arbitrary thing, separate from
reality, that we need to get over, in order to have proper and clear rational thought. We
approximate reality in our minds, and are not in reality seeing it, nor wholly knowing it.
Our feelings can be real and most often they are not. The mind has the capacity to
project self into reality and have reality project itself back into it. Sentience correlates to
reality, because if our sentience and conscious sense of self, didn’t correlate with reality,
we would die, and/or be absolutely insane. Insanity itself is when the wires of the brains
don’t conform to reality, and warp perceptions so that our inferences are all wrong.
Schizophrenics see god talking to them in how leaves rustle on a tree. Social anxiety
makes people infer far more danger in certain social interactions, then actually exist.

Emotion is the subjective experience of self into the universe. There is no separating our
reality from ourselves and how we feel about it. All objects in the universe exist as
objects, because they are defined by their use relative to human emotion. Our projecting
of our subjective self into things, creates things into meaningful objects that we can

study. We can only have objective reality if we infer usefulness in the things we observe.
Emotions themselves, our feelings are a form of information on the objective world, they
are information that translate the objective world into subjective experience. Emotions
relate to our survival, and interpreting our senses and reality in a way that favors our
own existence and propagation. Logic itself is an emotional construct. What we think of
as “objective” is really just inter-subjective, where we imagine how lots of people
independent of us would feel. More logical and objective people would be able to make
decisions not based on their own personal needs or survival, and this can be important,
for our survival overall, and thus that very “objectivity” must always serve a subjective
need and purpose.

The boldest claim I can make is this:
The initial quantum state of the universe, that is timeless, has nothing in it. Our
minds have the capacity to leap into this reality. It is the root of the human sense
of self and identity. To exist in this state, is to take a human mind back to its
primal initial state from which all conscious thought and being arise out of in this
reality. It is not a mental state that people like to readily enter or face, unless
they have to, or become a nun/monk. Being a hermit is not easy. The entering
into this state is ironically very emotional. In order to conceive of reality, we must
be able to conceive this state at some level in our minds. For at the root of all
thought, when we truly go into the deepest states of human consciousness, there
is simply nothingness. That nothingness is not meaningless. The very
structure of space-time is what influences quantum structures take form, and
inspire the formation of sentient thought. These are real system, real structures,
and not some magic thing. We will never be able to directly observe them, we
however can directly model them. Crystals form from the structure of space time,
in things most closely connecting to the thermal energy levels of space-time,
which are near absolute zero.

THE BODY AND FLESH

We are mostly not all that conscious in our thinking. Consciousness has a power to
control and change things. Most parts of us as humans, are beyond simple control, and
awareness. Becoming more innately connected to our bodies, gains us greater degrees
of self-control over our instinctual systems. Certain people are better at connecting into
their bodies and controlling them, while others are not. Much of the humanity in our selfcontrol over our primal and rudimentary instincts, has in itself different patterns. We all
know the different ways that people control their bodies, instincts and self. Our very
sense of our bodies and their primal instincts arises out the sort of human emotions we
feed into our body.

People that love power, and people that love social value and connections, will treat and
understand their bodies very differently. Everyone can connect with their body, they will
however come at that understanding differently based on the sort of personality and self
they can project into their bodies, and how their bodies own senses come to project back
into the mind. We can all be correct, in how we understand our flesh, all be different in
that conception, and still be approaching a more objective sense of reality. You can’t
control and understand you flesh truly unless you experience it as your own self and
being. You can objectively stand outside your body and look at it like a thing, or you can
subjectively experience it, in all its feelings, as you yourself. You can experience the
feelings in your body, as the feelings in your emotions. People that are more subjectively
linked to their body, are far more likely to have control and understanding of their flesh,
over those that examine it like an object.

Consciousness has to have a consistent form and relationship to our own flesh. We can
understand our own bodies as something personal and as self. Through empathy, we can
see how others connect to and feel in their bodies. We can see pain and suffering in
others very readily, when we are more connected to our own self and being. What can
be seen and understood, is only what the observer can see and understand in their own
self. Our bodies are extensions of our minds, and in of themselves reflect and generate
thought. This is possible because the bodies that more connected to consciousness, were
more able to survive. The mind shaped the mind body connection into a feedback loop,
that generates a holistic mind-body consciousness. You can most control your own self,
and not others. The capacity to project your identity into things, is most present in your
own body, and it in turn has the most power to impress itself into you. Survival and
sensation can’t be made independent of thought and self.

HUMAN CULTURE

We exist. We feel. We see the universe around us. We make rather accurate models of
how the universe around us works. We perceive reality in some form. We are not
evolved to see reality perfectly, nor will any life form evolve in such a way. Our brains
have many illusions in them, and our brains can be tricked. We have biases for certain
ways of thinking, that help us survive, though don’t necessarily relate to reality.

Human beings remember bad thing more than good things, because bad things are more
likely to kill, and thus making having more good experiences less likely or impossible.
Dead people don’t have new happy memories. The more likely one is to die, the more
they should be aware of bad things than good things. This is probably consistent with all
life that ever evolved into sentient beings, ever. Survival is the ultimate reality. This
“illusion” that distorts much of how humans see reality, and creates an unrealistic
pessimism, may be a quality of nearly all sentient life, to a certain degree. The
subjective requirements of survival inherently warp, and give rise to our objective
reality. We shape and name all things to the very human function and emotional purpose
they have, to use as people.

Sentient life though gains a new power over life, and survival. It can create new ways to
survive in how it thinks and relates to others, with culture. The sort of animals on earth
that can evolve into sentient life, are limited. Plants, and ocean coral are very unlikely to
become sentient, unless we give the earth another 10-20 billion years of time for life to
evolve. Our sun goes out in 4 or 5 billion years, so it won’t happen.

Living things with culture will have reached that point probably through a very narrow
and limited range of possibilities. Will a species with no mating, and asexual
reproduction become sentient, and have culture? Most likely not, because living together
with their own kind in close knit groups wasn’t essential to its survival. Rapid evolution
that creates highly stable increased complexity, capable of adapting to a diverse set of
environments, is itself a rare form of evolution. Evolution itself evolves and is made of
many different variables.

Culture will evolve in social animals, ones that raise their children, and have
reproductive mates. A certain “morality” will limit which sorts of life will evolve into
sentient beings and ones that will not. This morality is pure math and probability.
Certain conditions of survival are more likely with certain survival paradigms than
others. More “moral” paradigms will survive over time to produce a sentient creature.
This “morality” is bound by what is possible and not possible, and may have a very
narrow range of possible functional moral systems.

I am not saying all humans must have the same moral system. Within our
collective humanity will be a distribution of interrelated and connected systems
working in an equilibrium or in symbiosis. Morality is a not a function of
individuals; it is a function of collective groupings. Individuals survive or die,
while breeding in a collective gene pool and require for their own individual
survival cultural interactions with others. You could describe this as a singular
moral/ethical system that is distributed over a certain range of diverse human
groupings.

Fairness, is not just something just randomly evolved into our brains. We would never
have evolved into sentient beings with culture, without evolving by pure randomness

certain moral and ethical inclinations in our brains. Immoral and unethical animals won’t
survive as a sentient species. Imagine how long humans would last, if we modified our
DNA so our brains don’t have certain moral codes hardwired into us. Not all humans
have a sense of fairness and a sense of right and wrong, enough however do, for a
stable species to evolve. Most people now who don’t have such things, are brain
damaged in some way. Even sociopaths have certain “ethics and morality”, just not as
“warm” as we expect in real “humans”.

We also kill off humans we don’t see as human, and that we can’t trust. Sociopaths have
to be good at pretending to look like humans, and the ones that can’t and then go kill
people for fun, don’t last long. Though having a certain amount of functioning sociopaths
in society is good for its overall survival. There is a morality to them, and they can “want
to be” helpful to society. A group of humans will not have homogenous minds and
homogenous moral and ethical compasses. There can be a range and variety within a
group of humans, and thus make them more or less able to survive.

Whatever the case, there is a “humanity” in us that evolved out of randomness, and it is
a very rare condition, that is necessary for all sentient life. There are very limited stable
and progressively evolvable evolutionary paradigms that are possible for a sentient
species of animal in any universe, on any planet to develop. They will be similar. Morality
and ethics can evolve from pure randomness and yet possibly be consistent with a
completely alien lifeform on another planet, because those possible arrangements of
morals and ethics that work are nearly singular. There can be a universal “humanity” in
all alien life, though it would be vastly narrower than we may traditionally consider
morality.

At some root level, nearly all space faring species will have similar mathematics, even if
the notation systems are completely untranslatable between them, at initial appearance.
Binary math, will be something, every one figures out and needs to use at some level, in
order to develop their culture and technology. This is about the biological hardware that
underlays the cultural inclinations inherent to any sentient species, and not cultural
advancements like math. The ability to do math existed in people’s minds, before we had
math. Math has its roots in the cultural biology of the brain, and in how we render the
universe into something usable and meaningful for our survival.

(the dualistic reality of math will be in later chapters. Short version: dualism is
just the qualities found in the timeless absolute ground state, of what is possible
and not possible. There is only one reality. Absolute nothingness does have some
intrinsic qualities arising from probability. Nothing and something, is the only
possible duality for the universe. It is just that “nothing” isn’t exactly free of
certain qualities.)

All sentient life has morality and ethics. No advanced alien civilization, doesn’t have
advanced moral principles. I would even go as far as to say, all significantly advanced
civilizations of aliens across the universe, will have a shared “humanity”. Though our
communication systems will be so different, that it may be impossible to communicate.
Octopuses are the most “alien” intelligent creature on earth, and we can feel a certain
intelligence, and humanity in them. I feel the intelligence and feelings of an octopus,
when I see them, and they are in reality intelligent. It isn’t just projection. How to
communicate with a sentient octopus like species? I don’t know. I can sense a
“humanity” in them and intelligence that is beyond that of fish. It is an empirical truth
that I both feel, and can be proved by experiment.

Now I can’t project happiness onto “smiling” dolphins, without being an idiot. Their
smile is just how they look, and not an expression of emotion. This is just like how
“grumpy cat”, a cat with a frowning face, appears grumpy and we all know is not an
emotional expression. The seeming mental contradiction of these two things is funny
however. We enjoy things that feel more human, even if they are not in reality. An
octopus is more “human” than pretty flowers. Though pretty flowers might make most
people much happier to look at, and thus make the person feel more “human”, in
themselves, thus giving inanimate things a human identity, in their emotional function
and use to us.

TOOLS AND TECHNOLOGY.

Technology becomes an extension of culture. Culture and technology evolve now
independent of biological evolution, and for the benefit of biological life. If technology
and culture don’t work, they don’t exist for very long. There is also an intense constraint
on what is possible and not possible. Certain technologies must develop also in an
evolutionary chain, of increasing evolutionary stability and function, with ever increasing
complexity and diversity in those tools. Humans seem to try out every possible cultural
arrangement. Very few survived in time. Stability (what is possible to exist) and
complexity become forces that evolve culture, as well evolve biology and the laws of the
universe. Technology is part of the universe too.

Octopuses may never invent the wheel however, for a very long time, in their cultural
history. Pure ocean like species, may never evolve into a sentient species, nor develop
advanced technology. Many super useful things we develop require a chain of
developments to stack on top of each other. Dolphins for instance developed as land
animals similar to dogs, that went back into the ocean, their lack of hands will make

them evolving into a technological species, nearly impossible. Maybe if they develop
some sort of super tentacle tongue, they can have “hands”. Though in the water,
building technology wouldn’t really work as well on the land. Burning things with fire
doesn’t work well under water! Doing chemistry is really hard in water!

To a certain degree, certain physical conditions that life evolves in, will be different than
where sentient, culture bearing life, evolve. Life initially evolved in the oceans, and then
evolved into a land dwelling entity. Evolution on the land was much faster, and
developed vastly more intelligent creatures capable of bearing social connections. The
sea doesn’t change so much, as the land does.

This doesn’t need to be true to prove my point, it is however a wonderful thing for
someone to think about and explore. It is a mini thought experiment to work around in,
and go research the actual biology of this earth, and how it evolved. By considering the
limited possibilities of how life could evolve on other planets, we may be inspired to see
driving forces in our own evolution. Evolution is a purely random thing that will most
likely produce fundamentally very similar things.

Endoskeletons are more likely for sentient life, than exoskeletons. Carbon is a vastly
more likely base than silicon. Tiny differences in functional possibility create vast
differences in evolutionary probability. And oxygen, water, CO2 cycle for “breathing”
seems very likely to exist for sentient life. Breathing methane emitted from bacteria’s
farts, would be a sad life. Life at a basic level could evolve in a whole crazy host of ways,
beyond my imagining. Sentient life, will probably be more similar across the universe.
Space faring civilizations will be so narrow, as to be nearly impossible to exist, and will
probably be remarkably similar. I estimate around one star-faring species per 10-70

galaxies, where that even if we travel to every star in our galaxy and another galaxy, we
are unlikely to find even the remnants of a star faring civilization.

More stable, long lasting and complex universes, that are have longer windows
of time and more places, hospital to life, will in general have more technology
and more advanced culture over time.

THE GENOCIDAL INSTINCT

Warning this section is unsettling and very disturbing, even to the author. Like
the section on slavery, in part 2. These sections took an extreme emotional toll
on me to write and attempt to objectively lay out for the reader. I don’t want to
impose a moral framework on these things.

Idealism over perfecting man, drove modern eugenics and social Darwinism. These are
repugnant aspects of human culture, that in order to control better, I push forward this
idea. I don’t want to advocate genocide or creating a more civilized and better human
being. I want to open up a deep introspection to find those genocidal instincts within
ourselves, so we can better understand our own humanity and how we came to be. Our
very idealism, and warm feelings may have in their genetic primal roots, a drive to kill
and slaughter.
