thinkers for such a school of thought. They are not atheists, and they are not religious.
They don’t seek to create a new religion and they don’t seek to end the concept of God
in this world. Another solution to rationalism and how to connect it to the material world
is the power of the human mind to embody itself into reality. Only that which can
embody ourselves into is real. “I think there for I am” can expand the domain of human

thinking into the reality of the external world, into the minds of other people, and even
into the stars themselves. “I am alive, therefore the world is”. The power to embody is
not the power to project humanity into things, and see them as human.
Anthropomorphizing is more a solution to the problems in Empiricism. Embodiment is a
more literal and objective creation of human thought into objects and into other people.
The means by which we pass on culture to other people, the way we domesticate plants
and animals, the technology that we create to serve our lives, the creation of thinking
machines reflective of how humans themselves think, are all issues of embodiment.

There is no radical belief in absolute truth that we as people can know. They can believe
a world greater than the shadows exists, and that it doesn’t really matter. The only thing
we can know of this world outside of the cave is constructed in our imaginations from
our experiences of the shadows we see on the wall. It doesn’t take an empiricist view
that shadows are all that we can know, it more focuses on the mind that does the seeing
and how the patterns of cognition themselves may structure the world outside of the
cave, and be that world itself. This is sort of the magical quality contained in such an
ideology, that our very sense of being and mind has a meaning that extends into the
very root and creation of the universe. The scientific challenge of such a view is to find a
way to make that be possible, and be testable. This book and this part of the book is an
attempt to do just that. Leap into the mind itself and create the universe from nothing.
In the end, we can only know what our cognition is capable of conceiving and the fact
that is can form coherent, functional and intuitive models of reality is profound empirical
evidence.

Our bodies living in this world, are shaped by this world, and thus must be consistent
with reality to exist and survive. We are created from billions of years of evolution and
there are simply too narrow of options for us to exist and have a functional connection to

reality. Embedded in our bodies and culture is knowledge about reality beyond our minds
capacity to ever conceive. We didn’t need to ever know why we survived, we just had to
survive. Our cognition is not adapted to control everything. Human conceit and pride are
more likely to kill you than save you, if we had such knowledge. We can’t change human
nature. We can’t ever really know what that nature is in any absolute sense. The
important thing for this kind of rationalist to focus on is creating things in the real world
that work, help people, make us more human human, and expand human survival. They
must embody humanity into our extended reality. If science is objective truth, and
technology subjective truth, then the difference between a Rationalist Materialist and A
“Embodied Rationalist”, is which is more important, functional technology or true
scientific knowledge.

There is a correct answer.

Chapter 10: Evolving Dimensionality
Note: This chapter is not meant to be clear or understood readily. Read at your
own risk. This is the most dangerous stuff you can read. You will be expected to
look up and study everything on your own.

The human mind is connected to something more. It arises out of the universe we live
and reflects itself back on itself. We as humans can feel the truth in things. This delusion
guides nearly all understandings of how the universe works. One of the truly great
puzzles of physics beyond all its mathematical achievements and workable models of
existence, is how any of this can even be intelligible by human created math and
thinking. We can make simple math equations to explain the largest and most influential
forces around us. Humans can even feel which sort of ideas are more likely to work over
others. Great minds impose their very self and being into the world, and create patterns
from their own being, that end up correlating to usable systems to predict and calculate
how things work in the world. This is “magic”.

We as humans can leap into reality itself and into other dimensions through the power of
memory and imagination. This is a guide to thinking in zero-dimensions and 4dimensions. In later parts, we will visualize leaping into black holes, white holes, and
emerging multiverses. The irony being that it uses the same trick to do both. The
hardest concept in this book, and maybe in philosophy is to understand what “nothing”
is, from a deep intuitive level. Empty space is itself a hard-enough concept. This goes
even deeper. When you can leap into a zero-dimensional space, you can leap into higher
dimensional spaces mentally. At the heart of this chapter is a very difficult to grasp but
workable way to conceive of reality in 4 dimensions. You must do it emotionally,
subjectively and from in yourself, and not as a separate and distant external observer.

After you get that down, we will go into the 5th dimension, as a real and concretely
observable thing.

Zeros and Infinity

Most of my childhood I considered numbers. I thought about what is zero, what is
negative 1, what is 1. The ideas they formed are the foundation of everything in this
book. Zero is an almost magical number. It isn’t even a number really. It is neither even
or odd, and you can’t add up more it, mostly. If you divide something by zero, you get
an indeterminate amount, it is just something you aren’t allowed to do. If you divide by
a number approaching zero, you get a number approaching infinity. Infinitesimals are
the tiniest possible amount of something; they are a single point on a line. Zero is a
point, it is an infinitesimal. It isn’t nothing, it just the smallest amount of something
there is, and that means something.

Zeno’s Paradox: The Oldie but Goodie
•

https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Zeno%27s_paradoxes

•

http://plato.stanford.edu/entries/paradox-zeno/

•

https://plus.maths.org/content/mathematical-mysteries-zenos-paradoxes

All of his paradoxes are just the same paradox. Solve any of them, solve them all.

Imagine a wall, and each step you take towards it, you go half the distance to the wall.
If you take a billion steps, you will never reach the wall. Solutions to this classic Greek

paradox are in some regards the beginning of physics. The idea of “Greek atoms” arises
out of this thinking. The universe has to have a point where you can’t keep cutting it in
half. An atom, an indivisible block of matter, is an obvious solution. You keep cutting
until you reach a minimum amount you can cut, and from there you have the building
blocks of the universe. The Greeks by logic alone figured out the existence of atoms, and
to another degree the things that make up atoms. They found the “pixels” that made up
the universe. There are indivisible blocks that can’t be seen, except at the tiniest scales,
like our computer screens. The bigger the pixels, the less step you have to take to reach
the wall.

Another way to solve this paradox is to atomize/pixelate time itself. As your steps get
smaller, the time it takes to take a step get smaller, and you can arrive at a set time,
and have no paradox. If you can manipulate time, you can take infinite steps to arrive at
a wall, in a finite time in this world. At each step, time also takes half the time, so the
more steps you take, the faster each step is taken. Smaller steps are faster than bigger
steps. Though for this to work, it has to have a set rate, that can’t be changed, and yet
can be different depending on where you are in space. Time in a really small space will
act different than on a very large space. 1 meter will have one time, and 1/10^50
meters will have different rate of time. There has to be a way to smoothly move between
each time frame and define each one as correct. Relative time emerges as a solution.
Time changes space. You can imagine this as two runners at different distances from
the wall shoot an arrow at the same speed at the same time, and they will observe the
other persons arrow moving at different speed and being shot at a different time than
theirs.

Another solution is to say that position is uncertain at a specific time. At any given
moment, there is a fluctuation of position, and that uncertainty contains a domain, that

can cross that line in a finite period of time, with finite steps. As you get smaller at a
certain point you can no longer define exactly where you are in a definitive and
determined way, the smaller you get, the more probability defines location. You could
make that as a modeling of a certain “vibration” of the universe at some level. That
“vibration” could also be described as time, or even entropy, depending on how you
wanted to build a solution. You could say that a thing can’t have a certain position on the
line, or rather that the line has no certain position to occupy.

Instead of looking at the person taking the steps and how long it takes them, look at the
line itself and the properties in it. We can look at Zeno’s paradox in modern terms as
exactly the same as crossing over the event horizon of a black hole. With pure logic, one
can infer from this paradox the basic philosophical structure of general and special
relativity and quantum physics. The line itself bends with time, and that in order to even
look at a 1 dimensional space, one needs to connect in a time dimension and graph the
approach to a wall on a line with a 2D graph, with one axis being time. As you move
along the X axis towards the wall, you go down on the Y axis, and curve. In a system
where you never reach the wall, and get as close to the wall as possible, the line would
curve from flat to nearly perfectly vertical (Need a diagram here). The curving of the line
is all described by time. So as your steps get smaller, you are altering time more and
more, just as in real life, as you get faster or increase in energy, you alter time. You can
also infer the basics of quantum physics, and the uncertainty of observation, and the
uncertainty in even the exact location of things at the smallest scales. Logic alone could
make these assertions possible, with just the right thought exercise.

The experience of time, is based on where you are standing relative to the wall, and
different positions on the line will see time differently. Two racers one slow and one fast,
will actually observe time differently from each other, as they approach the wall at

different times. While the person taking steps towards the wall would feel everything the
same as before and not think time has slowed at all, they would see the line getting
longer. A line getting longer and time slowing are an expression of the same thing, from
different perspectives, when you consider time on the Y axis, and space on the X axis. If
you really took the paradox seriously, you have to reach such an idea, though without
any empirical reason to believe such a thing, it would be a bit absurd. Shooting arrows
with different perceived times adds in a difficult level of complexity for a deductive
argument. A very unlikely theory of gravity could have been made from Greek logic that
would have been consistent with Einstein and not Newton, millennia before science was
invented. The sheer absurdity of the solution, is why people couldn’t solve this paradox
for so long. The fact that it how reality actually works, is just a simple product of reality
being consistent, and that one can fit a solution to the discovered science. Deductive
logic with some facts can inspire scientific experiments and new discoveries.

Playing with infinities is a “basic” part of physics and math. Thinking seriously about
Zeno’s ideas is an important part of any model of physics. Quantum physics is a
challenge of figuring out what you can quantize, what you can make have a smallest
possible size that can’t be cut. Matter can be quantized. Energy can be quantized. Can
time? Can space? Can gravity? You can play with a thought experiment and come up
with multiple solutions that can be correct. Is the X and/or Y axis pixelated?

An Empty Box of Apples: “Heisenberg’s Apple”

Let’s say we take an empty box, we seal and suck out all the air, and make a sealed box
with a perfect vacuum. There is not one atom of matter floating in its space. And then
we freeze this box to nearly absolute zero. The walls of the box will barely influence the
inside of empty box at all. There will be fewest possible box atoms jumping around in

the empty space. We then can encase this box in 20 meters of lead, and put it 1 mile
beneath the surface of the earth. This will be an isolated *space*. I have a question
about this box and what is inside it.

How many apples are inside an absolutely empty box?

The answer in physics is not zero. Zero as this idea of absolute nothingness is an
idealized concept that “doesn’t” exist in the universe, except when talking about
impossible things. Anything that is possible, has a possibility of existing. Probability
makes it possible for anything to appear anywhere at any time, with an actually
definable amount of probability. No box in the universe is empty, ever. There are no
empty spaces in the universe, and in all spaces, there is something, and the possibility
for something else to be there. Empty space radiates energy, from nothing. All possible
things have a possibility of existing and thus exist.

The smallest amount of nothing in the universe is still not zero. In that empty frozen box
buried in the earth, there is a probability of an apple being inside it that is so small as to
be impossible, unless you change the parameters of the “experiment”. If we had 2
boxes, we would have twice as many apples. If we kept making more and more empty
boxes we would have more and more apples. If we waited longer observing these boxes,
there is more chances of apples coming into existence as time goes by, though in each
second the chances are the same as any other second. If we grow this box to 10^200
times the size of our own universe, and wait over a time 10^100 years, an apple
appearing in that box is nearly certain, because it already did. I ate an apple today, so I
am mostly certain they exist, relative the existence of everything else that I claim to
exist.

Single points don’t actually exist in the real universe. Things don’t exist as exactly one
thing in one place. You can think of the smallest things as sort of making a dent in the
fabric of the universe. What we normally call a point would be more the exact lowest
point in that dip, and the sloping edges of that indentation are just the probabilistic
space it “vibrates” in, most likely. In physics though we have to say it indents all the
universe a little bit, and is partly part of all the universe at once. This is not some grand
mystic idea of everything being connected. It is simple logic that needs to work out so
you don’t get absolutes and infinities in the universe. Infinitely small things don’t exist in
real life, and if they did, they would make things more black than a black hole. The
whole of an apple is made of tiny non-infinitely small things. With Zeno’s paradox, we
can’t be sure if it is vibration or space-time warps that solve this, or that those two
things are the same idea. If quantum uncertainty formed the basis of space-time, things
in physics would probably be more consistent and logical. I personally have to go with
time being the uncertain and probabilistic thing, that creates pixilation in the universe.

Dualism and Nothingness

Nearly all mathematically minded people thinking about reality have to believe in a
reality separate from our own, where math exists and then imprints itself into our
reality. The classic book on this is Plato’s “Allegory of the Cave”. It is a story any
educated person should go learn, and isn’t that hard to understand. It creates what is
called “dualism”, there is the world we live in, and a more “real” world of perfect forms
that our world is just shadows of in comparison. Numbers don’t exist in our world and
can only be conceived in our imaginations as sentient beings. Our very sentience is a
god like capacity to stare into the realm of the gods and see the truth of existence and

divine perfection of creation. Science, math, religion all have their own “divine” realm
separate from our own, with their own parameters on it.

Scientific materialism, where there is only the world we can see, is the only correct form
of thinking to build scientific models from. There can’t be a spirit world, and there can’t
be a reality that we can’t directly observe. If it can’t be seen and observed in theory,
then its existence is irrelevant and must be disregarded. Even the past is an imaginary
land, that can’t be observed or traveled to, yet even the most astute of minds can
believe in that delusion. Time traveling into your own past is as possible as traveling into
a fantasy world made up by a British children’s fantasy author, with elves. The fantasy
world might be even more likely to travel to, than into your own fictional history,
because one doesn’t have to be all that consistent to be “true”.

The universe though is discernible with mathematics. We can describe nearly everything
in the universe with simple elegant math, and don’t really have a good scientific
explanation for why. There is still this magical quality to science, that needs to be
pushed back on. The hardest magic to get rid of in Science, is the magic that underpins
much of scientists thinking. We as humans have visions of reality, that at times, when
worked out, become the basis of the greatest scientific discoveries. We seem capable of
perceiving something more than the immediate world we see. Reconciling this is hard.
Eliminating dualism from even the most skeptical of minds is hard, if they take seriously
deep thinking about where things come from and the origins of principled ideas. We all
have magical fantasy kingdoms we think are real, no matter how wise, educated, or
skeptical you may be in your grand genius.

To fix this in my own naturally rational dualistic thinking, I made a dualistic universe that
can actually be observed and be knowable. Dualism seems real, because it can produce

profound results, so I defined dualism by making this world and the magic realm distinct
and clearly defined. I made the magic reality as small as possible for it to create the one
we live in. We have to imagine what is the smallest possible fantasy world necessary to
create everything we know. The past itself is so massive, that only the present is a bit
bigger. The future is even bigger than the present we live, and contains near infinite
multitudes of possibility. “Absolute Nothingness” seems suitable for the basis of the
“magic” in dualism, and all the achievements in rationalist thinking, especially if one
considers Buddhism and mediation.

“Absolute Nothingness” needs to have a minimum set of qualities that a dualisticuniverse requires. Nothingness has to have a minimum quality that all things can
eventually arise from. Instead of there being endless perfect objects or idealized math,
there just needs to be a simple quality that can give rise to all the other things. Like say
that probability pre-exists reality, while math as we know it, doesn’t, is a possible
configuration. Numbers don’t have to exist in this system, nor anything that we would be
able to normally label. Quantum uncertainty is something that can exist in nothingness
before time. The universe we see could then be built up from that state with a little
time. A rationalist would need to build a model that could do this and approximate all the
systems we see now, arising step by step from pure probability, or with an additional
feature. It could be one thing like probability or one more thing in addition to it.

Only possible things, and not impossible things, have a possibility of existence,
eventually with time. If nothingness has probability, then it becomes like an empty box,
if it gets big enough and enough time passes, the universe and all we see can come into
existence, in some possible way. Math emerges from what is possible and not possible.
The universe requires consistency as a basic law with probability. Illogical or
fundamentally inconsistent things can’t exist. More consistent things are more likely to

exist and thus exist. “Math” emerges as a property of nothingness and probability. It is
the smallest and most likely conceptual “apple” to emerge in a box. We as humans are
far less likely “apples” that clearly are possible to exist. Any sort of inconsistent life, that
can’t function through time, has a very low probability of existence, the ones that are
more consistent and can move through time, are the ones that live.

The question then becomes what is “nothingness”, and how did it create the universe we
see. It is impossible for zero to be perfectly nothing. All numbers and maths emerge
from probability, and their usefulness in time. Nothingness in a sense has two qualities
here, and they play the key role in how things can come to be. You have random things
coming into existence from nothingness, and only consistent things surviving. Evolution
and adaptation can arise out nothingness as products of probability and consistency.
Survival itself can become a selected for feature of the universe. Stable universes exist
more than unstable universes. Evolving, growing universes are more likely to evolve,
changed and become something more. Too much change, and nothing survives, too
much stability and nothing changes. Things that exist must be able to adapt and pass
something on into the future.

Time emerges as an ordering of reality. Time is an emergent property from nothingness.
Nothingness is just randomness, and probability, that contains within it the possibility of
time, and a more ordered determined world. Time is one event leading into the next
event, and causing it to happen. Causality itself is an emergent property of Nothingness.
Causality in the highest form becomes something more like evolution. One thing leading
into the next. That process itself has a nearly magical like quality that created the very
life reading this sentence now. We can know these systems, and judge them now. All
that needs to be done is to identify what is more fundamental to the universe and thus
which quality caused which quality, until you reach a quality that can’t have any cause.

The nature of a timeless nothing universe, where it is possible for time to emerge, is the
puzzle.

Zero-Dimensional Space

Going back to Zeno’s paradox, you can imagine yourself entering into that every
shrinking space as you get closer to the wall. As the space gets cut in half each time, it
gets smaller and smaller. It begins to approach a space with the dimensions of zero. If a
one-dimensional line collapses into a single point, it is becoming zero dimensional. A
single point has zero-dimensions. It is pretty simple, and also very hard to really see and
understand. You can visualize this by continually zooming in on a single point. Imagine
looking into a thing, and keep zooming into to smaller and smaller sizes, go past the
atom, go past quarks, zoom in past a photon, and keep going until even photons are as
massive as galaxies. Keep “zooming in” and don’t stop, and your mind will “descend”
into absolute nothingness. This is a mental state people can have, do have, and those
that survive are forever transformed by. No true mystic, nor saint, nor serious thinker
has not faced this mental state. It is a “space”, with no distance, no time, no qualities,
no form. It is absolute nothingness. A single point has the value of zero. A thousand
points added up, is still zero. We will need to reconcile an idealized 0D space, with one
that actually could exist and create the reality we see around us. A point on line, and a
point on a plane are equal, no matter how many more dimensions you add.

For a 0D point to really exist and for it to solve Zeno’s Paradox, a point must be able to
evolve into a higher dimensional structure like a line. A point is infinitely dimensional can
evolve into as many dimensions as possible. Instead of looking at the problem from an
ever-shrinking line, one can think of the problem as how to take a single point and grow
it into a higher dimensional 1D line. We need to flip Zeno’s paradox and its head and

make it about the line itself changing, and not the runner on it. A real world 0D singular
point contains probability and it allows for random things to emerge from it. At a simple
level, you can just imagine that a point must vibrate. It can’t be defined by an exact
location in the real universe; the size of that vibration is a fundamental feature of time
and space. It is partly the basis of quantum uncertainty and how lower dimensional
things evolve into higher dimensional things. This vibration has a set rate in itself and
yet changes depending on where it is in space; we call this vibration time, and that
vibration rate, the speed of light. Zeno’s paradox is a time dependent paradox, that ties
space and time together into a single thing.

Random spaces could evolve into higher dimensionality, due to uncertainty in their
position. If everything in the universe had a defined position, nothing could actually
exist. It would all be absurdities like 10/0: infinities and zeros. Real numbers and real
things in the real universe need to “vibrate”, be uncertain, and be random at the tiniest
levels, in order to have real position that can relate to other things. In the real world,
idealized math can’t exist as a real thing due to its absoluteness. A vibrating point
becomes a line, as that vibration is described by time. If you take fixed perfect absolute
point, it can never evolve or change into anything, and will never be able to contain
time, nor evolve into something else. By a point being uncertain, and containing all
dimensions, it gains the ability to change, and that change creates time, which draws
out and expands into at least a single dimension. A line is created by an uncertain point
mapping itself out. A vibration in a line, makes it into a wave. Zeno’s Paradox doesn’t
happen on a single line, it happens on a plane with one dimension being space and the
other time, and when mapped together is a simple space-time structure. Wrapping one’s
head around simple ideas can be the hardest thing to do.

We experience this nothing dimension from the center of our beings. It is not truly
empty, even though it contains nothing, because it must contain the probability of
something different, and the capacity to evolve into our universe. Understanding what
can exist in absolutely nothing, is a hard thing for a brain to wrap itself around. You can
feel it, at a personal level. It is known from inside you. You can’t know it in a concrete
material way. To feel reality, to feel time, allows a person to see 4 dimensions more
readily.

TIME IS A KIND OF SPATIAL DIMENSION.

To understand time, you need to see it spatially, as an expanding entity, that manifests
itself out in the universe. How it manifests itself, defines how change happens in that
region. Time arises out everything, and to see time, you have to take your mind into a
universe before time existed, and see the universe evolve dimension by dimension into
the one we live in. Time emerges from physical properties in zero-dimensional space, it
has a real structure that it comes from, it is a physical thing, and not an abstract
concept. Your brain processes time as a subjective experience and not as a visual thing
you graph. The 3 “space” dimensions don’t have to be what we perceive them as, and all
3 are related to different aspects of reality. Spatial dimensions themselves might be
forces of the universe expressing themselves through time, and not actual space, or vice
versa. This problem in dualism is not solved yet.

If you want to know where the literal past exists in the universe, it can be
embedded in space itself, that is expanding away. The very distance between
things, contains time and describes relationships in time. This is not an abstract
thing, it is a literal thing we can eventually observe and define. The structure and
patterns of time in the universe are just small and not observed with the eye.

Time is observed with clocks, and when we can get smaller and more accurate
clocks, we will be able to see the finer structure of time itself. Its larger structure
is just universal expansion, that is built out of entropy at the smaller scales.

A NOTHING THAT CONTAINS EVERYTHING

Zero is not an idealized pure nothing, it is defined as infinitesimal. It is a really small
amount. In the real world, “nothing” is zero and infinite. This is the basis of relativity and
time. There is one more idea to help bridge this all together. Zero divided by Zero, is not
one, zero, or infinity. It is all possible numbers simultaneously. It basically like drawing a
vertical line on a Cartesian plane that goes straight up. “Y” equals every possible number
at a certain value of X. This is a very important mathematical concept that comes up
often in math, and for the real world and in real life based math, is something that
should be and is quickly pushed aside and told to avoid.

Because 0 times anything equals zero, we can say the zero divided by zero can equal
any number.

A “Nothing Universe”, can simply be described by 0/0, where it is basically nothing and
everything at once, while simultaneously not being 0 or infinity. It meets the criteria for

a basis of mathematics and creating a universe from nothingness, for a minimal dualistic
system. You then can imagine a universe oscillating between numbers. Everything in
existence is just a number. A number line is just how you describe a 1 dimensional
number. You can have a “number plane” or a “number cube”, or even have a 1000dimensional surface describing a single number. A number is just a single point
anywhere in space, and it can have as many dimensions as its wants.

A universe existing before time would just rotate between different numbers, randomly.
Each number would have no relation to the number before it. Time arises from
causation, so a universe without causation would be a universe without time. Anything
possible could come into existence, and not cause anything to happen in the next
moment. This is timeless. There is no way to determine one event from another. The
sequence of numbers has no meaning. You have a universe, you have “existence”, and
yet it is nothing and timeless, while also being able to become any possible thing. This a
rough sort of proto-time. All you need for time to exist, is for a random number to
emerge, that could cause another number to exist after it, so that they are connected. It
would need to be a number that all other numbers could evolve and grow from, that we
can see in the range of possible “numbers” in our universe. It would need to be
something that could cause something, and evolve into something more complex.

If we look at basic numbers, the first number to come into existence in any math
system, would have to be one that all other numbers can be derived from. “1” can’t be
the first number. You can’t make -1 from 1. You can make 1 from -1. 1^2=1. -1^2=1.
Thus -1 is more primary than 1. If we take this a step farther, the square root of -1 is
the most primary. i^1=i, i^2 =-1, i^3=-i, i^4=1. Complex imaginary numbers are
more fundamental than real numbers. Then we need to consider Pi. E^Pi*i, seems to
cover most any possible number in existence, and has interesting qualities as a number
that can explain the patterns in our universe, and how all of math comes into being.

This is a pretty number, and probably connected to the first number to come into
existence. It has unique properties that would also make it good for creating a
universe. It has a kind of internal symmetry. Time needs a kind of symmetry to
form. There has to be more than one thing, for something to cause something
else. The universe has to grow for there to be time.

Leaping into New Dimensions: A Visual Guide

To really think in the 4th dimension, you need to exist in the zero dimension as
an immediate and personal thing.

If you leapt into a single dot/point, you would experience all of reality as all black or all
white. The subjective experience of a mathematical point is for it to be all of your
observable reality. You see “black” in every single direction, and not some tiny dot
graphed on a line. An infinitely thin plane is equivalent to infinitely thick or a 0-D space.
Absolutely nothing can’t be conceived from outside of itself. In a flat land, the universe is

infinitely thin, so you can’t enter into and experience the world how they would
experience it. There is this false sense of reality from observing it from above and not
inside it. You can’t be inside an infinitely flat plane, unless you change how you conceive
an infinitely thin plane. The flatness of flatland, is the very 0 dimension, the very
nothingness. The subjective experience of nothingness can be infinite thickness and
everything.

To make it simpler let’s imagine that even in a zero-dimensional space, that all the
known higher dimensions you know, exist in that space. You don’t have to get all super
small, and forget about being able to look up or down. You will still get to look all
around, and be you. You can look in any direction, for this visualization. Imagine you are
in the center of a sphere. The sphere is like a big movie screen all around you and at
any distance you like it to be. It can be like a movie theater that is all around you in
every direction you look, where there is just you and the screen. There is nothing in this
closed sphere, except your ability to see in any direction. 3d space is not grid like, it is
more polar coordinate like. A simple mathematical description is a sphere, with a wave
like line going from the center to the edge of the sphere. This model is how to
understand any sort of quantum model, and possibly how to understand particle wave
duality.

Zero-Dimensional Space

If you looked in any direction, you would see the same thing. All black. The experience
of nothingness is all surrounding and all encompassing. If you are that dot, then all of
reality is that dot for you. You are darkness or light in its entirety. Zero-dimensional
space is just all white or all black in every direction. Now this state is indeterminate. It
can be anything. It is both all white and all black, at the same time. You can look around
in any direction, and all is black, sometimes the screen will flash white. This is a real
feeling, that a person can have. It is a real state of mind to exist in total nothingness, a
true void, then you can find a single point, and change your experience of this
nothingness reality. This is just a point that can randomly flash, with no pattern or
structure. It just comes and it just goes. As you look around certain orientations can
create a white screen, and then in the next moment it is gone, and you can go search
for it again. If there was a pattern to the white, you would be able to follow and orient
towards it. Without a pattern, it is just a random sequence of white flashes that appear
at random points across the screen. It would be a bit like only being able to see the
white static of a TV screen pixel by pixel, though that TV static has an actual pattern and
comes from energy from the universe when first formed into light.

Some stare into a fire, or feel a single point in their body. They engage and become one
with the very thing their mind focuses on. It is contradictory to describe, and
experienced differently by many people. Just sitting in black void of nothing, is not good
though. The human mind needs connection. You can find the right things to connect to,
a clearer mental signal, from this state of mind. Meditation is taking the mind back
through dimensionality to a zero-dimensional state of nothingness. Prayer is an
orientation towards pure light, where it takes the mind towards a state of determined
absoluteness and the future. To live in a zero-dimensional reality is a choice of
perspective. Absolute white or absolute black. Meditation and the ying-yang symbol are
not random notions in human imagination and invention. To embrace total emptiness is
not something any one can just do. It is a highly dangerous mental state to be in, and
the mind protects you from it, for good reason. We naturally meditate towards a more
determined state.

1-Dimensional- Time

If a signal forms in the zero dimension, you can move into the first dimension. Your
orientation becomes a direction of movement, the signal you listen to at a given
moment, determines the future. If you lock into a signal that actual forms from all the
random ones in nothingness, you can make that signal become your whole universe and
reality the longer you can follow it and track it. It is like you find a radio station you like,
and it keep changing station numbers. You have to keep rotating the radio dial to find
the signal you want to follow. It is very possible that there is no signal even to listen to
and the rotations of that dial is just creating its own pattern and signal to listen to. Sort
of like a DJ scratching and mixing record to make music over the base music. You could

stare into tv static and looked at it pixel by pixel and find a meaningful set of information
communicated to you through time, or possibly not.

The flashing random signal now changes into a pattern. What you will see is oscillations,
of black and white. As you transition into the 1st dimension of time, you will only see one
signal, no matter where you look. Everything will be the same, no matter what direction
you look. It is sort of the most boring movie in reality, just a screen flashing white or
black. It could make a sort of musical like beat visually. It is however just all black or all
white. And nearly everywhere you look around, this “signal” will be the same. From the
outside, this is like a point that is just flashing patterns. In a purely graphical way it is
just a line with different sections of white and black on it. Time makes us experience
those patterns as a signal, that you can actually experience. If you look around, you can
find a specific point that is special, just like you emerged from 0D space. This underlying
pattern in 1D space will exist in all dimensions evolved on top of it. There are no
universes without time.

In this first universe, you will be able to see a future, see something fixed, and not
fluctuating that leads towards a possibility of greater stability. I think of this like a
guiding star out of darkness. A possibility for something, exists in a place of infinite
nothingness. In a universe of all black there is still possibility, there is only possibility.
There is vast nothingness undetermined. If the universe is white, then all is determined,
set and known, it is absolute, and unchanging. The only thing that could arise in it that
whiteness that would be different than infinite determinism, is complete chance,
complete randomness. A single black dot can form in the absolute whiteness, and it can
grow. It can grow into all of reality. Until all that remains in the infinite black is the
possibility for the universe to be determined again. A white dot in the vast distance
trillions of light years away, lies in a direction towards wholeness. That white dot in a sea

of absolute darkness and nothing, is the moment the universe gives birth to time. Time
is deterministic, and arises out of the pure randomness of empty nothingness. Time is a
direction in absolute nothingness towards everything.

Emotionally- You reach out from the darkness into the light. In one dimension, you can
experience time. You can experience change. You can orient your mind towards
something. You can orient a universe towards a state different than it had before, and
move towards it. Time becomes reality in the 1st dimension. It is both time and space.
You move towards something. Space expands and moves. To experience a 1 dimensional
universe would be to experience a universe that flashes between white and black. It
would be mostly black, with moments of white. Time gains its directionality, because
“you” can orient yourself towards what sort of experiences you want to see/experience.
You can focus on the white. Like in a universe of all black, there can be a white dot,
infinitely far away, that you can point yourselves towards. Whiteness is an abstract
thing, that your mind can conceive in nothingness. You can move towards it, and not
just see it. You can change reality by your orientation. Real life though presents many
paths to the future that are both similar and fundamentally different.

2-Dimensional Space and Time- A Line with Time

2D- In 2 dimensions, things get weird. Whenever we look around, the signal changes.
We see only black or white still. This is like being able to turn the dial on a radio to a
different station. Mostly as you look around, you will see all black. Though at certain
points when you look, you will see a massive amount of signal, and varying patterns.
From the outside. This you being able to move through a line and experience different
signals. There are many possible futures to choose from, where you are able to pick
from a stacked array of lines, and observe that. This is a plane with patterns in it.

“Straight” lines through that are a form of time, that you can experience. Your whole
vision will be black and white only. However, you can “rotate” and orient yourself
towards different sets patterns that actually seem to have meaning. This would be like
being on a radio dial, and you can change that dial to different stations. Most all the
ranges are emptiness, but as you orient in certain directions, you will see patterns of all
black or white flash at you. You can choose which patterns to look at more. You can be
drawn towards the brighter and whiter directions, where you can get a signal.

Emotionally, you gain free will to change. You live in a world of light that can change.
You can choose what “voice” you listen to, as you emerge from the depths of darkness
deep inside yourself. While there can be a future, change, evolution and growth, you will
still have to pick among the different signals. See who you are listening to in the world,
and move towards that reality. Some signals don’t lead far, others lead farther. In a
simpler universe, there is just one point, one god, one direction. This direction doesn’t
mean you know, or are god. Life will suck and be all darkness. That white point is far
from you, and can only help you find your way.

A 3-Dimensional (Flatland): 2 Space-1 Time

As you look in different directions on a flat plane, you will see different lines form
patterns of varying vertical parallel white and black sections. These lines will extend like
longitudinal lines on a globe. They are like pixels on a screen, but are the same vertically
and vary horizontally. This is what is to be inside that flat plane. From the outside, this
looks like flatland, and from the inside you are experiencing an infinitely thin plan, being
stretched out vertically all around you. As you rotate, you won’t just see just black or
white, you will see vertical bars of black and white arranged around you. They are like
pixels that go up and down vertically forever, that are stacked side by side. The

pixilation is caused by the time dimension and not the space dimensions. You gain a
form of peripheral vision, compared to the 1D+1 world you emerge from into this one. If
you shook your head back and forth in the 1D+1 world, you might begin to see this
2D+1 world emerge.

You can now experience a 2-dimensional plane with time. You will be able to recognize
things by patterns and codes they broadcast. And sort of “see” like we do now. If a blind
person had to walk around, and all they could see was vertical lines arranged in different
patterns, they could get around in the world, better than just the blind. They would have
depth perception like a dolphin with their ears. Though in flatland they could just rotate
360 on a flat plane, and not look up and down. Doors and corners, would be clear.
Distance could be seen. Would be sort of a range finder, one could spin around on one
axis. You could also have “color”, for what sort of thing it was seeing at a certain range.
You would be able to “spot” different things.

In this universe, you would have a better “memory”. “Memory” forms each of the
preceding dimensions. As memory evolves, dimensionality evolves. “Memory” arises out
of time. Time seems to create more than existed before, because it “remembers” and
builds on itself. You can virtualize the 4d world in a 3d one with enough memory.
Computers with more and more memory can virtualize more and more dimensions, from
its narrow 2-dimensional mind (1d space with time).

Emotionally- You can expand beyond yourself and the voices in you, and experience
other voices around you, that can also listen to other voices. You move into a reality of
human beings. On a flat earth, we can know others. We have depth, range, choice. The
land has shape and terrain, at a basic level. You have to walk and move in a world as
you follow a signal.

4th Dimensional Universe/Our Universe: 3 Space–1 Time

Evolving towards a 4-dimensional universe would be like, taking those all vertical lines
that you see as you go around, and then being able to look up and down. You still see
only vertical lines, but as you look up and down you can see different ones. Now you can
look in any direction, and see different vertical lines form. Vibrating your “head” around
will create an illusion of “depth” that will create an image. The vibrating of a world of
vertical lines shapes into a world of 3d spatial perception. A chicken can see 3d, with one
eye, by bobbing its head back and forth, thus why birds bobble their heads. Two eyes, or
even ears, can create an illusion of depth perception. 2 different images of vertical lines
arranged in horizontal pattern, can have a more traditional 3d spatial image arise out of
it.

When time is collapsed in a lower dimension universe, it can simulate a higher
dimensionality. Vibrations, probability, and uncertainty create the possibility for higher
dimensions to emerge from lower dimensions. The Zero Dimension has many properties
in it, that help create the evolution of all dimensions to higher level ones. In my
visualization, the very reality of 3d space exists in the zero dimension in how we
perceive it from the inside, and this is not some abstract unreal thing. It is what was
possible, and thus existed in some form, even if it did not exist discretely yet. Everything
and nothing are the same thing, and contain within this reality all possible possibilities.

To understand time as property of space, you have to connect it to the very expansion of
space. This expansion is not always in the same everywhere in the universe. This
expansion is also gravity itself. Entropy, universal expansion, and time, are all
connected. Though they are not the same thing. They are properties that arise out of
similar causes, most likely. Time travels faster between galaxies than it does in galaxies.
The directionality of spatial expansion creates differentials in time dilation.

Space is perfectly and absolutely flat, at all times. You can’t really describe space as
being warped. This is not really hard science or logic here. Just think about what it would
mean for observation for space to be curved. How can you have more or less space in a
set region of space? Is one cubic meter of pure vacuum not equal to another cubic meter
of vacuum? Our perception of more space or less space in a region distant from us, is

based on differences in time, as time changes between two points, the perception of
space changes. The man walking in Zeno’s paradox will never see time change for
themselves, though those on the outside will see him slow down.

We often think of objects all moving through space, and that space is expanding as
things move outwards. Rather, I think of space moving through things, because space is
expanding. “Curvature” arises out of “space” moving through things, and thus allows
space to act on objects at a distance. This movement and “expansion” of space, is
described by time, and is time itself. Time is a literal thing we can see in this universe, in
how the curvature of space alters how things move. Time is a tangible thing. It is
moving in physical directions in our universe. Time however can be traveling at different
rates depending on where you are, and you can record/observe that from a distance,
though never actually experience that directly. Light bending around stars, can be
described simply by time dilation and not the curving of space. Space curves at the
smallest level, as an infinitesimal. It pushes things towards other things, from
differentials in its volume on each side. It is like a radial wedge, where the skinny side
points towards the direction of gravity “pulling”, and big side, sort of “pushes” in the
direction space moves, creates a warping in time.

Spherical Coordinates and Expansion

The universe is far messier and not made of perfect clean math. It is something
you need to experience in order to understand, and not just contemplate as an
impersonal idealized object.

At a basic level the universe uses spherical coordinates and not Cartesian ones.
Cartesian grids make it easy to see everything as one massive connected entity.
Everything in the universe has a grid position. There is a fixed tangible realism to grids,
that people get attached to. They are simpler math, that our brains can wrap concepts
around. The universe is more like a wave, and filled with curves, and spheres. The shape
of what we see in the universe is not square boxes. We see literal waves and circles.
Nothing in the universe is a square, and the root ideas that formed the universe are not
squares. Radial/Polar Coordinates with wave functions, describes the universe better.
This is also means that there isn’t one universal grid, to connect things by one universal
standard, in a way. Just the mental shift from grid coordinates to spherical ones, is a
massive mentality change. The grid math is easier; the spherical curved lines are more
real. Luckily, we can convert between them easily, and do all our math in the easy
square grid way, then at the end of calculations convert them into more realistic curved
spaces. (thanks to Euler: 𝑒 "# + 1 = 0)

The universe is more like an indeterminate point, wave, circle, sphere, and
cylinder.

If a sphere intersected a plane, you would see a small circle, grow into a bigger circle,
then get small again. You would be seeing a sphere slice by slice in 2D space. A great

deal of our universe and the geometry one needs to understand, is how higher
dimensional things intersect with lower dimensions and appear to our eyes. These higher
dimensions are created by time, and thus can’t be perceived as more physical and
spatial things. Much of what physics does in its modeling is model time as space
dimension, so we can see it. A sphere is a circle with its size being bound up in a time
dimension. You can draw the sphere only if you progress through time.

The challenge then becomes what would a sphere be that we see in our universe be if it
was emerging from in a higher dimension of time, intersecting into our universe. It is a
sort of “cylinder”. You can look at the whole of reality as a cylinder, and each moment of
time we live in, as spheres contained within that cylinder. Its axis up and down it, is a
progression in time. If you stacked infinite spheres on top of each other, and separated
them by infinitesimal distances in one direction, it would map out a cylinder. If those
spheres were empty, and the surface of those sphere were infinitely thin, then they
would add up still, into a solid cylinder. This is a hard-enough idea, and it doesn’t even
get into the harder levels of thinking one needs to model it completely.

Spatial expansion changes how these cylinders express themselves. You can look at
expansion as a singular thing, as a sort of inflating ball. Where each moment in time is
just one level of inflation. This however doesn’t model the world well. You need to
visualize many balls all inflating, in a big sea of them. Each ball will have curvature, and
collectively be a flat expansion. The challenging concept to consider, is what if every ball
inflated forever, and in itself was filled with endless balls individually inflating. This
creates a kind of endless branching and expansion, that requires another level of
dimensional thinking. It isn’t just how much something expands from another dimension,
but on what branch of that expansion it exists.

Chapter 11: General Relativity and Einstein

Warmup:
Let’s say you are in space. You have 5 identical planets that are equally far away from
you. You shoot them with a planet destroying death ray (Star Wars 7). You will observe
each of these planets blow up at the same time, if you are at the death ray site. From
each planets perspective, they will see itself blow up first and each planet blow up at
different times, depending on how far away they are from them. Every planet will have a
different order of when planets blow up. Now the gods eye view is the planet destroying
death beam. It caused everything, therefore could determine a more precise level of
causality and sequence of order. If the gods eye view doesn’t cause everything, and isn’t
the root causality, then there can be no exact point in the universe that has a correct
view of what happens first. We often can’t ever observe the root causality of things we
see in the universe, and thus have no means of determining an objective truth, readily.

Causality and Locality

The speed of light is a constant in a vacuum. The study of this speed laid the foundations
of a revolution in physics led by Albert Einstein. A defined speed of light that is constant,
has radical and deep consequences for how one has to see reality. The speed of light is
an incomplete term, because it is not about light actually. “The speed of causality” is a
more accurate term. Nothing can happen faster than the speed of causality. This creates
what is called locality. Because things can’t travel instantly great distances, the universe
acts locally. Things influence the things around them, more than the things far away
from them. Gravity can only travel at the “speed of light”. There is a limit to how fast
something in one place can influence something in another place. There is no way for
anything to cause something to happen that is far away from it any faster than it would

take light, in general, to travel there. There are no magical connections that link
anything faster than light. Even if there were real psychics and your family died 2 light
years away from where you where, you wouldn’t ever be able to know until enough time
had passed for some form of signal to reach you.

The universe is massive and yet has little immediate influence on the local reality we live
in. The most powerful explosions in the universe still take time to reach us. We can still
see back to the earliest parts of the universe, when we look up into the sky. As we look
farther out, we look back farther in time. Nothing reaches us faster than the speed of
light. This creates an observable universe. Events as massive as the big bang, can still
be observed if we look far enough away from us. We are at all times experiencing things
that have happened through the whole history of the universe. The distance we look out,
directly relates to and connects to time. Distance itself is correlated into time so deeply,
that it is not easy to separate them, and maybe never at all.

If we could see everything in “real time”, then the whole sky would be brighter than the
sun. All the light in the universe would just hit us at once. Without locality, the universe
wouldn’t have darkness, space, and time. No place in the universe is any more the
center, than any other place. All points in the universe have their own local reality and
time, that then can influence things around them at a certain absolute maximum rate.
Whatever happens today to you on earth, can only ever effect anything in the universe
around you as fast as the speed of causality (the speed of light) can reach it. The speed
of light, is an expression of time itself. Time has to move through the physical universe
we live in. Time is fundamentally interwoven in the nature of space. We can observe
time itself in the movement of distant galaxies. When we look at the expansion of the
universe, we are observing time more than just simple space. Thinking about time
differently is the really hard part of Einstein. Locality and the speed of causality are

about time as it relates to space. You can actually see time, in how space moves, and in
how things move through it.

People want to think about the universe in ways where things are consistent with how
they feel as a person, and not accept simple logic. Not even Einstein was immune to this
problem. He couldn’t accept the natural logical conclusions of his work. He made the
math for universal expansion that we use today, and considered it his greatest mistake.
He came up with quantum entanglement as an absurd conclusion to quantum theory, to
disprove certain quantum theories, and it ended up being a cornerstone of physics. His
mind could take things to their logical conclusion and couldn’t always accept the rather
unbelievable results. The expansion of the universe and quantum entanglement while
exotic and new, are as real and fundamental to the universe as drinking a cup of water.
They are more concrete, solid, logic and real than drinking a cup of water.

Space

Things are relative in space, because space is not a fixed thing.

Relativity and all things being relative is a consequence of space and time themselves
being able to change. We experience space and time on the earth as fixed things, and
that only objects move around. Space and time are like objects, like balls, they too
move, have “speed”, and direction. They may also possibly entangle like quantum
particles.

If we really want to get at the heart of the problem, that people can’t understand, it is
empty space. Nothingness, normal empty space, a vacuum, is something. We can’t
experience absolutely nothing. Space is a thing, a vacuum at some level is an object. It
has energy, it has properties in it. You can certainly measure how much of it you have,
at any given moment. Empty space at its most empty is in of itself something. It is the
least amount of something, that something can be, and still exist. Empty space can do
things to the world around it. Space can move in of itself. You can have an object move
through space, and you can have space move around an object. Space is not “material”,
by its very definition, it is however something, and different parts of empty space, are
different than other parts of empty space. It has properties in it, and it changes.

When an object is moving through space it is not the only thing to consider. We have to
understand how space is moving around an object, to understand how it is moving
combined with its own movement. Galaxies for the most part don’t move relative to each
other. Galaxies in the universe in the largest generalist sense just spin, they don’t go
flying through the universe. Yet we can observe galaxies all getting farther away from
each other. They aren’t moving in any direction, and yet are moving apart from each
other. The space between galaxies is expanding, the galaxies themselves aren’t overall
moving. When we observe them, we see them “flying” apart. This is simply not
movement in the traditional sense that we see on the surface of the earth. They are not
being pushed apart, nor flying apart, they are just getting more distant from each other,
because “distance” itself is changing. The spaces between galaxies, and not the galaxies,
are moving and changing, and so we see a change in distance between them.

Space between galaxies is expanding. The space between galaxies is increasing, inside
the universe. They are not expanding out into more space. Galaxies are not moving into
new unknown regions of space; they are not moving. Space is increasing inside the

universe and between galaxies. Things don’t have to move, in order for you to see them
moving. Space itself can change, and make you perceive movement. There is a change
in that things relationship to you. Things really do get farther apart from each other.
Though at a basic level, you can’t say which one is moving and which one is not, unless
you can map how space itself is moving and expanding too.

Think about this seriously. You have a field of objects, all getting farther apart from each
other, and they are not moving, and they have no direction of movement. There is no
center to this field. Any point can be the center of this surface. This often explained
using a balloon, and marking dots all over the balloon, and then blowing up the balloon,
more and more. We need to imagine that the dots don’t get bigger, and we can observe
the distance between all the dots expand. This expansion is a way of describing time
entering into our 3D space. This is a basic way to understand it and not really how the
universe works. It is more like you have a field of many balloons that are all expanding,
and new balloons keep coming into existence. You could also imagine it like zooming in
on a picture and everything expands. We don’t want to think of this as a sort of force
pushing from the inside, like a blowing up balloon. There is no “pressure” in the
traditional sense to universal expansion. Neither is there stretching. Space is growing
with time everywhere, in a direct and exact relationship. A single expanding balloon, is
just one kind of time, and it curves. “Space” is not curved at the larger scales, and only
curves at the smallest scales.

The empirical fact is that space is expanding, in that there is more of it every moment.
More space is coming into existence all over the universe all the time. 70% of the energy
is the universe is contained in the vacuum of empty space, and this amount will only
increase until it is nearly 100%. This expansion is caused by “gravity”. Most of the
“gravity” in the universe causes the universe to expand. Gravity is not inherently an

attractive force. Gravity is a description of how space and time move. We created the
theory of the big bang before we really understood this fundamental and observable
reality to the universe. If 70% of the universe is dark energy, then it is more likely that
dark energy created the universe and not a super dense singularity.

Things moving away from you, are creating more space between you and it, and this
changes even your perception of how fast time is traveling relative them. This is not the
same as the kind between galaxies. Things are actually moving through space. Our
perception of time can be changed by how things move through space. Time is
happening everywhere independently. It is arising out of every point in the universe
equally. You should think of time more like the force filling the many balloons. The more
you move through space the slower time becomes, if you move through a lot of space
very quickly time begins to slow more and more, until you can’t even go faster. You
move through more balloons as you accelerate through the universe, and if you have
more matter, you interact with more of these balloons. You can see these differences in
the perception of time, as simply a description of differing amounts of space, that you
can’t see, because that “space” is “warped” locally.

Time

Relativity is about the observation of things that are separate from us, moving in space
and time. Space in the universe is flat, time is curved. Time moves differently depending
on where you are in the universe, and what you are doing. Time can move very slow,
until it is almost stopped. Time however cannot move faster than the speed of light (the
speed of causality). Space moves very differently around things when time slows. What

you can observe changes with how time and space work around an object. Imagine if
each of those black dots on a balloon was pushing down on the balloon and creating a
dent. The bigger the dent, the bigger the dot. The deeper the dent, the more “dense”
the dot. A dent is a distortion in time, that is observed as a distortion in space. The more
something resists the balloon at a single point, the more time itself slows down because
it is “expanding” slower at that point. If there is no resistance to change, then time flows
at its fastest rate, such as in the regions of vast voids between galaxies. When space
changes, time changes. They are the “same” thing; they are inherently connected.

The way space moves around objects changes how we see it. The changes in the amount
of space between us and a thing, changes our perception of time between two objects.
The faster the space increases the more the difference in time between those two things.
Things moving away from you slow in time because there is more space between you. If
something gets far enough away and is moving fast enough, our observation of it, can
slow to almost nothing. We see that time as slowing to almost nothing, and the thing
accelerating away from us at faster and faster speeds, doesn’t feel themselves slow in
time. This perception of slowness is because we are observing more space between two
things. The space is not this fixed thing, and our perceptions of a things time is based on
how light moves through the altered space around it. It can even slowdown in time, so
much as to disappear from our existence. If it didn’t disappear, it would have to travel
backwards in time for us to observe it and that would just be not cool. Changes in the
observed rates of time, preserve locality, and keeps things in reality. The faster you go,
the more energy you gain, the more mass you have, the more you resist change, the
more distorted the perception of space is around a thing. You can go faster than the
speed of light, and if you do, you will enter a vast nothingness of nearly infinite space
around you, because you increased space so much that it can no longer be a part of the
universe you were in. You can accelerate a thing so much that it becomes like a black
hole, possibly.

Time is time wherever you are personally. At any location time is experienced exactly
the same. You can’t experience time moving slower or faster, in your “frame of
reference”. If time moved faster or slower, you would experience it exactly the same.
Time is how fast things can change, and that is set by the speed of causality. By its very
nature, it is a constant, because if it wasn’t time wouldn’t exist. Everywhere in the
universe experiences time differently relative to you, the more distance it has from you.
Time is absolutely the same relative to the place it’s in. Time is also absolutely set
relative to the universe itself. Time actually needs to be observed happening at different
rates, so that universe can actually exist. Things have to be separated from each other.
Different places need distance between them, to be different. Time is just a sort of
distance between things, that lets the universe exist and have different places in it. You
need to wait before you can see something happening far away from you. The farther
away, the longer you need to wait to even see it.

Space-Time Gravity

Gravity is just a property of space and time. It can both push things apart and
pull things in, depending on the situation/geometry.

If you take normal Einstein physics, a black hole has time come to near stop at its event
horizon. Inside of its event horizon space expands towards infinity inside it. You can
have a black hole with a set and defined surface area on the outside, like a sphere or an
empty ball. The spheres outside area doesn’t change. Its inside area though can fit a
whole galaxy inside it, in a manner of thinking. You can’t observe how it moves like a
normal thing. Space just goes right through things, and you can’t block it with anything.

Space, “moving around”, is what creates gravity. Gravity is how space and time move in
the universe. Time creates “gravity”, by it being slower towards more massive objects,
and between two regions of different time rates, they “perceive” the amount of space in
the other differently.

Space is form of time, without direction. The curvature of space time is described by how
much it dilates time. So, it is time that is curved, and not space exactly. You measure
the curvature, by how fast clocks move in a given region compared to another region. If
there was more space, then there would be more distance between two things. We can
create another kind of distance between things with time, and in how fast time moves
between them. That difference in time between two things is expressed by the laws of
gravity and inertia. The “curve” is the difference in the rates of time, and those
differences create “acceleration” towards slower time. Time is shorter near large dense
material objects, and the very distance between things is shorter towards them. Basic
visualizations (other than balloons) of this are like memory foam mattress, heavy dense
objects make deeper impressions, and things roll towards those objects. Two large
massive objects, sort of roll into each other by the bending of mattress space time. The
slope in the dent is time, and that dent is a shortening of the “distance” So a straight
line follows the curves of time. We can only see time, as things change, yet it functions
in much the same way as space in of itself works. Time is like a very special form of
space that has direction and can curve.

Equivalence

Equivalence is one of the most important ideas in Einstein’s work. The speed of causality
causes things to be locally contained. This is called “locality”. Space-time arises out this
quality and keeps things in their own area, by making space and time, change with how

things move through space. You can’t really say what is moving and not moving in space
exactly. How things are observed between two objects is changed by their speed,
because space and time changed as things move. General relativity came together with
a simple beautiful thought. A man falling from a building feels no gravity or acceleration.
It is not different than falling through empty space. And if you stand on the ground, or
are being pushed up in an elevator, if the force pushing on your feet are the same
strength, then these two experiences are exactly equal.

We all know the classic story of Newton under an apple tree, and getting hit by an apple,
and this somehow being an insightful moment of how gravity works. The story is missing
a key part. He looked up at the moon, and realized what made an apple fall, makes the
moon orbit the earth. He created an equivalence between planetary motions, and gravity
on earth. No one had done that before. The heavens and the earth were treated as two
very separate worlds, with different laws. He then worked out the math/laws to make it
possible to explain such large and small things with the same math. Insights in physics
are often driven by symmetries. You have to find the right things to make symmetrical
though. You find odd parings of things, and you find symmetry between them, as a way
of reducing the universe to more simple laws.

Einstein took Newton’s insight to another level. Free falling and gravity are equal. Things
just flying in a straight line and gravity are equivalent. The gravity you feel when you
stand on the earth, is equivalent to the experience of being pushed up in an elevator, or
pushed back into your chair when a jet plane takes off. He wasn’t saying they similar, he
was saying they were exactly equal. Now making math to explain how that is possible is
a lot harder than what Newton had to do. Newton just had to make simple equations to
show that movement in the heavens and on earth, were ruled by the same principles.

If you are falling towards the earth, you actually will feel no acceleration. You only feel
any acceleration, when something is pushing on you. If you are falling towards the
earth, you aren’t really accelerating, in a classical way. You won’t feel acceleration until
you hit the earth.

When you stand on the earth, it is pushing up on your feet. This is the big change you
have to make in how you think about gravity. The earth is pushing up on your feet, you
are not pushing down on it. The earth in a certain way is expanding out and accelerating
you from the ground up. That is how the math works. How even physicists understand
that is not all that clear. The fact that gravity is pushing up on us, to make us stick to its
surface, and we aren’t being pulled into it, is confusing and yet also makes sense. There
is no force being acted on you from a distance pulling you with gravity. Gravity doesn’t
pull you, you feel gravity when it pushes on you, and that should be the important idea
to make it feel more real, and realize gravity has no magic power to pull things, and is
much more like a ball hitting a ball.

At a deeper level this is making gravitation and inertia equivalent. Which is not such a
crazy thing. If you drop 2 balls of very different weights, in a vacuum on the surface of a
planet, they will fall at exactly the same rate, and hit the ground at the same time. If
you have more inertia, you resist change more, though your experience of gravity is the
same as things with less inertia. In a rocket, jetting away in space or standing on the
earth, that acceleration pushing on your feet is the same thing. If you are just moving
faster, then you have more inertia. A car that is driving faster has more energy and
takes more force to slow down, it has more inertia. If you have more material mass, you
have more inertia. These are the same thing. Inertia doesn’t relate to how fast you
move; it relates to how much energy is in a system.

Everything follows straight lines if they have inertia. If something isn’t being accelerated,
it is following a straight line. If you are going to make math to explain that, then you
going to need to change the definition of a straight line. It is going to be very weird.
Curving space and time, made this possible. Einstein just made what things experience
as straight, different than what we see, with our immediate senses. They are still
absolutely straight in space, they just get curved by time, and thus gravity is a property
of time and how it changes.

Inertia is where things keep doing what they are doing. This is basically a straight line. If
an object is just sitting and not moving, it is following a straight line in time. Though an
object just sitting on the earth is being accelerated up from the earth pushing on it.
Gravity pulls and curves things towards it. Objects we throw up, curve back towards the
earth and hit the ground again. It is like bending the lines on graph paper to make
something curve, rather than making the line curve on a perfect square grid like graph.
The curve is not in space; the grid is warped by a hidden dimension of time. The straight
lines we see on a graphs grids, can be altered. If you graph time as a dimension like
space on a graph, this creates the curves (linear algebra makes this easy to
understand). Things are moving in straight lines on the graph paper, the graph paper
itself is being warped and changed.

We measure how fast clocks are moving, to measure a gravitational field. We measure
time dilation, to measure gravity fields. If you had a stack of clocks reaching from the
surface of the earth far into space, then all those clocks would have different rates of
time passing on them. We measure space-time curvature, by measuring time. Things fall
towards the earth, because it is the shortest route in time. We feel the earth pushing up
from under our feet, because of time pushing out (or in) on us.

Newtonian Relativity

Newtonian relativity makes velocity and rest equivalent. You can’t define something as
moving fast, unless you describe it in relation to something else. Anything you can
describe as moving quickly in one direction, you can describe as not moving at all. A ball
thrown up in the air can be accelerating up and decelerating down, or you can flip it and
say the ball is decelerating up and accelerating down. There is no difference in the math.
Negatives and positives can be switched at will, and rest and velocity can be switched at
will, all depending on the perspective one takes. The big important thing to realize is
that there are more of one thing moving in one way, than another thing. If a ball is
moving in a certain direction at a certain speed, we can say it has speed because the
earth is so much more than it. Reality becomes what is bigger and more, with speed
being more about the things relative to the greatest amount of stuff. The earth is so
massive compared to our lives on it, that we can easily lose sight of this relativity
between motion and rest.

Special Relativity

Let’s say you have a special rocket, and it can always accelerate at 8g non-stop all the
time, with endless energy to do so. It is going to be a very special object that is different
than the rest of the universe. Compared to the universe it is going to be changing the
most compared to it. There is no natural thing in the universe that can do this. Now if
you had normal rockets doing this and leaving the earth, you couldn’t properly describe
one as more proper than the other, if the rocket where to stop accelerating after gaining
tremendous speed. To the rocket, the earth would be moving away extremely fast, and
in effect be weightless in space. No matter how fast a spaceship goes in space, if it is not
accelerating, it is “weight-less” inside, and no different than just floating in empty space

unmoving. The world you came from though will be moving away very quickly. Your
future is moving away from where it came from.

Speeds effect how space and time function. With small differences in speed between a
rocket and the earth, space-time doesn’t change much. This is easy to see when we
compare no speed to light speed, and put that difference in speed relative to that.

(Speed of the rocket – Speed of the earth)/the speed of light= how much space time
alters.

The bigger the speed of the rocket, the closer this number gets to zero. Changes of 100
times the speed of sound, will barely change this ratio relative to such a massive number
like the speed of light. As we get numbers approaching 1, we get closer to moving at
100% the speed of light. Think of this as ratio of (a thing) to (space-time). If we look up
at the rocket and it going 90% the speed of light, we will see it as having slowed down
in time and being crunched up, it flattens in the direction it is moving. It won’t stretch
out in space-time, it will squish along the direction it is moving and up down relative to
