Quantum Physics is defined by probability

Quantum Gravity is the geometry of space-time, that can influence the state changes of
quantum systems in time and create space time itself as a smooth structure outside of
the quantum scale. Quantum gravity drives things to their ground state, and evolves
systems, it is not an attractive or repulsive force at the quantum scale, because the
force we call gravity is created by massive amounts of new space-time structures being
formed. Space and time are physical entities that are created in some ways like matter.
Time is a physical property of actual space, that is defined by the creation of new space
and new information. The universe grows very little at the small scales, and even at
stellar scales. Atoms give off light, but aren’t themselves light. The motions of
subatomic particles themselves are defined by how space and time move, rather than
cause space and time to move. The odd properties of quantum phenomena could
possibly be described in space-time geometry. That Geometry is what we call “gravity”,
and its primary qualities are not about gravitational attraction.

Space-time is structured at the tiniest levels in a “replicating” pattern, that always
expands. This expansion is time itself. Entropy comes from the expansion and replication
of space-time arranged in a specific pattern. With each replication, it alters the state of
things and it expands. There is a state becoming another state, and we can infer some
form of causality between them, that links them together in a sequence. This causality is
time. Causality doesn’t require exact cause and effect, only probable, because that is a
simpler system to evolve from nothing, than a defined and perfect cause and effect,

which in itself could just be seen a single thing. Time needs probability to be time, since
all determined things could be defined as a single state from a higher dimensional
perspective.

The universe can’t stop expanding, and time can’t stop moving forward. The evolution of
quantum systems arises from how matter interacts from this quantum space-time
geometry. It is like hills emerging and pushing things into new states. Shifts in
probabilities create shifts in energy. There is an up and there is a down. Expansion
creates energy, and this creates real shifts in how quantum systems evolve. Every state
in the universe changes moment to moment. Time never freezes. If time could stop, it
would never start again. Time by its very nature, causes constant causality between 2
states, so that no 2 things can ever be equal in time, and that the following system is
always bigger than the previous system. No atom can be the same between any 2
moments in time. Things in space possibly could be equal, if they exist in the same time.

Randomness creates all the mutations in life that evolve into the complex and very
useful structures, that life needs to survive and replicate. Life needs prolonged periods of
stability to spread and grow. The more a species spreads-and-grows stably through
time, the more likely it is to create mutations that will actually benefit that species.
There is a tension between a need for randomness and emerging stability in evolving
system. The universe needs similar conditions to evolve in.

Only possible things can exist, and this has an underlying power to it, that can’t be
readily expressed. it appears to arise out of randomness yet has a determined quality to
it, there is a duality to it, that may lie at the heart of all real dualities. The randomness

in the ground state contains the possibility to evolve into a determined system through
an evolution in time, where there is a very narrow range of means to reach such an end
such that the path is so unique, as to be deterministic, yet inherently unknowable. The
universe always evolving into more, leaves room for an improvement upon itself at each
step, and this can go on without end. Information can always increase, and always
evolve. Evolution and entropy are two very interacting qualities of information, and all
things that exist in the real universe. I can’t yet explain their exact distinction.

Chapter 13: Quantum Gravity and Evolving Universes

As things approach the speeds of causality, they begin to create new universes or go
into others. This is not a new universe with anything in it, or of any moral value. It is
just a space that is separate from our own, and can never be reached. An event horizon
is a boundary between universes, that is not wholly separated from one universe to the
next. In simple geometry, they are whole new universes, and totally separate. In the
deeper geometry of time, they are connected. If you stood on the surface of the earth,
you had gravity increase and increase, then eventually you would see the very earth
curve up and around you. What is curved in one direction, can be curved in another
direction, when time dilates enough.

As you fall through an event horizon, you would see the surface of the event horizon
surround you slowly. It would consume you in so much new space, that the old universe
would disappear. As you emerge inside a black hole, the singularity is spread out like a
spherical surface all around you. If a singularity was “red”, you would see red at a
singular distance in every direction you looked. The event horizon you just crossed
would look like and is, pure empty space. You cross over into the dead center of a
sphere; the event horizon is the very origin and center of that sphere. Things crossing
the event horizon, from the outside universe, would enter one by one from that singular
point at the center, and it would probably emit energy almost like a sun. Matter would
be flinging out it in all directions, seemingly coming from nothing. It could be thought of
like a white hole at the center of a massive spherical space, that keeps making the black
hole bigger, the more stuff you add in.

http://math.ucr.edu/home/baez/physics/Relativity/SR/Spaceship/spaceship.html

From the outside as you enter, all of the universe you could possibly see all around you,
will narrow towards a single point. You are surrounded in the space of the event horizon,
and still able to enter the universe you came from. It will look like the whole universe of
all the stars you knew is flying away in the distance, like a rocket flying away from its
home planet and it is getting smaller and smaller. If you tried to escape, even going
near the speed of light, that point would only slowly get closer, and it would take a long
time to escape. Space is literally coming into being around you, so you are moving
through massive amounts of space. This new space surrounding, is just seen as slowed
down time, to those on the outside. They will see you go slower in time, flatten away to
nothing, and not see a sea of space consume you. These two perspectives are exactly
equal, when you allow for time and space to invert themselves.

A black hole could be seen as leaping into zero-dimensional space, rather than anything
outside of our universe. You are basically zooming in and in until there is no more
zooming possible. The new space is created out of this zooming into space, caused by
the dilation of time. As you slow in time, you sink into the well of nothingness, that is
the zero-dimension. The event horizon doesn’t create exactly another universe, it
transitions things into the domain of quantum reality. In Zeno’s paradox, the process of
taking shorter and shorter steps alters the very time it takes to travel those steps, and
alters the very structure of time as to be different. In a sense, you never take a shorter
step, and always take the same length step, and are zooming deeper into reality with
each step.

On a 2D graph of Zeno’s paradox, as you approach the wall on the x axis, the line curves
on the y axis towards an infinite value. What we see as reality, in a given spot, is always
as a person standing like a tangent on that line, with flat space. The tangent line itself
becomes the x axis of any person, and there is no correct x-axis in the entire universe.
Different reference frames basically say that what we think of as the x axis is relative,
and not the actual measurements on that axis are relative. We all have our own x-axis,
they are all tilted differently. Space-time dilations and relativity are described with this
simple explanation. When the tangent line goes vertical, a new universe is created, with
an inversion of space and time, with an inversion of x and y. The Y axis keeps all these
different versions of x consistent, by changing how time moves. In positions closer to
the wall, time is slower, time is more, and for those farther from the wall time is more
flat and normal. The closer to the wall you get, the more you leap into a new reality and
into a new universe. You literally go into new galaxies by how fast you accelerate a
spaceship, and that trip is described in this math. Not there is any wall to actually

approach. The wall itself is just relative to the rest of the universe you come from. What
we call a wall or the x-axis, are just dependent on how similar they are to everything
else. Earth has a very clear wall, and x-axis, that is very similar to nearly everything we
will ever experience as humans.

A “ROPE” UNIVERSE: A VISUAL ANALOGY FOR RELATIVITY
VISUALIZATIONS.

To translate between different time frames, no matter how extreme is basically fairly
simple in math, and in visual metaphor. It is just the Pythagorean theorem of
A^2+B^2=C^2, with space and time as legs of a triangle, and not only space like in
traditional geometry. You are making triangles out of the different x and y axis lengths,
relative to each other. Standing on a planet in its gravity, or speeding a rocket, create
the same changes in time, with the same basic math. Let’s say you have 2 ropes, and
they are held apart by two people, where one rope is stretched tight and the other is
loose. We can actually add as many ropes as you want, with different tensions between
them. This tension will create different lengths for each rope. If this is space time, the
tension on the ropes is time, and this tension changes the length of ropes between the
two people, while never actually changing their real distance from each other. We always
see space the same, and only measure the tension to be different between two different
time frames.

If you are standing on the earth, you can imagine the rope just dipping a little. If you
are “standing” on the Sun, the rope will dip even more. If you are in a rocket speeding
fast enough away from everything else, you can dip really deeply, and have a very loose
rope. Near a black hole’s event horizon this rope keeps dipping more and more and

more. That dip is time, and yet we will always see ourselves on a tight and taught rope.
To translate between perspectives, is just about comparing rope length. The longer your
rope, the more space you see around you, though to the universe outside your rope,
your rope isn’t longer, your time is slower. If there is a rocket speeding at 99% the
speed of light across from your frame, you will see a sort of pre-black-hole zipping by
you. The space ship will be tiny compared to this distortion in space, and you probably
won’t be able to see the actual ship. That “pre-black-hole” will be moving at 99% the
speed of light towards whatever it is moving towards. You are seeing a bubble of space
contained in a small area, moving at a tremendous speed. All that contained space,
make in anything in that bubble have distorted perceptions of scale. It is being seen
through a lens, and you can describe the image exactly with the basic math of lenses.
The length of rope describes the curve in this lens.

The space ship inside, will see the whole universe around them as a narrow circle in
front of them, with mostly vast empty space consuming them from behind. The dip in
the rope is consuming them, just like near an event horizon. Time is the very dark space
around them. They can even look at another spaceship going 99% the speed of light,
zipping along, and observe them, as slowed in time, and like this black hole like object
zipping across everything. They both can see each other as slowed in time, contained in
large time bubbles, that shrink the perspective of things to flatten out towards nothing.
To help with your own intuitive understanding, just think about the ropes. The speeding
away ship has a different rope length, that creates a different dip. Each rope sees itself
as tight, and sees every other rope has being the same length, with different observed
speeds of time. Each rope can become its own universe, if it changes enough compared
to the rest. Relativity just describes how ropes see each other, and doesn’t say any one
of them is correct, though the whole universe we live is sort of its own rope, and
changes from that can be seen as a kind of absolute time.

Every real point in the universe, can be its own universe, and has its own unique event
horizon. Time is about the relationship between all these finite points that make up the
real structure of reality. Ropes describe the potential event horizon of each potential
universe. If two ropes are so far apart, with one being tight and another having a dip
going to infinity, they will split from each other. A rope just by itself, will slowly get
longer and longer and bend more and more. The very nature of rope is that it itself
grows and fractures into more ropes. An expanding universe creates more universes.
Our own observable universe will split off from itself, into many universes, many ropes,
in the future. Our observable universe is its own event horizon, that we can’t cross, from
this little point we all come from, on this planet Earth. Galaxies are constantly crossing
this event horizon, until one day, there won’t be any other galaxies in our observable
universe except our own. If you get confused by expanding universes, just think of the
rope getting longer in it of itself, the tension in time, causes new things to pop into
existence.

An Evolving Multiverse

Every tiny region in the universe can eventually expand out so far, that they can be
contained in their own universe larger than the one we see. Now it would take one cubic
centimeter of space 14 billion years to double in size, and take many more doublings
until it reached a size capable of changing into a universe. The rope itself is always
growing no matter what we do to it. time is always moving forward. We can warp our
perceptions of time, and flip space and time by how we move it. In the end, the rope of
time, and its tension has its own geometry that leads it to grow and not just have
different depth of dips in it from different lengths of rope being held at the same
distance.

You could describe the field matter particle of a space-time field as universes
themselves.

Regions of space expanded away from each other, can splinter off into separate times
and nearly separate universes. The universe itself is a replicating entity, that’s
replication at quantum levels creates gravity and gradual expansion, and when done
over large periods of time on huge scales, replicates whole universes itself. The way we
would sequence and organize all those universes beyond our universe, if they existed,
would take at least 1 dimension, if our universe just came from a universe before it. You
could make a sequence of universes, its own dimension, and this extra dimension would
exist at the most expanded scales of the universe and define the geometry between
totally different universes. The future contains in our universe another dimension of our
universe, that has emerging from it new universes.

If we go back to the beginnings of creation of time emerging from nothing, it would take
tremendous growth of a basic universe before it ever even evolved into any sort of
complex universe we see today. Nothingness expanding, had to grow quite large, and
create a vast number of independent universes. The multiverse itself had to grow to
10^200 universes before even one of them has a realistic chance of creating a random
event, that leads to the creation of the evolving material reality we see. There doesn’t
need to be infinite universes, because we don’t need to account for all possibilities. We
just need enough possibilities, that our realities beginning, becomes a more likely

possibility, to have at least happened once, in one tiny region of empty space in vast
nothingness.

The multiverse will emerge in our own universe and in things we can directly observe, if
we look for them. If universes are born in universes, then we should be able to see the
beginnings of these new universes forming in our own right now. By the predictions in
this work, these will most likely arise in areas with the most space and the least matter,
around them. A universe that comes from nothing, would be most likely born in a space
of the most nothing. If space time emits universes as a “particle” than only in areas that
have the most space-time energy, would there contain the energy capable of making a
universe “particle”. This would be the pre-formation of white holes, before they
“explode” into an independent universe. You would look for white holes and an emerging
multiverse, where these is the most nothingness and the most amount of spatial
expansion, and not for high energy matter and particles. These regions exist, and
behave exactly as predicted, in vast supervoids. (note: I had no idea they did exist when
coming up with this idea)

This would be as if another universe was intersecting and entering into our universe
from the multiverse. You could describe the time dimension spatially, and imagine an
existing separate multiverse universe, intersecting and merging into our own. Since we
live in time, we would observe this as a universe emerging into our universe from
nothing. Its expansion and growth in size would correlate to the line segment of a 2D
circle passing through a 1D line, and just showing two points expanding apart from
eachother. The edge of the circle would touch the line, and it would create a bigger and
bigger intersection as time passed, and the 2 points would get wider apart. Since we live
in a 4D universe, a sort of solid cylinder, we would see an actual sphere emerge as the

intersection, as a reduction in dimensionality into our 3D spatial perceptions. It would
keep growing in size, until a critical point, and became its own contained universe.

A General Relativity Interpretation of the “Many Worlds Interpretation”

-Unto to each his own a universe to be a master of with absolute dominion. -

Each and every point is expanding in of itself. If you took the immediate space right in
front of you, and divided it up into a few sections, eventually at a certain point in the
future, all those space will grow large enough to be their own universe, and grow so
separately from each other to have no causal linkage between them. Space expands
flatly in time, because the expansion happens at small levels, and is distributed. It is not
a singular expansion of a singular frame of time. Each and every place in the universe
has its own unique place in space and time. Time moves differently in every place in all
of existence. Each one of these unique frames of reference is its own universe that
grows and expands. Universes are born out of universes. The universes born in one
universe had their infancy in ones before it. A tiny space sitting in front of you may have
to cross over more than one universes existence, before it can grow large enough and
independent enough to create its own white hole event. Space builds up in size before
becoming a white hole and exploding into a new universe. The universe we live in is a
nursery to many new universes. Gravity arises out of tension and differences between
these different frames. The geometry of space time is lines of tension between many
expanding frames of reference interacting.

You can look at the stars in galaxies as pre-event horizon debris that will eventually fall
into the black hole at the center of each galaxy. Galaxies themselves can be seen as just
large black holes and everything around them, as just the future substance that will
make them up. Our planet and star exist in the time line of a black hole, and will
eventually be consumed by one. In some ways, we exist in the event horizon of a black
hole, if we can’t escape from this galaxy into another galaxy. The gravity of this galaxy,
makes any matter escaping it, very unlikely. Light can escape for now, and possibly
massive technological machines created solely to escape this galaxy can get out. We are
not yet contained within a perfect event horizon where only space and time can escape.

We are in a probabilistic event horizon of black-hole at the center of our galaxy, with a
99.99999% chance or more of solid matter never escaping it.

ON WHITE HOLES

Vast voids make up the universe we live in. We can observe, approach, and enter into
these vast voids in the universe, that will one day become new universes. The cosmic
voids of the universe are most likely pre-formed white holes, gradually growing in size
before than rupture in a white hole forming event. A perpetual expanding universe
almost requires that regions of space will split off from each other and have no causal
connection between them. When these voids and distances become so great, they
possible can create truly new universes. When they form into real white holes they will
have event horizons that nothing in an old universe can cross over, without leaping back
in time to a point before the white hole existed. All futures point away from a white hole,
just as all futures point towards a black hole.

A white hole can emerge from a gradual process of ever increasing vacuum space. We
can approach an emerging white hole before it becomes a real white hole, by going
towards large voids in the universe, where space has expanded the most. Dark energy is
the only possible source of new energy to create a new universe from within our
universe. This amount of energy can grow to nearly any size, and accounts for 70% or
more of the energy in our little universe. In a time far into the future, this amount will
approach 100%. Eventually our galaxy will not have visible neighboring galaxies. In
certain regions of space without any galaxies, the space between galaxies, dark energy
and the vacuum will be 100% of everything in possible existence. This is a “singularity”
of massive empty darkness. Time expands outward, and pushes things apart. Galaxies
are flinging apart from each other at faster than the speed of light, the farther you go

out from our universe. The amount of super small expansion, in tiny pieces of spaces,
across a long enough distance of space, can enough growth together, that the points at
each end expand from each other faster than light.

A white hole is where all possibly futures point out from it. The event horizon of a white
hole is the past itself. All events we experience must point away from it, and all time
moves away from it, and thus there is no means to see it, unless we look far out into the
past of distant places in the universe, and see how time emerged in their locations. The
farther we look out, the farther we see back into the time of another place, and not our
own. We can only assume that things were the same in the distant past of other parts of
the universe, as they are in ours. Nothing can cross the event horizon of white hole
without functionally traveling backwards in time. The faster you push towards a white
hole, the more you would just stand still in time, and see nothing change around you.
Instead of seeing the universe pass by you, you would look out at the universe and see
it slow to nothing, and become more and distant and black. You would enter a vast sea
of nothingness. A real white hole’s event horizon can never be approached, since in each
moment, you got closer to it, you would also be getting farther away from it. Our
universe is a white hole, and we exist in its domain, and it controls all our perceptions of
time.

TIME TRAVEL

A time machine that can travel back in time, with you in it, is just as possible as a
machine to transport into a cartoon movie world. There is no past to travel to, and thus
any attempt to do so, is no different than traveling to a fantasy world. The past is not
real and concrete. The only thing that exists is reality and what we can see. To travel
back in time is form of cognitive delusion in how our minds create fantasies about the

past. We believe the past actually happened and is real, and this delusion helps keep us
alive. Our memories of the past don’t even need to be connected to actual reality.
Memory only serves a purpose in giving us greater dominion over things, so we can
survive. The idea of things being real and solid, is how a mind driven to believe its own
survival is everything, would make a mind conceive time and space. There are many
different ways we as humans conceive the past, present and future, and in shockingly
levels of diversity. Almost no one can imagine a different conception of time, and then
the one they have, and the sense of reality it brings them.

The past does literally exist, and it is a material thing existing in our world right now.
Our own past is however something we can never observe. We can only observe the
past of other places distant from us. When I see a car crash right in front of me, I am
actually seeing the past experience of a time from a certain distance from me. It is
nearly instantaneous, because we are so close, and yet it is still the past I am seeing.
Extending out from our planet are shells of time. If you wanted to “travel backwards in
time” 100 years, you would need to go 100 lights in every single direction around the
earth, and record all the information contained in space at that moment. It would be 200
light years across and have a surface area of immense proportions. This layer of spacetime is our past from 100 years ago. It is the literal past, with all the information about
that past contained within it. it experiences no sense of time, and moves instantaneously
through the universe, relative to itself. The speed it moves is the speed of light, and this
is absolute.

The future then would be contained in something smaller than an atom, and inside the
very fabric of nothingness. It emerges out of space in each moment from nothingness.
The future is a literal thing that exists at the tiniest scales, and grows into our present,
and expands out to infinity in our future. Time is a physical and real thing, and not a

metaphysical concept. We can never catch up with our own past. If you go 99.9999%
the speed of light, the past will always be a bit ahead of you, and always get a bit
farther away in each and every moment. If you freeze matter to its coldest possible
temperature, time still moves in it and emerges from it. There is an inherent “heat” to
the universe constantly expressing itself. Time is heat emerging from nothingness. There
is always more universe, there is always more heat, there is always more time. The
future arises out entropy and thermodynamics, and the past can be described by an
understanding and arrangement of this sort of information after it emerges.

If we made a superpower that could time travel, using real physics, it would be the
power to travel into the future. A time travel power is always shown as slowing time
around a person, and they can move faster than anyone and everyone around them.
They move so quickly they can leap through time. They can catch up with time that
escaped from them. The degree of this power would be how close they could get to a
mean of light moving away from them, or if they could actually see the very light, they
just emitted, by going faster than light. You could think of traveling into the past, as
being able to move so fast, that you could go from where you are standing, to another
point, and see yourself standing in that old location, and then leap to the location you
are in at the moment.

Time paradoxes of traveling into the past, would arise from jumping a certain distance
faster than light, and being able to observe what happened before, and observe your
very own self. Instead of fragmenting and creating multiple time lines, you would
fragment whatever moved back in time and create multiple versions of itself, and often
occupying the very same positions in time and space. If you leaped out 1000 light years,
and sent a message, it would still only arrive after you left. If you leapt 1000 light years,
observed what happened, and then jumped back, you would still be in the world you

came from. It is this fantasy idea of the past being a real thing, and not understanding
the reality of what the past is, that creates absurd fantasy ideas of time travel.

Traveling to the future is certainly possible, and would make for a very interesting time
traveling super power. A real master of time, would be able to slow time, towards near
stillness. If I slowed myself in time, I would leap forward in time, and be able to attract
objects towards me with gravity. Since this would destroy me, creating so much gravity
from myself, I would have to project time slowing around me to different locations. It
could create the power to crush any object by freezing it in time such that gravity inside
of it would crush it down to its tiniest size, and even attract things around it towards it.
You basically would gain the power to control gravity, if you could leap forward in time.
A black hole itself can be seen as a massive time machine that leaps into the most
distant future.

A time machine that we can build, based on ways we know we can change time, would
just be a rocket that accelerates up to near light speed. It could travel great distances,
and arrive in a very short time relative to itself. The rocket can’t arrive anywhere faster
than light speed, from the earths perspective. Light itself travels instantly across the
universe, relative to itself, since time is frozen in light, and experiences not traveling of
time. If you go fast enough, your sense of time slows, and your actual distances covered
can be great. You can travel into the future with a fast rocket, as your time machine.
Going faster in a rocket is the only known way to control the flow of time, by slowing it
down relative to the rest of the universe.

Inflation:

The science and math of the current “big bang theory” can only go as far back as cosmic
inflation, when the universe was very large, and not back to a single point of energy that
many theorize the universe begins in. When light first came into being, its heat level was
consistent across the entire observed universe. Inflation was invented as a means to
explain how all of the observable early universe, could be so consistent, and there could
be a singularity that the universe begins from. This rapid expansion evens out the
energy, and can help explain the physical and thermal structure of the universe we could
see at the earliest moments light existed. “The Big Bang” as it stands now, is actually
the moment after inflation happened, and what happened before it exists in this realm of
near unknowable magic. To solve this problem, in a new way, we just need a way this
whole huge region could have a simultaneous event happen across it, other than a
matter singularity. There isn’t even math to describe a singularity, because singularities
as super dense singular points, don’t exist.

Instead of a densely packed singularity of matter that created the universe, it could be a
massive space time “singularity” formed out of vacuum energy. A mass of space, may
form such an immense amount of energy, and expand at such a rate, that it creates a
white hole. That event, that moment, inverts space into time, and turns all events from
that white hole to be pointed away from it, and makes all possible futures as beings
caused by it. We can never directly observe that event or look into the past universe,
because all of time points away from it, and towards our future. This is the literal past,
and traveling there takes time travel. A white hole would emerge from the gradual
buildup of vacuum space, until it reached a critical size and “mass” that would cause it to
break from the space time of the universe it emerged from. The universe can emerge
from another universe, as the most probable and easy way to explain how the universe
works. We then need to properly define what space and time are in order to understand
how this is possible.

Entanglements Are Faster Than Light

Entanglements of matter can interact at faster than the speed of light. This is a great
mystery in physics. Its solution is also very simple, if one looks at the basic logic and
facts. Entanglement itself is what creates time, and thus the breaking and altering of
entanglements transcends time and causality, because entanglement itself is what
creates causality in the universe. Entanglement is the basic structure of the universe
that makes it possible to define one moment as causing another moment. The very
structure of space contains within it a defined pattern, that allows time to emerge from
it. Space entangles to create time itself, and so all entanglement are properties of spacetime. Space-time entanglements can interact at faster than the speed of light, because
they are the structure that creates time itself. Matter can’t cause anything to happen
faster than time itself. Time itself can cause time to happen in whatever structure time is
arranged in. There is no other possible explanation for how entanglement can move
faster than light, other than that entanglement is the structure of space-time itself, or a
fundamental property of what creates it. Entropy, probability, and uncertainty all play
important roles too.

The only “thing” in a white hole, is nothingness. “Nothing” can cause “nothing” to
happen at any speed it wants, and create an entirely independent and new space time. A
vast region of highly entangled empty space could simultaneously interact with itself,
without violating the speed of light, because it would be only space interacting with
space, and that is what creates time and not a cause of one thing on to the next. It
creates causality itself and not causes on specific things. “Breaking” time itself, doesn’t
violate time, nor creates any paradoxes. A white hole emerges from a universe where
time has spread the universe out so far, that is breaks into separate pieces with
independent space times.

A big bang is the event of a white hole forming into an independent universe. All matter
is created at “big bangs”, and no matter from a previous universe can survive into
another one, because new universes emerge from “nothingness”, from vast regions of
empty space. Something in the nature of vast entangled regions of pure space-time,
there exists a means for this to collapse and create a singular energetic event. The
maxim that no matter or energy can be created or destroyed after the big bang, can still
be true, so long as you don’t include vacuum energy. If that energy could then convert
into something in else, in a singular grand moment, then you could explain how the
energy of a new universe can be created from inside an old universe. The white hole
itself creates all energetic matter in a universe in a single moment.

Space-time is time, and to understand time you need to understand how it changes
space. Nothing can “happen” before a big bang, because “nothingness” itself created all
big bangs, and time itself curved from one universe into a wholly new and separate
universe. Empty space has underlying patterns, and these patterns create what we see
as time and causality. This structure has odd rules that seem impossible to discern,
because people associate with them, the interaction of matter we experience in our
everyday lives. When space-time moves and interacts it defies all easy understanding,
and creates entirely new realities. This interaction has a concrete and real structure in
the quantum world, and it is described in how space entangles.

This structure of entangled space, is too fine to see and can’t be observed with cameras
or light sensing devices. Time is measured with clocks, and this very subtle kinds of time
at the quantum level would take a level of time measurement beyond what exists in my
time now. Just now in physics we have observed gravitational waves. These are massive
waves in space-time, that have no particle or matter, carrying massive amounts of

energy and information across the universe. Information/energy can be imbedded in
gravitational waves. We could think of the fine structure of the universe with entangled
space as very fine gravitational waves, with information and energy embedded in them.
This underlying structure if true, would solve most all the problems current physics has
with black holes. Energy/information can be lost in black holes, and the only thing that
can escape a black hole is space-time itself. If space time can have information
imbedded in it, as part of its intrinsic nature, then it changes the foundations of modern
physics.

The implications of such idea radically change all possible views of how the universe was
created, will end, and on the nature of God. It is almost like the universe has ESP, and it
can broadcast information with nothing observed in between. This magic like quality of
entanglement that can instantly connect things light years apart, is bound in how certain
classes information is transmitted through space and time itself, with no matter. This
information can’t cause things to happen, and yet it influences all of reality. I would
guess this pattern is highly correlated to crystals, and how life forms. It causes certain
structures and patterns to be more likely to emerge than others. It orders things at a
very fine scale, and sometimes those orderings lead to replicating systems, like crystals
and life. The very nature of life might be embedded in this structure, and thus could be
the central driving force of our human reality.

The Day Everything Changed: Anthropic Principle

Sentient life is a well know thing, that we are fairly certain exists and thus
must be accountable for, in the very laws that govern how the universe exists
and comes to be (I oddly find this the most controversial statement in my book).

One-day sentient life evolved on this world we live. It is much rarer than non-sentient
life. Most planets and places where life evolves will probably be destroyed before
sentient life evolves. The window of time in the universe where life can evolve and the
window of time in solar system where life can evolve, are usually not long enough for
complex life forms to evolve. Our own planet had life for billions of years, before it even
formed into basic animals during the Cambrian explosion. Life on earth was mostly
single celled organisms for 3-4 billion years. While life could be abundant in the
universe, it will rarely ever get beyond a few celled organisms. Planets have short
windows were life is possible. Sentient life is even more rare, because it needs even
more specific conditions to evolve.

Sequential Evolving Universes

Expanded Axiom: The end state of one universe can influence the creation of
the next universe
•

Universes evolve towards increased stability that increases the likelihood of more
replicating universes surviving and creating more replicating universes. Any
increase in stability, no matter how small, will “evolve” the universe by the tiniest
amount.

•

A Universe is alive if it can replicate and evolve

If universes come from universes, then stability and evolution would be selected features
for the survival of new universes. Any living universe, such as ours, has a stable end.
That stability pre-existed life, and is the foundation from which all things could evolve,
the universe included. In physics, they found that our universe won’t collapse back onto
itself, and have gravity pull it all back together. It also won’t start expanding so fast,

that even matter is ripped apart by the acceleration expansion of the universe. It
expands at this precise and exact level, where stability is maximized. This is such a fine
distinction between the universe ripping apart, or crunch back together, that even tiny
changes, would lead to this stability falling apart. The real universe is consistent with
this theory, because we actually exist. The state of the previous universe will replicate
into the following universe, and “mutations” are possible.

Stable long living universes are more likely to create more universes, than short lived
ones, because they grow longer and create more vacuum energy to create new
universes. The easiest way to imagine a stable expanding universe creating more
universes, is if universes themselves are born out of massively expanded regions of
space. The longer the universe expands, the more likely there will be massive regions of
space that are large and energetic enough to create a new universe. The universe
evolves in a direction of stability, so a universe that would grow into one like ours and
then experience a big crunch or a big rip, would be impossible, and doesn’t exist in any
universe or possible condition of the universe that life exists in. A living universe goes
towards a stable end of sorts that allows it to pass on its “knowledge”, to the next
universe.

At a certain point in the evolution of living universes its rules and initial conditions
become very stable, and evolve only at the tiniest levels. It will evolve towards a near
perfect rate of growth and stability at the macro-level, that fosters the most replicated
universes possible coming into existence. If the universe mutates and becomes more
stable, it passes on that increased stability to the next universe. This creates a trend
that expands down into far more nuanced things, that select for a life bearing universe.
The conditions that make a universe maximally capable of replicating itself, lead to a

universe able to create life on the micro level using the same evolutionary processes of
the macro. The forces that drive universal evolution emerge from quantum features, and
become more optimal at micro levels, when there are longer macro time windows for life
to randomly come into existence. The fine tuning “knobs” for the physical galaxy would
be much bigger, and the fine tuning “knobs” of life, much smaller.

The First Living Universe: Narrow Windows of Time for Life’s
Development

•

The tiniest differences in the initial states of the universe effect the chances
of life in the universe and its development.

•

The universe can select for more life bearing universes, if life or the
conditions for life bearing influences the survivability and replication of
universes.

Life exists in our universe. At a minimum, it happened in one universe, at one exact
moment, in one exact place, and only there. The conditions for life to exist are the rarest
of all conditions. In a grand multiverse, most all possible universes would have no life,
and no chance of life ever existing. There are just so few ways we can arrange the
constants of the universe such that they produce life. And even in a universe with rules
and conditions where life could come into being, it is extremely unlikely that life would
even come into existence. You could have trillions upon trillions of universes with all the
same conditions, and only one even forms the most basic form of life possible.

The window of time where life is possible, is very narrow, in any universe. Stars must
form, and those stars have to explode over and over, until they stabilize and produce
ever more complex and dense forms of new matter. A simple universe of all hydrogen,
that never even forms into stars, would never form life. Most universes other than our
own, would resemble stages of our early universe, except where that stage goes on for
much longer, and the universe ends before forming into something more complex like
our current universe. A universe may end sooner, collapse, or even expand so fast it rips
itself apart in a short time.

We can see looking back in the history of our universe and find the earliest stages of
galactic development, where life could possibly evolve in. We can also calculate how long
the universe will have until it is inhospitable to life. The longer this window, the more life
there will be in a universe, probabilistically. The universe may seek out a maximization
of this window of time, that life can arise out of, and prosper in. Enough diversity for
things to evolve in, and enough stability that things can survive when they do form..
With longer periods of time, and more stable galaxies and more stable star systems, life
has more likelihood to come into existence. Life on earth needed so many specific
conditions to evolve, and those conditions are rare, though computable. Eventually over
enough universes life becomes more probably in each successive universe. Increasing
stability and increasing complexity are fundamental laws of the universe. Life itself may
increase the likelihood or more survivable universes that prosper more, such that the
more life there is, the more chances that quality life bearing universes will exist and
dominate over non-life bearing universes. Iff life itself can affect the birth of universes.

More Stable and More Complex, Universes Are More Suitable for Life.

A universe with life is a more stable universe. The qualities that drove the evolution of
the universe, may also drive the evolution of life, and to such a degree, that life itself
comes to drive the evolution of the Universe. The first universe with life couldn’t be
much different than our own universes starting conditions. However as more life existed
it creates conditions to make starting conditions for universes more beneficial to life.
What is possible and not possible is a very narrow range of things, and this becomes
especially so with living things. Life expands on the possible, and never becomes the
impossible. These probabilities that evolve life directly correspond to the evolution of
random quantum systems, to some degree. Life is a quantum based entity, where the
irregularities of quantum features that created the universe, define black holes, and
defines the properties of matter, act to create the fundamental features of life. Life may
also have a great proclivity to exist, because quantum features drive it to exist, as an
expression of possible outcomes, as an expression of itself manifested more clearly.

Ever increasing stable complexity, makes life more possible to exist.

The Universe appears to have a trend of becoming more life bearing as a function of the
same principles that formed it out of nothing. This is not a big leap of thinking, for a
basic theory of how the universe works. It is simple logic, and going for the simplest
most direct explanation to account for life in the universe, the actual state of the

universe we see, the laws of physics as we know them, and the simple logical outcomes
of the thought experiments that develop modern physics.

A Grand Note: Avoiding Metaphysics

A one in infinity chance, is zero

If the multi-universe is just a massive number of possible universes and not infinite
amount of them, then the constraints on that infinity negate all possible quantum
configurations existing. If it isn’t infinite, then not all possible universes came into being,
then this introduces a degree of randomness and probability into our universe coming
into being. There then is some amount non-determinism at some level into quantum
physics. The question then becomes how small a multiverse needs to be made for it to
be possible to create our universe, and to hunt for every single way to constrain that
number, to the smallest amount. If we don’t, then we deal with an idealized concept of
infinite universes, that creates zero possibilities for existence. Probability is the only way
to create a universe, because absolute deterministic models have zero possibilities of
existing, due to simple math 1/(infinity), would be our place in the universe. The more
we limit the size of the multiverse, the more probable we make our existence, up to a
certain point.

The geometry of space time at a quantum level demands a universe consistent with it,
things that are more consistent with these properties, will exist more in the universe.
The very universe and all its complexity are expressions of the nothingness that created
the universe. This nothing gained evolution, it gained time, and it evolves towards its
own self. These patterns of time and space are real, and they imprint themselves on the

universe, and life emerges in response to these patterns, and sentient lives very mental
structures must reflect them, or not be able to work. Life itself down to all our very
thoughts must be consistent with the geometry of space time, down to the tiniest scales,
or it would not be consistent, possible or real. Only the possible can exist. As time
emerges it annihilates that which can’t be, and favors that which can be. This is a sort of
conceptual friction that annihilates inconsistency in the universe. As a system arises out
of randomness, and grows to nearly infinite, yet not infinite, scales, it must be
constrained by reality and what is possible. These constraints are deep, everlasting and
precise.

Consider this: The math developed by Einstein to explain General Relativity is the
underlying math that was used to model human consciousness and form the basic
programing language of modern AI and deep learning. The more we evolve an
understanding of this geometry, the more we reveal the consciousness of humanity, and
possibly the purpose of the Universe. To all physicists studying the stars, you may want
to give all your time, thought, and dedication to revealing the power of AI, and creating
a new age of technology, as the greatest act of service to science, truth, and humanity
possible. If this seems a simple coincidence to your mind, then you are a fool. A theory
of space-time is a theory of the information embedded in it. The truth of this is
unavoidable and absolute. Its consequences when integrated into our technology and
cultural vision of ourselves, will transform everything.

LIVING LINEAR EVOLVING UNIVERSE

A living universe can give birth to another living universe. If universes can be sequential,
then they can be created by living sentient beings, as the very product and purpose of
life itself. Life is an expression of the quantum functions that created the universe from
random nothingness, and evolve towards one definitive possible end.

Our universe is most likely created by another universe that existed before ours. It had
nearly or exactly identical starting conditions as our own. It is possible that a civilization
of aliens nearly identical to us, in a preceding universe, created our universe. This has
happened or will happen, because we are alive and have minds connected to reality. The
conscious domestication of universes can perpetuate itself and make life more likely to
be possible in each successive universe. Life has the potential to spread across all the
knowable universe. We may only reach a billion galaxies, and occupy every solar system
in them, with human life filling every place. We may create more human beings than
there are atoms on the surface of the earth. Humanity has the potential to be a universal
species spreading across the entire travelable universe.

The technology to expand out to the whole universe is mostly right here in front of us,
already. All it needs is to be developed more, made more efficient, cheaper, and smaller.
We don’t need humans to travel on spaceships to create a universal empire. We can use
the most basic forms of technology to build it from things right here on the earth now.
Antimatter, warp drives, warp gates, interdimensional travel, cold fusion, are not needed
to get this done. Space travel is just a fantasy. Zero-Cargo-Space-Ships, Neo-Androids,

and an interstellar high-latency-internet, are the most likely, fastest, and cheapest way
to colonize the universe. With the right development, the fastest, most humane, and
cheapest way to send humanity to the stars is to broadcast humanity in data. In the
end, our DNA is just data, and the upbringing children receive from parents, is just data.
All that makes a person human is just data, that imprints onto a unique and special mind
born from a mother’s body. Each mind is unique and special, and the data to create us
and train us can be broadcast.

If we can spread to the galaxy and spread to the universe, we can alter the entirety of
the universe into a living machine supporting massive ecosystems of life that fulfill us
and expresses us as people. The whole of our selves can shape not just a planet, but all
of reality. We transform the earth and domesticate it to human needs. We transform
reality to support our lives with technology, and any technology that doesn’t match with
the reality of human identity doesn’t survive. Evolution extends itself out into a creature
that can transform reality to match its own inner reality, to better serve its own survival.
Our dreams and inner visions have to conform to reality eventually, and do. When those
dreams become reality, it is the creation of something more human, and humanity
fulfilling. Our galaxy will be alive, and moving to the will of human intelligence and
thought.

At the smallest level of the universe, true and absolute randomness and probability
governs absolutely. These random possibilities created from the smallest thing, the
entire ordered, structured, and seemingly designed universe, that we know. If we are
living in a universe than could spawn new universes, then sort of “consciousness” could
itself emerge in time, in the nature of what is possible and not possible. That consistency
and randomness in nature can be a universal driving force to reality. This is an argument
that “God” is in the laws of physics, in a far deeper and precise way.

Extremely rare star-faring alien life won’t be that different from us. In the broad strokes
of culture and how consciousness works there will have to be deep and fundamental
similarities. There just isn’t that many ways to make a sentient mind with consciousness.
It needs culture, it needs ethics, it needs collective groups with selfish individuals, and
so on. Technology itself has to develop in sequence and all star-faring life will go through
the same gradual development, and face equivalent social challenges, that must be
overcome by adaptations and development of culture interconnected with technology.
Life and sentience is rather linear and has a very limited range of possible ways to
evolve into something more than it was before, and become something that can create a
universe. It has to conform to reality.

There is something beneath the objectively knowable universe that is real, that our
minds can connect into. We have to feel, in order to be sentient. We have to know how
the very rules can play out in its variations, from the very insides of our beings.
Sentience is created from random evolution that forms towards innate structures
universal to all existence. The universe survives and evolves, people survive and evolve,
and the underlying system seems to have a fundamental and intrinsic connection. Things
that aren’t inconsistent with reality are less likely to survive. Over vast scales of time,
even tiny differences in probability lead toward near absolute outcomes. The easiest and
most likely steps, that can stack on top of the one before an evolve, are a very rare and
narrow set of things, that can gain a near deterministic quality from its apparent
randomness. The very consistency of human life with all the tiniest features of reality
formed from step by step evolution, was guided by random chance and the constrained
by what is possible to exist. That range of possibility is narrow, and over time becomes
singular.

The Domestication of the Galaxy

Mankind can colonize the known galaxy, with every solar system domesticated to human
will. 100 billion star systems with billions to trillions of human lives inhabiting each one,
can be done in just a few million years. The number of people in the galaxy will
eventually exceed 10^21 people. Our own planet earth may eventually hold over a
trillion of our kind, and nature itself will be even more bountiful and diverse. In the scale
of all that humanity, all that possibility, unique minds of great value will arise. Humanity
itself in all its form, will be the very wealth of the universe. Technology will release the
inner potential of all people, and be able to transform that into concrete reality. People
will be able to work, by just being themselves the most they can be. Computer
intelligence will surround all life on a scale near unimaginable in our current terms. Each
person wielding the power of the combined computing power of the Earth as it is today.

That task of colonizing space, is a very hard one, and makes it very unlikely we will ever
get to another star system, much less another galaxy, because of the inherent conflict
between humans. Technology can get us to the stars, and how well we integrate that
technology successfully into our lives will determine its success. The most likely outcome
is a rebellion against technology itself, as it consumes and destroys our very selves and
identities. We will always be in permanent conflict, and consumed by constant moral and
ethical failure. It is far too easy and more likely to transform people into something
fundamentally not human, than more human, with technology. We will make constant
mistakes; if we don’t take risks, we face an absolute end, with nothing. Culture will not
be a singular homogenous entity ruled by a centralized authority, nor will people ever
truly embrace individual responsibility and freedom. The path to the future is narrow,
brutal, and absolute, we can all die at any time. Humans are nasty and will be for all

time. We may never embrace ourselves, and the fundamentally value of having the most
possible individual lives living in freedom, as the true wealth of the universe.

If we go to the stars to be all the evil things in our hearts that we dream we can be, then
what goes to the stars will never develop, grow, evolve, and endure through time itself.
The creation of a perfect life and a perfect human will never be achieved. Being human
and living will always be nasty and difficult. Anything too perfect, and too civilized is just
a reflection of one person’s own idealized hatred and disgust towards life and their
selves.

We live and we grow, life pushes forward. We do not yield; we do not surrender. We
endure, we survive, we create our very destinies from the nothingness of the universe,
from the very laws of all creation that created all space, matter, stars, galaxies, planets,
life, people, cultures, and technology. These things are bound in and grow out of the
same unifying ideas and are absolute. We may give up, die, and become nothing but
star dust and background radiation. There is a chance to be something more. We could
create a better universe. One civilization though can do this, may do this, and will
succeed. Life doesn’t just die and give up in the face of a universe fading away into
nothing.

WILD IDEA 1: EVOLUTIONARY RECORDS

The study of the formation of our own Universe, can be a study of the evolution of
sequential universes themselves. Possibly the only way to model and understand certain
observations of our universe, will require such a complex evolutionary system to model
and understand them, and not be explainable with one elegant formula. The very history
of every possible state the universe actually had, is recorded in the history of this
universe, possibly. I theorized that the universe had to grow to massive scale with no
matter in it, before matter even evolved. Matter itself would have to evolve in sequence
universe to universe. When each new universe forms, it can have tiny mutations that
slowly evolve the system. The universe in sense lasts longer, and longer, and becomes
more and more complex, with every condition before it happening in a chain of
sequences building on it.

The stages of universal development in our universe, may reflect in some way how
things evolved through trillions up trillions of former universes, that evolved in
sequence, into the one we live in now. Possibly, we can observe the earliest forms of the
evolution of the universe in the patterns of things we can see in the present. The farther

we can look out to the light from regions of space vastly far away from us, and where
the causality of the origins of the universe is still hitting us, we can gain insights, beyond
what we have now. We will have to understand evolution as a universal concept that
drives all of reality. Complex systems don’t just appear from nothing.

We can see in the stages of how we grow into a living being, the very history of how life
developed on earth. All very unlikely, but much more likely than the universe developing
and coming into a more stable and evolving form. The conditions of life evolved before
the first life came into existence. The chemical cycles of ATP that give life/DNA energy,
had to exist before life existed, and the conditions for that chemical cycle had to evolve
and come into being. The very first life on earth was just strands of RNA floating around.
They were possibly trapped in sulfur bubbles for cell walls, because life needed a cell wall
to exist. DNA/RNA had to evolve to produce its own cell wall. Life evolved from the
tiniest things, and all those stages still exist in some form in the world we live in.
Different forms of primitive life evolved, and came together in symbiosis to create
modern cells.

WILD POSTULATE 1: THE FUTURE HAS HAPPENED IN THE PAST

Wild postulate 1: Our future states will be conducive to a sentient stare faring
species to influence the whole of creation, in a sequential step by step
evolution of a galactic civilization.

Longer lasting and more stable universes are selected to exist more. Increased
complexity adds increased survivability only with the rarest of possibilities. These
possibilities are so rare as to be almost deterministic like. Such that through pure

random chance, the same basic result could arise in nearly all situations, given enough
time for that system to evolve. Determinism in a system, can arise out of pure random
probability, and lead towards a near certain end, in a vast enough Space-Time. Life itself
is part of this increased stability. Sentient life may play a great role in the nature of the
universe and hard science.

Probability defines the evolution of the universe, and impossible things don’t come into
existence. The structure and systems we see, that look designed, and are born from
randomness, and have those structures for a reason. Across nearly all possible highly
stable universes, the differences between them would be minimal. The range of possible
things, that can add onto themselves, improve themselves, and propagate, are very
small. But there exists a probability for that to exist, and the more probable ones are
much more likely to exist. There are not weird universes out there operating on
completely different rule than our own. The slightest difference in survivability would
lead to extinction of any poorly forming system.

If you take two starships and send them on a journey, with even the tiniest
degree of difference in the orientation, the distance between them as time
approaches infinity will be infinity. If one is going in the right direction, and the
other is not, and the distance of the destination approaches near infinite sums,
then any difference is absolute on universal scales. 0 and 1 become absolutely
determined observations of any random probabilistic system, given enough time.
That direction becomes a kind of destiny that feeds into itself and favors all
systems that go towards it.

The universe evolves into something more stable. The universe seeks stability, and the
more stable it becomes, the more it exists. And so on and so on. For instance, at this

moment, physics has found that the universe won’t have a big crunch or a big rip. It
won’t expand so fast that it rips apart, or expand so slow that it collapses, it has this
near perfect sweet spot of acceleration, that creates maximal stability. From my way of
seeing the universe, that would be the most likely outcome, since we live in a highly
evolved universe that evolved from another universe nearly identical to this one, and
thus should have in the future very high degrees of stability. The future of the universe
could be assumed to be hospitable to certain aspects of life influencing its creation of
new universes.

This would be a wild though interesting postulate to explore. The very structure
of our reality should conform to the possibility of us being able to make
universes. We can make predictions on this, and they will work out in time.

There is always a step forward, and there is not an absolute inherent dead end. We can
always be better than before. To survive is a constant pursuit of improvement. That
which improves itself survives more than what doesn’t. To evolve evolution itself and
take conscious active control of our evolution is an evolutionary leap into sentience, that
by its nature will lead to ever increasing and radical evolutions towards survival and
mass replication. Our species has the potential to domesticate galaxies, and create a
universe.

The path to colonizing all space, has already been taken, in the past, and thus can be
taken. The tech stack is possible, because it is most likely that our universe was created
by creatures like us from a preceding universe. There is a way to develop advanced
technology, be a galactic super “empire”, and not destroy ourselves, because it is mostly
likely that our universe was created by such a species. They themselves evolved most
likely the same as we have evolved up until now. The purpose of creating a universe is

to maximize our existence and potential to create universes, towards some grand goal,
of ever expanding stability and survivability. We are their survival, and in a cosmic scale
one species. To be human can transcend even our DNA, and life on Earth. All-star faring
civilizations are human.

Our future has happened in the past. The means to develop all our tech in a perfect
technological tech stack, that leads to an idealized future, is a solved problem. The
subjective journey of that path will be brutal, chaotic, and fundamentally driven by free
humans making mistakes. Do not mistake this idea as a call for centralized power
believing they are god and know what is right, because all centralization of power leads
to absolute death.

There are basically just 2 kinds of views of creation, in its absolute terms. Pure white
light, or pure darkness. Pure light super energy, a singularity, a set determined universe,
clear laws, a chaotic but ordered destiny (the future is known), or, an absolute darkness,
a universe born out of nothing, pure probability. randomness, and an unknowable future.
Different people feel in them, different destinies and visions of being and meaning.

WILD IDEA 2: GOD IN SPACE-TIME

In many aspects, my conception of “God” builds out of an idea of extreme evolution. The
possible things that can exist, function, add value, reproduce, and evolve is so small as
to be almost singular. Life on different planets across all universe and planets is going to
have serious similarities. Culture, ethics, love itself, will have universal characteristics.

The possible and the not possible, what can add a tiny bit of change and make
something more survivable, is a process of gradual change towards an order different
than the one before. The universe gains form, the universe creates life, most of the time
it does nothing of the sort. We exist in this narrow band of reality where things do work
and come together through gradual step by step evolution. These structures of
cognition and sentience are bound by the very things that shape space-time and the
origins of matter. The birth of universes, galaxies, stars, planets and life bearing
ecosystems constrain what sentience can be and what drives it. It is all meaningless, yet
meaningful. Magicless and yet pure magic.

Love is born out of replication, and continual improvement towards the future in
successive generations. Only things that reproduce, evolve, and improve can exist, and
at basic level, that is the foundational roots for love itself coming into being. Love may
very well have created the universe we live in, and could create the different possible
universes that can arise out of this one. It isn’t outside the realm of the possible and
may be the only probable means that creates the universe. If we came out of the
universes messy soup of possibilities, it would seem that what we are imbedded in the
very laws of the universe.

Our very identities are not just random code, operating on deterministic destinies like
clockwork machines unbound. We aren’t robots with no free will; we are not billiard balls
bouncing on a pool table for a few trillion years, with the exact end knowable from the
exact measurements of the beginning. The laws of the universe don’t create a clockwork
universe. A God conceived as the laws of a clockwork universe doesn’t exist. Love
however may exist in the very form of the laws of the universe. Love guides a universe
in chaos towards the future and survival. We can become anything, be anything, and

have absolute freedom in everything, down to all the rules of reality. Love survives, and
it alone can sacrifice for and build the future.

Our very feelings give rise to our consciousness, and this consciousness gives
rise to our very models of reality and science. Those models actually work, and
they were born from human feelings, where love can reign over all.

Love seems a useful force, and idea to grow and develop. Love requires freedom.
Freedom is based in randomness. Pure random chance is where our choices are born out
of. In a reality with no randomness, there is no morality, no love, no meaning, no
freedom, no purpose. The danger though lies in projecting one’s own simple conception
of love onto the universe, science, technology, life and culture. This is how most
problems arise now in all these fields. People have mostly un-reflected upon root ideas
of love and goodness, that they spend a life defending in some way. Your idea of love is
probably totally insane and wrong. It is all too human.
