Summary

A single person, can be a point of fundamental leadership and inspiration towards the
future. God can be represented as the orientation in time, we must go as, in the flesh of
a human being. Newton, Aristotle, Christ, Steve Jobs can be seen gods and demi-gods
that directed man’s development. Living sentient beings could have created state of the
end universe that built the following universe. The pursuit of science near the end of the
universe is to conceive an initial configuration of the universe that will generate a better
universe, in the following one. And possibly influence its development after the “big
bang”. Or to find a way to simply replicate and expand humanity more readily into a
following universe as a means of metaphysical reproduction. The idea we are living in a
simulation is not what it would appear to be to the theorist speculating about it. It would
be a search for God, and thus the simulation itself, to the those that made it, would have
more moral value than even their own reality. The people in it, would be the very
modeling of God, to broadcast into another universe.

Broadcasting from the old universe into the next one, while respecting the speed of light,
is possible, if you receive a signal from far enough away, and that signal was broadcast
for a very long time in the preceding universe. This paradigm may extend to even the
creation of a new universe. From planet to planet, we develop a greater morality, from
galaxy to galaxy another level of character, and in seeding life into another universe we
rise to something totally different. We can replicate through data transmission between
planets, and possibly eventually between galaxies, and then universes. If we look far
enough away from us, and with the right tools, we will be able to see the beginning of
the universe, the information from a very distant point in space and time. If there was
something existing before the big bang, as seems very likely to be true, we may be able
to observe something of the universe before our own, if it was transmitted to us.

We in theory will be able to observe information that travelled to us from another
universe. If it was sent by a nearly god like species, then that information could very
well influence and configure a receiver. If they knew how life could evolve, they could
make it a signal that living things could receive. This is my best attempt to explain
people getting messages from “god” that could be true, and how life from the very
beginning could be influenced. Revelation, sentience, and our feelings of the divine,
could have a divine form, mixed in with the 99.9999% self-delusion. This is not “aliens
are in my head telling me what to do!”. Humans have magical thinking, and it seems
fundamental to being human. This is also how one has to solve the information paradox
of a black hole, and what can transmit out from one. Space.

Wild Idea 3: Memories of The Past and Future

Creatures precognition may be more than analysis of the present and past. It may be
possible to send signals back from the future, and not create a paradox. In that we can
only know if we received a message from the future after that future event has passed.
The sort of “information” that can be known in the past from information from the
future, may be only recognized if it has already been experienced before. The future that
happened in a past universes civilization nearly identical to our own can be seen as the
future of our universe, such that we will recognize and dream of forms from that past
universe as the ideal possible future of our own.

Memory in some forms, works like a computer hash. A hash takes a large file of data,
and creates a short unique code for that file, if one letter is changed, the hash radically
changes. We don’t remember the past. We remember compressed encodings of the
past, that when presented with those memories, we can recognize them to be correct or
not. We don’t remember the past. We can recognize what was the past and is not the

past, by these compressed encodings. When we see in front of us the past, that we have
an encoding for, we can recognize it and sequence it temporal hashes.

Déjà vu is experiencing something that falsely triggers this feeling of a past memory.
You recognize something that can’t be memory as something you remember. The
underlying memory that is falsely corresponding, doesn’t even have to be similar.

•

A hash of a picture is remembered.

•

Every unique image will have a unique hash.

•

If presented with that unique image you have a hash for, you will remember that
image as a correct memory.

•

You can have false memories and false identifications of having seen something
before, that you have not, based on hashes not being 100% unique.

The information broadcast through time is these hashes, and can’t be known unless they
match an actual experienced event. Maybe we can know if have received a message or
not. The very existence of messages implies a future to exist in, and thus a reason to
have hope. Knowing you can survive is of great use to survival. Human destiny, our
sense of purpose, and the frame work, that we construct our identity around, are bound
in a sense of time, that projects into and from the future. Or at least at some level,
people experience life with an illusion like this to guide them. Information could be
broadcast from the past from a very distant and long dead civilization. While we also
could make that same technology and broadcast to our past. No information could be
broadcast back, like “buy this stock”. Life is probability and knowing the outcome of a
probable thing, destroys its existence.

Emotions arise out of the way human memory is formed and experienced, as an
embodiment of time. Evolution and Survival is the subjective emotional experience of
time as flesh and blood. Our emotions arise from a will to live and reproduce and to
experience our existence and reproduction as meaningful. Reproduction must always be
a set of emotions favored over individual survival, while not favoring group survival. If
this sense of survival can be tuned to the right frequency, then it can amplify the
potential for a star-faring civilization to exist and prosper. An animal could naturally
evolve such a receiver, if ones that did survived and prospered more. The message itself
could influence the configuration of even crystals, or certain rare events, where life
comes into being initially. At a simple level, it seems possible, that something like
gravitational-waves could influence the configuration of quantum systems towards
certain configurations, and thus transmit self-replicating information, which could then
evolve into sentient life. Love is an interesting emotion, that drives us to be better.

The Dark Night Of The Soul

Within us as humans, we can look into this place in us, with absolute darkness,
absolute nothingness, and find meaning. People have two senses of the divine,
absolute nothingness and absolute light and everything. They are equivalent.

The amount of light you see depends on how much “god” you put into the absolute
nothing of the universe from which all things came into existence out of, and how far
into the future your sense of reality is dependent on. Teleological thinking orients
towards light, and deductive thinking towards darkness. This dualistic interplay of
divinity as absolute nothingness and absolute being, are very real cognitive experiences
in many “spiritual” human beings, between the two essences of human nature.

I experienced absolute darkness and fell through absolute nothingness for eternity. I
found the tiniest and most distant star in that darkness to orient, after I died. I can’t
universalize my experience to all people. If the universe was like a ying-yang symbol, I
would be fixated on the white dot in the blackness. I found in the nothingness a guiding
direction. A point of light in nothingness, to orient creation towards. I found myself, a
direction to guide me, from a voice both inside and outside me, at once. Eastern
dualism, as compared to western dualism, lies more at the direct human experience of
reality. We can also conceive creation in it. It is not good and evil. Different souls will
see different things, and both be true.

There is a structure of to our consciousness that correlates to the very
structure of the universe at its very origins. We couldn’t even be sentient,
unless we evolved a mind that connected to this. Possible things are things
connected to the very laws of creation at the beginning of the universe, by the
laws of probability and what is even possible to exist. Random evolution can
create sentience, by creating random combinations, until one combination hit
on the one that correlated to what can actually work and not work. This can be
a gradual process, until you hit sentience, an actual awareness of that initial
state of the universe. We as humans are collectively sentient, and not
individually fully aware. It takes a large grouping of humans to contain all that
“knowledge” contained within nothingness, in beautiful tapestry of different
cognitive structures.

Our minds seem connected to more than just random survival. We have a sense of time,
a sense of destiny. We have built real things from this feeling. We built civilizations and
grand achievements in technology. These things are real, and we made them from the

feelings inside of us. Children have looked out at the world, and felt the laws of nature;
through a life of thinking and study, they at rare and special times create the most world
changing ideas. Newton and Einstein’s true formative thoughts, that shaped all of their
successes, were born out of their younger childhood minds.

The ability to truly hold onto your identity and childhood dreams, creates a will
capable of changing the world.
